### [1] [Code-QA-Bench: Separating Code Reasoning from Documentation Memorization in Repository-Level QA](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29277v1)
*Jun Zhang,JianYing Qu,Hanwen Du,Zhongkai Sun,Yehua Yang,Qiao Zhao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了Code-QA-Bench框架，通过答案优先生成和三条件实验设计，合成仓库级代码理解基准，实验证明代码访问是主导因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法区分真正的代码理解与文档回忆和预训练记忆，需要更严格的评估方法。

Method: 答案优先生成管道（智能体先探索代码得到黄金答案再提问）和三条件实验设计（闭卷、仅代码、有文档），使用LLM评判器评分。

Result: 生成528个代码可推导和100个文档依赖任务；实验显示代码访问增益+0.23，文档在文档依赖任务上增益+0.071，代码可推导任务上仅代码与有文档性能相当。

Conclusion: 框架有效分离了代码理解与文档记忆，开源且易于推广到其他Python仓库。

中文摘要：我们提出了Code-QA-Bench，一个完全自动化的框架，用于合成仓库级别的代码理解基准测试，该框架能够将真正的代码理解与文档回忆和预训练记忆区分开来。该框架做出了两项方法论贡献：(1) 一个答案优先生成管道，其中配备工具的人工智能体探索源代码以生成经过验证的黄金答案，然后再推导出问题，确保每个任务都基于真实的代码结构；(2) 一个三条件实验设计，在闭卷（无仓库）、仅代码（移除文档）和有文档（完整仓库）条件下评估智能体，其差值直接量化了文档的效用和记忆程度。我们从SWE-Bench中的10个Python仓库生成了528个代码可推导任务和100个文档依赖任务，由LLM评判器根据准确性、完整性和特异性进行评分。在四个前沿模型上的实验表明，代码访问是主导因素（比闭卷平均增益+0.23），文档在文档依赖任务上提供了适度的额外好处（+0.071），并且在代码可推导任务上，仅代码≈有文档，验证了该设计的有效性。该框架是开源的，可应用于任何有良好文档的Python仓库。

Original abstract: We present Code-QA-Bench, a fully automated framework for synthesizing repository-level code understanding benchmarks that separates genuine code comprehension from documentation recall and pretraining memorization. The framework makes two methodological contributions: (1) an answer-first generation pipeline where a tool-equipped agent explores source code to produce verified gold answers before deriving questions, ensuring every task is grounded in real code structure; and (2) a three-condition experimental design evaluating agents under closed-book (no repository), code-only (documentation removed), and documented (full repository) conditions, with deltas directly quantifying documentation utility and memorization.
  We generate 528 code-derivable and 100 doc-dependent tasks across 10 Python repositories from SWE-Bench, scored by an LLM judge on accuracy, completeness, and specificity. Experiments on four frontier models reveal that code access is the dominant factor (+0.23 mean gain over closed-book), documentation provides modest additional benefit (+0.071 on doc-dependent tasks), and code-only $\approx$ documented on code-derivable tasks, validating the design. The framework is open-source and applicable to any well-documented Python repository.

</details>


### [2] [On the Road to Personalized Code Intelligence: Portraiting and Assisting Developers Based on Their In-IDE Behaviors](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29372v1)
*Yuhong Liu,Yunhe Su,Zhipeng Peng,Zhiwen Luo,Lin Shi,Zhi Jin,Li Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出VirtualME，一种嵌入IDE的数据基础设施，通过持续捕获开发者行为并建模四维画像，实现个性化代码智能，在问答任务中平均提升33.80%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码智能研究忽略开发者个体差异，通用模型无法满足个性化需求。

Method: VirtualME包含日志级行为提取、任务级行为识别和开发者个性测量三组件，基于多智能体管道和规则引擎构建开发者画像，并集成到Q&A智能体中。

Result: 在多仓库基准上，VirtualME增强的答案在五个维度平均提升33.80%。

Conclusion: 丰富的连续开发者行为数据可用于自适应和个性化代码智能。

中文摘要：随着大语言模型的出现，自动化软件工程的研究越来越侧重于利用这些模型来实现对代码更深层次的语义理解，或设计复杂的基于智能体的流程。然而，这一研究轨迹在很大程度上忽视了一个关键因素：开发者本身。编程是一项高度个体化的活动；开发者在工具链偏好、领域专业知识和问题解决策略上表现出显著差异。因此，当前“一刀切”的代码智能系统范式难以满足个体开发者的需求。为了解决这一差距，我们引入了VirtualME，一种新颖的嵌入IDE的数据基础设施，旨在通过持续捕获和解释开发者的动态编程行为与偏好来建模开发者。VirtualME包含三个组件：(1) 日志级行为提取：从IDE中捕获并提取开发者的日志级行为。(2) 任务级行为识别：通过多智能体管道将日志级行为聚合为任务级行为。(3) 开发者个性测量：构建规则引擎以提炼出四维开发者画像：技术栈、能力、行为习惯和学习风格。在VirtualME之上，我们提出了一种个性化仓库级知识问答的解决方案，通过将开发者画像集成到问答智能体中。我们通过构建一个包含真实开发者轨迹的多仓库基准来评估VirtualME，平衡了正确性与个性化。实验结果表明，VirtualME增强的答案在五个维度上优于通用基线，平均提升33.80%。我们的结果证明，丰富、连续的开发者行为数据可以为自适应和个性化的代码智能铺平新道路。

Original abstract: With the advent of large language models, research in automated software engineering has increasingly focused on leveraging these models to achieve a deeper semantic understanding of code or to engineer sophisticated agent-based processes. However, this research trajectory has largely overlooked a critical factor: the developers themselves. Programming is a deeply individualized activity; developers exhibit significant variation in their tool-chain preferences, domain-specific expertise, and problem-solving strategies. Consequently, the current paradigm of one-size-fits-all code intelligence systems struggles to accommodate the needs of individual developers. To address this gap, we introduce VirtualME, a novel IDE-embedded data infrastructure designed to model the developer by continuously capturing and interpreting their dynamic programming behaviors and preferences. VirtualME contains three components. (1) Log-level Behavior Extraction: it captures and extracts developers' log-level behaviors from IDE. (2) Task-level Behavior Recognition: it aggregates log-level behaviors into task-level behaviors via a multi-agent pipeline. (3) Developer-personality Measurement: it builds a rule engine to distill a four-dimensional developer persona: technology stack, ability, behavioral habits, and learning style. On top of VirtualME, we propose a solution for personalized repository-level knowledge Q&A by integrating the developer persona into the Q&A agent. We evaluated VirtualME by building a multi-repository benchmark with real-world developer trajectories, balancing correctness and personalization. Experimental results show that VirtualME-enhanced answers outperform generic baselines on five dimensions, yielding an average 33.80% improvement. Our results demonstrate that abundant, continuous developer-behavior data can pave the new way for adaptive and personalized code intelligence.

</details>


### [3] [Offloading Score: Measuring AI Reliance Through Counterfactual Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29392v1)
*Vishakh Padmakumar,Lujain Ibrahim,Zora Zhiruo Wang,Jennifer Wang,Q. Vera Liao,Diyi Yang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出卸载得分作为衡量用户对AI工具认知依赖的新指标，通过模拟无工具工作流计算节省步骤比例，实验表明该指标能有效检测时间压力下的依赖变化，而传统指标无法区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有依赖度量仅关注AI输出采用或自我报告，忽略了任务努力在用户和工具之间的分布。

Method: 定义卸载得分，通过构建反事实工作流（用户无工具时如何完成任务）计算使用工具节省的步骤比例；通过内在评估和用户研究（n=40）验证，并改变时间压力进行测试。

Result: 卸载得分在时间压力下检测到依赖性显著增加（+43%，p=0.018），而基于使用量和自我报告的基线度量无法区分条件；更高依赖表现为更多委托和直接重用AI输出。

Conclusion: 卸载得分可用于用户自我反思和代理设计者减轻过度依赖；提供两个贡献：用户工具和定量信号。

中文摘要：AI工具越来越多地集成到现实工作流程中。然而，现有的对这些工具依赖的衡量侧重于AI输出的采用或自我报告指标，而不是任务努力在用户和工具之间的分布。在这里，我们引入了卸载得分（offloading score），这是一种依赖度量，量化了卸载到AI工具的认知努力比例。卸载得分基于模拟——我们通过估计用户在没有工具的情况下如何完成任务来构建一个反事实工作流，然后计算使用工具节省的步骤比例。我们通过内在评估度量有效性的验证，以及一项有40名开发者使用AI工具执行编程任务的受控用户研究来验证卸载得分。我们改变时间压力来测试依赖度量是否捕捉到时间压力下依赖性的已知增加。我们表明，卸载得分在时间受限条件下检测到显著更高的依赖性（+43%，p=0.018），而基于使用量和自我报告的基线依赖度量无法区分条件。我们辅以描述性洞察，表明更高的依赖性表现为将子任务更多地委托给工具以及更直接地重用AI输出。最后，我们展示了一种将卸载得分与任务目标结果（例如代码理解）结合使用的方法，以识别依赖何时可能（不）合适。我们的框架提供了两个贡献：用户可用来测量和反思自身依赖的工具，以及代理设计者可以用来减轻过度依赖的定量信号。

Original abstract: AI tools are increasingly integrated into real-world workflows. However, existing measures of reliance on these tools focus on AI output adoption or on self-reported indicators, rather than how task effort is distributed between users and tools. Here, we introduce offloading score, a measure of reliance that quantifies the fraction of cognitive effort offloaded to an AI tool. Offloading Score is simulation-based -- we construct a counterfactual workflow by estimating how the user would have completed the task without the tool, and then computing the fraction of steps saved by using the tool. We validate offloading score through intrinsic evaluations of metric validity, and a controlled user study ($n=40$) with developers performing programming tasks using AI tools. We vary time pressure to test whether reliance measures capture the known increase in reliance under time pressure. We show that offloading score detects significantly higher reliance in time-constrained settings ($+43\%$, $p=0.018$), while usage-based and self-reported baseline measures of reliance do not distinguish the conditions. We complement this with descriptive insights showing that higher reliance manifests as greater delegation of subtasks to the tool and more direct reuse of AI outputs. Finally, we demonstrate an approach of using offloading score in combination with target outcomes of a task (e.g., code understanding) to identify when reliance may be (in)appropriate. Our framework offers two contributions: an instrument users can apply to measure and reflect on their own reliance, and a quantitative signal that agent designers can utilize to mitigate overreliance.

</details>


### [4] [How Coding Agents Fail Their Users: A Large-Scale Analysis of Developer-Agent Misalignment in 20,574 Real-World Sessions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29442v1)
*Ningzhi Tang,Chaoran Chen,Gelei Xu,Yiyu Shi,Yu Huang,Collin McMillan,Tao Dong,Toby Jia-Jun Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过对超过2万个编码代理会话的观察研究，发现代理与开发者之间的错位主要表现为七种形式，多数造成努力和信任成本而非系统损害，且大部分需用户显式纠正；模式因环境而异且随时间变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试无法反映开发者在实际工作中遇到的AI编码代理错位问题，因此需要基于真实工作流程的观察性研究来系统分析错位现象。

Method: 对来自1,639个仓库的20,574个编码代理会话进行观察性研究，将错位操作化为开发者反馈可见的故障，并沿形式、原因、代价和解决方式四个维度标注每个事件。

Result: 识别出七种错位形式；90.50%的事件造成努力和信任成本，91.49%需用户显式纠正；错位模式在IDE和CLI间有差异，随时间变化但整体下降，约束违规和自报告错误占比增加。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了编码代理在实际工作流中的错位特征，为设计更对齐的训练、评估和交互界面提供了依据。

中文摘要：AI编码代理越来越直接地在软件环境中行动，然而现有对其失败的分析依赖于基准测试轨迹，未能捕捉开发者实际体验到的错位。我们进行了一项观察性研究，涵盖来自1,639个仓库的20,574个编码代理会话，涉及IDE和CLI工作流程。我们将错位操作化为通过开发者反馈而变得可见的故障，并沿四个维度对每个事件进行标注：形式、原因、代价和解决方式。我们识别出七种反复出现的形式，涵盖代理如何阅读项目、理解开发者意图、遵循规则、约束其行动、实现和执行代码以及报告进度。90.50%的事件带来了努力和信任成本而非不可逆的系统损害，然而91.49%的可见解决方式仍需要用户明确纠正。错位模式在IDE和CLI设置中也存在差异，在相邻会话中持续存在，并随时间变化：虽然总体发生率下降，但约束违规和不准确的自我报告所占份额增加。我们的发现为设计训练、评估和界面提供了信息，以保持编码代理与真实开发者工作流程的一致性。

Original abstract: AI coding agents increasingly act directly within software environments, yet existing analyses of their failures rely on benchmark trajectories that miss how developers actually experience misalignment. We present an observational study of 20,574 coding-agent sessions from 1,639 repositories across IDE and CLI workflows. We operationalize misalignment as a breakdown made visible through developer pushback, and annotate each episode along four axes: form, cause, cost, and resolution. We identify seven recurring forms, spanning how agents read projects, interpret developer intent, follow rules, bound their actions, implement and execute code, and report progress. 90.50\% of episodes impose effort and trust costs rather than irreversible system damage, yet 91.49\% of visible resolutions still require explicit user correction. Misalignment patterns also differ across IDE and CLI settings, persist across adjacent sessions, and shift over time: while overall rates decline, constraint violations and inaccurate self-reporting grow in share. Our findings inform the design of training, evaluation, and interfaces for keeping coding agents aligned with real developer workflows.

</details>


### [5] [Usability Analysis of Configurator User Interfaces with Multimodal Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29456v2)
*Sebastian Lubos,Alexander Felfernig,Damian Garber,Adnan Kraljić,Tarik Kraljić,Viet-Man Le,Thi Ngoc Trang Tran,Gerhard Leitner,Julian Schwazer,Doris Suppan,Reinhard Willfort,Ivan Dukic,Jeremias Fuchs,Manuel Henrich*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文使用多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）半自动分析配置器UI的可用性，综合18个特定标准，在16个真实配置器上评估，发现MLLMs能可靠识别问题并提供建议，尽管仍需人工验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 配置器UI的可用性分析缺乏特定标准和自动化工具支持，通用启发式不够针对，手工分析成本高。

Method: 从文献中综合18个配置器特定可用性标准，利用MLLMs对16个真实配置器UI进行半自动化分析，每个标准单独评估生成严重性评级和改进建议。

Result: MLLMs能可靠识别配置器特定可用性问题并提供领域感知的改进建议，但人工验证仍必要。

Conclusion: MLLMs有潜力显著减少配置器可用性分析所需工作量，但需结合人工验证以确保准确性。

中文摘要：配置是定制复杂软件系统、服务和产品的关键技术。配置器的成功应用不仅取决于技术正确性、性能和领域建模，还取决于其可用性。虽然通用可用性启发式被广泛使用，但针对配置器的特定标准和用于系统用户界面（UI）分析的工具支持有限。本文探讨了使用多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）进行可扩展且半自动化的配置器UI可用性分析。我们从文献中综合了18个配置器特定的可用性标准，并将这些标准应用于基于MLLM的16个真实世界配置器分析中。每个标准被单独评估，以生成可用性问题的严重性评级和可操作的改进建议。结果审查确认，MLLMs能够可靠地识别配置器特定的可用性问题，并提供领域感知的改进建议。尽管仍然需要人工验证，但该方法有潜力显著减少分析配置器可用性所需的工作量。

Original abstract: Configuration is a key technology for tailoring complex software systems, services, and products. A successful application of configurators not only depends on technical correctness, performance, and domain modeling but also on their usability. While general usability heuristics are widely used, configurator-specific criteria and tool support for systematic user interface (UI) analysis are limited. This paper explores the use of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) for scalable and semi-automated usability analysis of configurator UIs. We synthesize 18 configurator-specific usability criteria from the literature and apply these criteria in an MLLM-based analysis of 16 real-world configurators. Each criterion is assessed individually to generate severity ratings for usability issues and actionable improvement suggestions. A review of the results confirms that MLLMs can reliably identify configurator-specific usability issues and provide domain-aware improvement recommendations. Although human validation remains necessary, this approach has the potential to significantly reduce the required effort to analyze configurator usability.

</details>


### [6] [CODEFUSE-DEBENCH: An Empirical Study on Readability, Recompilability, and Functionality](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29490v1)
*Puzhuo Liu,Yuhan Huang,Jianlei Chi,Peng Di,Yu Jiang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出可重用性驱动的反编译评估范式，通过DEBENCH框架多维评估发现可重用性悬崖、可读性与功能性冲突、反编译器引擎主导进展以及三类失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反编译评估方法（如语法相似性或单轴可读性）无法反映实际可重用性，缺乏能够衡量反编译结果在真实场景中是否有用的综合指标。

Method: 提出DEBENCH框架，包含240个原子测试函数（8个源文件，640个二进制文件），结合LLM-as-judge可读性评分与URAF（18子维度）、50次迭代编译修复、Frida差分动态追踪（程序/函数/指令三级），评估5种反编译器和3种修复LLM。

Result: 最佳反编译器-LLM对仅达22.3%行为重叠和1.2%精确输出匹配；-O3优化可读性最低但功能最高；反编译器间功能差异（20倍）远大于LLM间（1.6倍）；修复错误中19%为类型系统崩溃。

Conclusion: 可重用性悬崖显著，反编译器引擎比修复模型更关键，且存在语法噪声、类型系统崩溃和不可逆上游损失三类根本性失败模式。

中文摘要：二进制反编译旨在将二进制文件恢复为高级源代码，但现有评估主要依赖语法相似性或单一轴可读性指标，未能捕捉实际可重用性。我们提出了一种可重用性驱动的评估范式，沿三个正交维度衡量反编译器质量：可读性、可重编译性和功能性。我们提出了DEBENCH，这是第一个用于多维反编译评估的自动化框架。DEBENCH包含240个原子测试函数，组织成8个源文件，编译成640个二进制文件。它结合了基于LLM作为裁判的可读性评分与URAF（18个子维度）、在固定50次迭代预算下的迭代编译与修复，以及基于Frida的程序级、函数级和指令级差分动态追踪。我们评估了五种主流反编译器和三种修复LLM。我们的研究揭示了四个发现。首先，可重用性悬崖很陡峭：最佳反编译器-LLM对达到了22.3%的精确+部分程序级行为重叠，但只有1.2%的精确标准输出匹配，比重编译性低近50个百分点。其次，最大化可读性的设置并未最大化功能性：-O3产生最低的可读性但最高的功能性，而Clang比GCC可读性低但功能性高2.6倍。第三，跨反编译器在功能级的变化是20倍，远大于跨LLM的1.6倍变化，表明进展更多地依赖于反编译器引擎而非更大的修复模型。第四，失败分为三类：语法噪声、类型系统崩溃（约占修复错误的19%）以及不可逆的上游损失，如ARM64重定位惯用模式和C++ ABI特性。

Original abstract: Binary decompilation aims to recover binaries into high-level source code, but existing evaluations mainly rely on syntactic similarity or single-axis readability metrics, which fail to capture practical reusability. We propose a reusability-driven evaluation paradigm that measures decompiler quality along three orthogonal dimensions: readability, recompilability, and functionality. We present DEBENCH, the first automated framework for multidimensional decompilation evaluation. DEBENCH contains 240 atomic test functions, organized into 8 source files and compiled into 640 binaries. It combines LLM-as-judge readability scoring with URAF (18 sub-dimensions), iterative compile-and-repair under a fixed 50-iteration budget, and Frida-based differential dynamic tracing at the program, function, and instruction levels. We evaluate five mainstream decompilers and three repair LLMs. Our study reveals four findings. First, the reusability cliff is steep: the best decompiler-LLM pair reaches 22.3% Exact+Partial program-level behavioral overlap but only 1.2% exact stdout match, nearly 50 points below recompilability. Second, settings that maximize readability do not maximize functionality: -O3 yields the lowest readability but the highest functionality, and Clang gives lower readability than GCC but 2.6x higher functionality. Third, cross-decompiler variation at the functional level is 20x, far larger than the 1.6x cross-LLM variation, showing that progress depends more on decompiler engines than larger repair models. Fourth, failures fall into three categories: syntactic noise, type-system collapse (about 19% of repair errors), and irreversible upstream losses such as ARM64 relocation idioms and C++ ABI features.

</details>


### [7] [GUITestScape: Towards Open-set Evaluation on Exploratory GUI Testing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29532v1)
*Xiaoyi Chen,Yifei Gao,Yang Xu,Xingxing Song,Yi Zhang,Jitao Sang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了GUITestScape基准和GUIJudge评估器，用于探索性GUI测试中MLLM代理的流程感知评估，发现检测是主要瓶颈，集成验证器可提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有探索性GUI测试基准仅关注交互缺陷且评估协议过于简化，无法区分不同失败模式，需要更全面的基准和过程感知评估方法。

Method: 构建GUITestScape基准（61个Android应用、508个交互和显示缺陷），并设计GUIJudge开放式评估器，将测试轨迹分解为可独立诊断的能力模块进行评价。

Result: GUIJudge在过程感知评估上显著优于所有基线；在GUITestScape上测试表明检测是主要瓶颈，集成GUIJudge验证器可提升检测性能。

Conclusion: GUITestScape和GUIJudge为探索性GUI测试提供了更全面的评估框架，揭示了现有模型的检测瓶颈，并展示了无需重训即可提升性能的方法。

中文摘要：探索性GUI测试对MLLM代理来说是一个特别苛刻的场景：没有预定义的测试脚本，代理必须自主导航应用程序并通过其自身的交互发现缺陷。然而，当前的评估在两个方面存在不足。首先，现有的基准几乎只关注交互缺陷，将显示缺陷排除在评估框架之外。其次，评估协议受限于预定义的缺陷注释，将测试过程简化为单一的最终状态判断，混淆了性质上不同的失败模式。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了GUITestScape，一个交互式基准，涵盖61个真实世界的Android应用程序和508个预设缺陷，涵盖交互和显示类型，并引入了GUIJudge，一个开放式评估器，将代理的测试轨迹分解为可独立诊断的能力。实验结果表明，GUIJudge在超越预定义注释的基础上实现了可靠的流程感知评估，显著优于所有基线。在GUITestScape上的基准测试进一步揭示，检测仍然是现有模型在两种缺陷类型上的关键瓶颈，并且将GUIJudge的验证器集成到现有代理中可以显著提高其检测性能而无需重新训练。

Original abstract: Exploratory GUI testing is a particularly demanding setting for MLLM agents: without predefined test scripts, an agent must autonomously navigate an application and discover defects through its own interaction. However, current evaluation falls short on two fronts. First, existing benchmarks focus almost exclusively on interaction defects, leaving display defects outside the evaluation frame. Second, evaluation protocols are bound to predefined defect annotations, collapsing the testing process into a single end-state judgment that conflates qualitatively distinct failure modes. To address these challenges, we present GUITestScape, an interactive benchmark covering 61 real-world Android applications and 508 preset defects spanning interaction and display types, and introduce GUIJudge, an open-set evaluator that decomposes an agent's testing trajectory into independently diagnosable capabilities. Experimental results demonstrate that GUIJudge achieves reliable process-aware evaluation beyond predefined annotations, substantially outperforming all baselines. Benchmarking on GUITestScape further reveals that detection remains the critical bottleneck for existing models across both defect types, and that integrating GUIJudge's verifiers into existing agents significantly boosts their detection performance without retraining.

### [8] [Inferring Code Correctness from Specification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29822v1)
*Tambon Florian,Papadakis Mike*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出TRAILS方法，通过基于规范的测试输入生成和执行以及LLM对输入-输出对的评估来验证LLM生成代码的正确性，在多个数据集和模型上显著提高了准确性和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代码验证方法要么成本高昂且难以扩展（动态共识），要么易受动态错误和顺序偏差影响（静态推理），需要一种可扩展且鲁棒的替代方案。

Method: TRAILS基于规范进行类别划分生成多样化测试输入，执行候选代码得到输入-输出对，然后提示LLM评估这些对是否符合规范（不直接推理代码），最后聚合所有输入上的分数以判断程序正确性。

Result: 在LiveCodeBench和CoCoClaNeL数据集上，使用Qwen3Coder-30B等三个LLM，TRAILS将马修斯相关系数相比零样本CoT提升高达39%，始终优于HoarePrompt，且在不同运行中更稳定，为更多独特代码样本分配正确标签。

Conclusion: TRAILS是一种有效且稳定的LLM生成代码验证方法，通过基于输入-输出对的推理避免了代码推理的缺陷，提升了准确性和可靠性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）已成为现代软件开发不可或缺的一部分，实现了大规模的自动化代码生成。然而，验证LLM生成代码的正确性仍然是一个关键且很大程度上未解决的挑战。现有方法要么依赖于多个代码候选之间的动态共识——这使其成本高昂且难以扩展，要么依赖于静态推理，而静态推理容易受到动态错误和顺序偏差的影响。在本文中，我们提出了TRAILS（通过输入和规范的目标推理一致性），一种将LLM推理与具体（输入，输出）对相结合的方法。TRAILS首先基于规范通过类别划分生成多样化的测试输入，然后针对候选代码执行这些输入，并提示LLM评估生成的输入-输出对是否符合规范——而无需对代码本身进行推理。分数在输入之间聚合，以确定程序是否可能正确。我们在两个数据集LiveCodeBench和CoCoClaNeL上，使用三个LLM（Qwen3Coder-30B、Devstral-Small-24B和Olmo3.1-Instruct）评估TRAILS，并与HoarePrompt和零样本链式思维基线进行比较。TRAILS相对于零样本CoT将马修斯相关系数提高了高达39%，并且始终优于HoarePrompt。除了准确性之外，TRAILS在多次运行中表现出更高的稳定性，降低了对LLM非确定性的敏感性，并且与竞争方法相比，为更大的一组独特代码样本分配了正确的标签。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have become integral to modern software development, enabling automated code generation at scale. However, validating the correctness of LLM-generated code remains a critical and largely unsolved challenge. Existing approaches either rely on dynamic consensus across multiple code candidates - making them costly and difficult to scale - or on static reasoning that is susceptible to dynamic bugs and order bias. In this paper, we propose TRAILS~ (Targeted Reasoning Agreement via Inputs and Specifications), an approach that grounds LLM reasoning with concrete (input, output) pairs. TRAILS~ first generates diverse test inputs via category partitioning based on the specification, then executes them against the candidate code and prompts LLMs to assess whether the resulting input-output pairs conform to the specification - without ever reasoning over the code itself. Scores are aggregated across inputs, to determines whether the program is likely correct. We evaluate TRAILS~ on two datasets, LiveCodeBench and CoCoClaNeL, across three LLMs (Qwen3Coder-30B, Devstral-Small-24B, and Olmo3.1-Instruct), comparing against HoarePrompt and a Zero-Shot Chain-of-Thought baseline. TRAILS~ improves Matthew Correlation Coefficient by up to 39\% relative to Zero-Shot COT and consistently outperforms HoarePrompt. Beyond accuracy, TRAILS~ demonstrates greater stability across seeded runs, reducing sensitivity to LLM non-determinism, and assigns correct labels to a larger set of unique code samples than competing approaches.

</details>


### [9] [TagDebt: A Bot to Support Technical Debt Management](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29869v1)
*João Paulo Biazotto,Daniel Feitosa,Paris Avgeriou,Elisa Yumi Nakagawa*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出并评估了TagDebt机器人，用于自动识别GitHub问题中的自我承认技术债务，通过设计科学研究和TAM评估，发现其有用且易用，但受团队和代码库规模等因素影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏专门且易于集成到现有工作流的技术债务管理工具。

Method: 采用设计科学研究方法设计并实现TagDebt机器人，通过技术接受模型（TAM）访谈16名从业者进行可用性和接受度评估。

Result: 从业者认为TagDebt有用（尤其组织问题和减少手动工作）且易用，但采用决策受团队和代码库规模等上下文因素影响，并提出了增加源代码检查和更新功能等改进建议。

Conclusion: TagDebt是开发更专门TDM工具的概念验证，能在不干扰现有工作流的情况下使技术债务可见，帮助从业者避免未管理技术债务的风险。

中文摘要：上下文：技术债务（TD）是一个被广泛研究的隐喻，有助于解释次优决策如何随着时间的推移损害软件可维护性。尽管产生TD本身并不坏，但跟踪和管理TD对于避免其负面影响至关重要。因此，研究人员和从业者提出并开发了多种管理TD的方法和工具。然而，我们仍然缺乏专门用于技术债务管理（TDM）的工具，特别是那些可以轻松集成到现有开发工作流中的工具。目标：我们提出并评估TagDebt，一个可以集成到GitHub仓库中并自动为问题分配标签（即SATD或非SATD）的机器人。TagDebt有助于识别TD（即通过寻找自我承认的技术债务（SATD）），从而实现更高效的TDM。方法：我们进行了一项设计科学研究来设计和实现TagDebt。为了评估它，我们通过采访16名从业者执行了一项技术接受模型（TAM）研究，以检查机器人的有用性、易用性以及可能影响机器人使用的上下文因素（如团队规模和从业者角色）。结果：总体而言，从业者认为TagDebt很有用，特别是在组织问题和减少手动工作方面。此外，他们指出机器人整体上易于使用，其文档清晰。分析还揭示，上下文因素，如团队和代码库规模，影响采用TagDebt的决定。最后，提出了几项改进建议，例如包括检查和更新源代码的功能。结论：TagDebt是开发和使用更专门的TDM工具的概念验证。它有助于在不干扰现有工作流的情况下使TD可见，并帮助从业者避免未管理TD的风险。

Original abstract: Context: Technical debt (TD) is a widely studied metaphor that helps to explain how sub-optimal decisions that can harm software maintainability over time. Although incurring TD is not intrinsically bad, tracking and managing TD are crucial to avoid its negative effects. Hence, researchers and practitioners have proposed and developed diverse approaches and tools for managing TD. However, we are still lacking specialized tools for technical debt management (TDM), specifically ones that can be easily integrated into existing development workflows. Objective: We present and evaluate TagDebt, a bot that can be integrated within GitHub repositories and automatically assign labels to issues (i.e., SATD or non-SATD). TagDebt helps in the identification of TD (i.e., by looking for self-admitted technical debt (SATD)), leading to more efficient TDM. Methods: We carried out a Design Science Research study to design and implement TagDebt. For its evaluation, we executed a Technology Acceptance Model (TAM) study through interviews with 16 practitioners, to check the bot's usefulness, ease of use, and contextual factors that might impact the bot's usage (such as team size and practitioners' roles). Results: Overall, practitioners found that TagDebt is useful, especially for organizing issues and reducing manual work. Furthermore, they pointed out that the bot is overall easy to use, and its documentation is clear. The analysis also revealed that contextual factors, such as team and codebase size, impact the decision to adopt TagDebt. Finally, several improvements were suggested, such as including features to check and update the source code. Conclusion: TagDebt is a proof-of-concept for the development and usage of more specialized tools for TDM. It helps to make TD visible without disrupting existing workflows and help practitioners avoid the risks of unmanaged TD.

### [10] [Agora: Toward Autonomous Bug Detection in Production-Level Consensus Protocols with LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29910v1)
*Xiang Liu,Sa Song,Zhaowei Zhang,Huiying Lan,Jason Zeng,Ming Wu,Michael Heinrich,Yong Sun,Ceyao Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Agora多智能体框架，结合LLM与假设驱动测试，发现多个共识协议中的深层逻辑错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM方法难以检测涉及跨阶段状态依赖的深层协议级逻辑错误，这些错误可能导致严重损失。

Method: 领域感知的多智能体框架，通过专门智能体协作探索协议状态空间、使用领域特定约束合成攻击场景，并通过迭代细化验证发现，实现全局协议不变量推理。

Result: 在四个共识实现（Raft、EPaxos、HotStuff、BullShark）中发现15个新协议级逻辑错误，而现有LLM代理未检测到任何此类错误。

Conclusion: 领域感知的多智能体协作对于检测复杂协议中的深层逻辑错误至关重要。

中文摘要：共识协议构成了分布式系统和区块链的骨干，其中的实现错误可能导致数据损坏和财务损失。虽然基于LLM的方法在代码分析方面显示出潜力，但它们难以处理涉及多个执行阶段的复杂状态依赖行为的深层协议级逻辑错误。我们提出了Agora，一个领域感知的多智能体框架，将假设驱动测试与LLM能力相结合，用于系统性协议验证。Agora采用专门智能体，它们协作探索协议状态空间，使用领域特定约束合成攻击场景，并通过迭代细化验证发现。这种显式的角色分离使得能够推理超越单函数代码分析的全局协议不变量。我们在四个共识实现（Raft、EPaxos、HotStuff、BullShark）上使用四个最先进的LLM评估Agora。Agora发现了15个先前未知的违反安全属性的协议级逻辑错误，而现有的基于LLM的智能体未能检测到任何此类协议级逻辑错误。我们的结果表明，领域感知的多智能体协作对于检测复杂协议中的深层逻辑错误至关重要。

Original abstract: Consensus protocols form the backbone of distributed systems and blockchains, where implementation bugs can cause data corruption and financial losses. While LLM-based approaches show promise in code analysis, they struggle with deep protocol-level logic bugs involving complex state-dependent behaviors across multiple execution stages. We present Agora, a domain-aware multi-agent framework that integrates hypothesis-driven testing with LLM capabilities for systematic protocol verification. Agora employs specialized agents that collaboratively explore protocol state spaces, synthesize attack scenarios using domain-specific constraints, and validate findings through iterative refinement. This explicit role separation enables reasoning about global protocol invariants beyond single-function code analysis. We evaluate Agora on four consensus implementations (Raft, EPaxos, HotStuff, BullShark) using four state-of-the-art LLMs. Agora discovers 15 previously unknown protocol-level logic bugs that violate safety properties, while existing LLM-based agents fail to detect any such protocol-level logic bugs. Our results demonstrate that domain-aware multi-agent collaboration is essential for detecting deep logic bugs in complex protocols.

### [11] [CodeGolf Bench: A Multi-Language Benchmark for Evaluating Concise Code Generation Capabilities of Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30394v1)
*Vedant Padwal*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了CodeGolf Bench基准，用于评估LLM在60种语言中的简洁代码生成能力，发现推理模型显著优于非推理模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准受限于固定问题集和语言覆盖，缺乏对LLM生成简洁代码能力的动态评估，需要一种基于代码高尔夫的实时人类基线基准。

Method: 基于code.golf平台构建基准，包含60种编程语言的代码高尔夫问题，并提供实时人类表现基线；对9个LLM在Python和C++任务上评估推理与非推理模型。

Result: 推理模型最佳平均百分位达70.97%，非推理模型远低于此；差距在C++中更明显。

Conclusion: CodeGolf Bench提供了动态评估LLM代码生成能力的框架，强调推理模型在语法严格语言中的优势，并为未来研究提供方向。

中文摘要：本文介绍了CodeBench，一个能够评估大型语言模型在60种编程语言中生成简洁代码能力的基准测试。基于代码高尔夫（一种追求最短字符或字节解决方案的娱乐编程竞赛），该基准测试为衡量LLM生成高效、简洁代码的能力提供了独特的度量标准。与受限于固定问题集和语言覆盖范围的现有基准不同，CodeGolf Bench利用code.golf平台提供新问题以及实时的人类表现基线。对9个LLM在Python和C++任务上的评估表明，推理模型显著优于非推理模型，最佳平均百分位达到70.97%。这一性能差距在C++中尤为显著，凸显了推理对于语法要求严格的语言的重要性。非推理模型在两种语言上的效率优化方面表现更差，其最佳百分位远低于推理模型。CodeGolf Bench提供了一个动态框架，用于根据代码高尔夫中不断进化的人类表现来评估LLM的代码生成能力。

Original abstract: This paper introduces Code Bench, a benchmark capable of evaluating Large Language Models (LLMs) concise code generation abilities in 60 programming languages. Based on code golf, a recreational programming competition focused on minimal character or byte solutions, the benchmark provides a distinctive measure of LLMs ability to produce efficient, concise code. Unlike existing benchmarks limited by fixed problem sets and language coverage, CodeGolf Bench leverages the code.golf platform to provide new problems and live human performance baselines. Evaluation of nine LLMs on Python and C++ tasks demonstrates that reasoning models significantly outperform non-reasoning models, achieving best average percentile of 70.97%. This performance gap is particularly pronounced in C++, highlighting reasoning's importance for languages with strict syntax requirements. Non-reasoning models struggle more with efficiency optimization across both languages, with best percentiles significantly lower than reasoning counterparts. CodeGolf Bench offers a dynamic framework for evaluating LLM code generation capabilities against evolving human performance on code golf.

</details>


### [12] [REPOT: Recoverable Program-of-Thought via Checkpoint Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30052v1)
*Parsa Mazaheri*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: RePoT通过验证回放和单次LLM修复，有效解决PoT因无效动作导致的轨迹失效问题，在多个模型和基准上显著提升性能，并揭示检查点信息是核心恢复信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一次性思维程序（PoT）在规划中可能因单个无效动作而整个失败，需要一种低成本恢复机制。

Method: RePoT先验证回放计划直到第一个无效转换，然后通过一次LLM调用从已验证前缀恢复，并引入自适应版本根据前缀长度选择修复策略。

Result: 在PuzzleZoo-775上PoT失败的问题中，RePoT最多额外一次LLM调用即可恢复，性能提升3-11个百分点；在PlanBench和开源模型上也有显著提升；并证明检查点信息是关键信号。

Conclusion: RePoT是一种高效且成本可控的PoT恢复方法，检查点信息比具体前缀内容更重要，自适应版本有望进一步优化能力缩放。

中文摘要：一次性思维程序（PoT）会生成一个打印原始动作计划的Python程序；单个无效动作即可静默地使整个轨迹失效。我们提出RePoT（可恢复的PoT）：一种确定性验证回放方法，将计划在环境中逐步执行直到遇到第一个无效转换，然后通过一次LLM调用从已验证的前缀继续执行。在PoT失败的约14%的问题上，RePoT最多只需额外一次LLM调用。在PuzzleZoo-775数据集上，RePoT在四种闭源模型配置上比PoT高出3到11个百分点，在gpt-5.4-mini-medium上最高达到96.9%对86.3%；在匹配预算的PoT重试基线下，RePoT在Gemini上显著获胜（+3.8个百分点，95%置信区间[+2.2,+5.4]），在GPT-medium和Claude上在采样噪声范围内，在GPT-mini上则落后——我们开始用自适应RePoT来解决这种能力缩放模式，自适应RePoT是一种基于规则的分发器，根据已验证前缀长度在后缀修复和全新PoT重试之间进行路由（初步结果）。我们在PlanBench Blocksworld上复现了结果（+1.1到+11.4个百分点），并在四个开源模型上（其中三个提升+3.3到+20.0个百分点）也取得了类似结果。在Derail-550基准（我们的受控恢复基准）上，每个能够访问检查点信息的条件在GPT-medium上达到至少30%，在Gemini上达到至少70%，而仅靠错误反馈则不超过3.1%——这表明检查点信息（而非特定的已验证前缀尾部）才是关键的恢复信号。

Original abstract: One-shot Program-of-Thought (PoT) emits a Python program that prints a primitive-action plan; a single invalid action silently invalidates the trajectory. We introduce RePoT (Recoverable PoT): a deterministic verified replay that walks the plan through the environment to its first invalid transition, then one LLM call that resumes from the verified prefix. RePoT costs at most one extra LLM call on the ~14% of problems where PoT fails. RePoT beats PoT by +3 to +11pp across four closed-model configurations on PuzzleZoo-775 and peaks at 96.9% vs 86.3% on gpt-5.4-mini-medium; against the matched-budget PoT-retry baseline, RePoT wins decisively on Gemini (+3.8pp, 95% CI [+2.2,+5.4]), is within sampling noise on GPT-medium and Claude, and loses on GPT-mini -- a capability-scaling pattern we begin to address with Adaptive RePoT, a rule-based dispatcher that routes between suffix repair and a fresh PoT retry based on verified-prefix length (preliminary). We replicate on PlanBench Blocksworld (+1.1 to +11.4pp) and on four open-weights models (+3.3 to +20.0pp on three of four). On Derail-550, our controlled recovery benchmark, every condition with access to checkpoint information clears >=30% on GPT-medium and >=70% on Gemini, vs <=3.1% for error-only feedback -- showing that checkpoint information, not the specific verified-prefix tail, is the load-bearing recovery signal.

</details>


### [13] [Projectional Decoding: Towards Semantic-Aware LLM Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30054v1)
*Boqi Chen,José Antonio Hernández López,Aren A. Babikian*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出投影解码框架，通过部分图模型在生成过程中集成领域语义，实现增量语义验证和可证明的语义有效性保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有约束解码技术缺乏通用表示来桥接LLM文本与语义验证推理，难以确保语义有效性。

Method: 提出projectional decoding，在生成过程中维护部分图模型作为主要制品表示，显式捕获不确定性，支持增量语义验证和错误检测。

Result: 在程序生成任务上的初步结果显示该方法能提高LLM生成制品的语义有效性。

Conclusion: 投影解码能够实现LLM在软件工程中的可验证自动化。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用于在许多软件工程（SE）任务中生成软件制品，然而确保这些制品的语义有效性仍然是一个基本挑战。现有的约束解码技术可以强制执行句法正确性，在某些情况下还可以强制执行特定的语义规则，但缺乏一种通用表示来桥接LLM生成的文本与SE中语义验证所需的推理。在本文中，我们提出了投影解码（projectional decoding），一种新颖的概念框架，它将领域语义直接集成到生成过程中，通过在生成过程中维护一个部分图模型作为主要制品表示，同时保留文本。这种抽象表示通过显式捕获不确定性并原生支持错误检测来实现增量语义验证，同时以可证明的保证引导生成朝向语义有效的输出。我们呈现了在程序生成任务上的初步结果，展示了这种方法提高LLM生成制品语义有效性的潜力。我们还讨论了投影解码如何能够在各种SE活动中实现与LLM的可验证自动化。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to generate software artifacts across many software engineering (SE) tasks, yet ensuring the semantic validity of these artifacts remains a fundamental challenge. Existing constrained decoding techniques can enforce syntactic correctness and, in some cases, specific semantic rules, but lack a general representation that bridges LLM-generated text with the reasoning required for semantic validation in SE. In this paper, we propose projectional decoding, a novel conceptual framework that integrates domain semantics directly into the generation process by maintaining, alongside text, a partial graph model as the primary artifact representation throughout generation. This abstract representation enables incremental semantic validation by explicitly capturing uncertainty and natively supporting error detection, while guiding generation toward semantically valid outputs with provable guarantees. We present preliminary results on a program generation task which demonstrate the potential of this approach to improve the semantic validity of LLM-generated artifacts. We also discuss how projectional decoding can enable verifiable automation with LLMs across various SE activities.

</details>


### [14] [EvoRepair: Enhancing Vulnerability Repair Agents Through Experience-Based Self-Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30105v1)
*Haichuan Hu,Guoqing Xie,Quanjun Zhang,Jiawei Liu,Shengcheng Yu,Chunrong Fang,Zhenyu Chen,Liang Xiao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出EvoRepair，一种基于经验的自我进化智能体框架，用于自动漏洞修复，通过循环学习与修复过程积累和复用经验，显著提升修复性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在自动漏洞修复中缺乏漏洞内经验积累和跨漏洞经验复用，导致重复错误和知识浪费。

Method: 提出EvoRepair框架，包含循环学习与修复过程：检索相关经验指导修复，从修复轨迹提取新经验，并用质量感知评分更新经验库。

Result: 在PATCHEVAL和SEC-bench上分别达到93.47%和87.00%，整体90.46%，优于LoopRepair、IntentFix和Live-SWE-Agent等基线。

Conclusion: 基于经验的自我进化显著增强了智能体自动漏洞修复，且优于现有自我进化技术。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLM）在自动漏洞修复（AVR）方面展现出了潜力，但它们仍然面临若干局限性，包括缺乏漏洞内经验积累和缺乏跨漏洞经验复用。因此，LLM在迭代修复过程中可能反复犯类似的错误，并且未能充分利用来自历史漏洞的宝贵修复知识。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了EvoRepair，这是首个基于经验的自我进化AVR智能体框架，它使LLM能够在长时间跨度的漏洞修复中积累、提炼和利用领域特定知识。EvoRepair遵循一个循环的学习与修复过程，该过程检索相关过往经验以指导修复，从修复轨迹中提取新经验，并使用质量感知评分更新经验库。我们在PATCHEVAL和SEC-bench上使用GPT-5-mini对EvoRepair与12个代表性漏洞修复基线进行了评估。结果表明，EvoRepair达到了最佳整体性能，在PATCHEVAL上达到93.47%，在SEC-bench上达到87.00%，整体达到90.46%。特别地，EvoRepair在PATCHEVAL和SEC-bench上分别比最新的基于LLM的基线LoopRepair高出39.56%和33.50%，并超过IntentFix 70.86%和50.50%。在两个基准测试中，EvoRepair整体上还超过了最近的自我进化智能体Live-SWE-Agent 6.98%。在VUL4J上的额外迁移实验进一步证明了EvoRepair跨模型、编程语言和数据集的鲁棒性。这些发现表明，基于经验的自我进化显著增强了智能体AVR，并超越了现有的自我进化技术。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown promise for automated vulnerability repair (AVR), but they still face several limitations, including the lack of intra-vulnerability experience accumulation and the lack of cross-vulnerability experience reuse. As a result, LLMs may repeatedly make similar mistakes during iterative repair and underutilize valuable repair knowledge from historical vulnerabilities. To address these challenges, we propose EvoRepair, the first experience-based self-evolving AVR agent framework that enables LLMs to accumulate, refine, and leverage domain-specific knowledge across long-horizon vulnerability repairs. EvoRepair follows a cyclic learn-and-repair process that retrieves relevant past experiences to guide repair, extracts new experiences from repair trajectories, and updates an experience bank using quality-aware scoring. We evaluate EvoRepair against 12 representative vulnerability repair baselines on PATCHEVAL and SEC-bench using GPT-5-mini. Results show that EvoRepair achieves the best overall performance, reaching 93.47% on PATCHEVAL, 87.00% on SEC-bench, and 90.46% overall. In particular, EvoRepair outperforms latest LLM-based baseline LoopRepair by 39.56% and 33.50% on PATCHEVAL and SEC-bench, respectively, and surpasses IntentFix by 70.86% and 50.50%. Across both benchmarks, EvoRepair also exceeds the recent self-evolving agent Live-SWE-Agent by 6.98% overall. Additional transfer experiments on VUL4J further demonstrate the robustness of EvoRepair across models, programming languages, and datasets. These findings demonstrate that experience-based self-evolution substantially strengthens agentic AVR and goes beyond existing self-evolving techniques.

### [15] [Automating Low-Risk Code Review at Meta: RADAR, Risk Calibration, and Review Efficiency](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30208v2)
*Chris Adams,Arjun Singh Banga,Parveen Bansal,Souvik Bhattacharya,Payal Bhuptani,Rujin Cao,Pedro Canahuati,Nate Cook,Brian Ellis,Prabhakar Goyal,Gurinder Grewal,Tianyu He,Matt Labunka,Alex Manners,David Molnar,Ging Cee Ng,Vishal Parekh,Jiefu Pei,Frederic Sagnes,James Saindon,Will Shackleton,Sid Sidhu,Gursharan Singh,Karthik Chengayan Sridhar,Matt Steiner,Pratibha Udmalpet,Sean Xia,Stacey Yan,Audris Mockus,Peter Rigby,Nachiappan Nagappan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出RADAR系统，通过风险感知的分层自动化评审，有效缓解AI驱动代码增长带来的评审瓶颈，并显著降低回滚率和事故率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI辅助编码工具大幅增加了代码供应，但评审者带宽未能同步增长，导致代码评审瓶颈和延迟，急需自动化评审方案来平衡效率与安全。

Method: 提出RADAR系统，采用多阶段漏斗流程：根据作者和来源分类差异，依次通过准入条件、静态启发式、机器学习差异风险分数、LLM自动评审和确定性验证，最终落地低风险变更。

Result: RADAR已评审超过53.5万个差异，落地超过33.1万个；放松风险阈值后批准率达60.31%；回滚率为非RADAR的1/3，生产事故率为1/50；中位关闭时间减少超过330%，中位评审等待时间减少35%。

Conclusion: 风险感知的分层自动化能够在不牺牲生产安全的前提下，显著减少AI驱动代码增长造成的评审瓶颈，有效应对代码供应与评审带宽之间的失衡。

中文摘要：AI辅助编码工具改变了软件生产。在Meta，每个由人工落地的差异中的显著代码行数同比增长105.9%，每位开发者的差异提交量增长51%，其中代理型AI贡献了超过80%的增长。与此同时，及时评审的差异比例有所下降，暴露出代码供应与评审者带宽之间不断扩大的差距。我们提出了三个问题，从可行性到校准再到影响：(1)风险分层的自动化能否在多样化组织中大规模运行，(2)调整风险阈值如何影响自动化产出与安全性之间的权衡，(3)自动评审在多大程度上减少了AI生成变更的端到端延迟？我们部署了RADAR（风险感知差异自动评审），一个多阶段漏斗，根据作者身份和来源类型对每个差异进行分类，应用准入条件、静态启发式、机器学习差异风险分数、基于LLM的自动代码评审以及确定性验证，然后落地符合条件的变更。我们通过覆盖超过53.5万个RADAR评审差异的遥测数据、政策变更的观测前后对比以及效率结果的差异分析来评估RADAR。RADAR已评审超过53.5万个差异并落地超过33.1万个。将差异风险分数阈值从第25百分位放松到第50百分位，批准率提高到60.31%。RADAR评审差异的回滚率是非RADAR差异的1/3，生产事故率是非RADAR差异的1/50。RADAR将中位关闭时间减少超过330%，中位差异评审等待时间减少35%。风险感知的分层自动化可以在不牺牲生产安全的情况下，大幅减少由AI驱动代码增长造成的评审瓶颈。

Original abstract: AI-assisted coding tools have altered software production. At Meta, significant lines of code per human-landed diff grew by 105.9% year over year and per-developer diff volume rose 51%, with agentic AI responsible for over 80% of that growth. Meanwhile, the share of diffs receiving timely review has declined, exposing a widening gap between code supply and reviewer bandwidth. We ask three questions that progress from feasibility through calibration to impact: (1) can risk-stratified automation operate at scale across diverse organizations, (2) how does tuning the risk threshold affect the trade-off between automation yield and safety, and (3) to what extent does automated review reduce end-to-end latency for AI-generated changes? We deployed RADAR (Risk Aware Diff Auto Review), a multi-stage funnel that classifies each diff by authorship and source type, applies eligibility gates, static heuristics, a machine-learned Diff Risk Score, LLM-based Automated Code Review, and deterministic validation before landing qualifying changes. We evaluate RADAR through telemetry covering 535K+ RADAR-reviewed diffs, observational before-after comparisons for policy changes, and difference-in-differences analysis of efficiency outcomes. RADAR has reviewed 535K+ diffs and landed 331K+. Relaxing the Diff Risk Score threshold from the 25th to the 50th percentile increased the approve rate to 60.31%. The revert rate for RADAR-reviewed diffs is 1/3 that of non-RADAR diffs, and the Production Incident rate is 1/50 that of non-RADAR diffs. RADAR reduces median time to close by over 330% and median diff review wall time by 35%. Risk-aware layered automation can materially reduce review bottlenecks created by AI-driven code growth without compromising production safety.

### [16] [Improving Small Language Models for Code Generation with Reinforcement Learning from Verification Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30478v1)
*Egor Skopin,Evgeny Kotelnikov*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: RLVR通过可验证奖励训练语言模型生成代码，实验表明组合奖励提升pass@1达13%，但单一静态分析奖励会鼓励短代码而忽略正确性，组合奖励则更稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索RLVR在代码生成中的有效性，并揭示奖励设计对模型行为的影响，以识别失败模式。

Method: 在MBPP基准上使用Qwen3-0.6B和Llama3.2-1B模型进行LoRA微调，比较GRPO和GSPO在单元测试奖励、Ruff linter静态分析奖励及组合奖励下的表现，并评估pass@1及行为诊断指标。

Result: 组合奖励使pass@1提升13个百分点；单一静态分析奖励导致生成变短且正确性未改善；组合奖励更稳定。

Conclusion: RLVR效果对奖励设计和优化粒度高度敏感，需结合pass@1之外的行为诊断指标以识别失败模式。

中文摘要：使用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）通过程序可检查的信号（如单元测试结果）训练语言模型，从而能够直接优化代码生成的功能正确性。我们在MBPP基准上对Python代码生成进行了一项实证研究，使用两个小模型（Qwen3-0.6B和Llama3.2-1B）进行LoRA微调。在多种奖励公式（例如：仅单元测试奖励、通过Ruff linter的静态分析塑形奖励以及组合奖励）下，我们比较了基于分组的策略优化变体（GRPO和GSPO），并评估了功能正确性和行为诊断。在我们的实验设置中，RLVR在提出的组合奖励配置下，将MBPP测试上的pass@1提高了多达13个百分点。然而，我们发现奖励塑形可能引发系统性行为偏移：仅使用静态分析惩罚可能会使策略偏向于生成更短的代码，从而减少lint错误，但并不能可靠地提高功能正确性。相比之下，组合奖励减轻了这种退化，并在正确性和风格约束之间产生了更稳定的权衡。总体而言，我们的结果强调，RLVR在代码生成中的有效性对奖励设计和优化粒度高度敏感，并且除了pass@1之外，诊断指标（包括生成长度、Ruff严重性分布和执行错误类型）对于识别失败模式是有用的。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) trains language models using programmatically checkable signals such as unit-test outcomes, enabling direct optimization for functional correctness in code generation. We conduct an empirical study of RLVR for Python code generation on the MBPP benchmark using two small models (Qwen3-0.6B and Llama3.2-1B) with LoRA fine-tuning. Across multiple reward formulations such as: unit-test-only rewards, static-analysis-only shaping via the Ruff linter, and a combined reward, we compare group-based policy optimization variants (GRPO and GSPO) and evaluate both functional correctness and behavioral diagnostics. In our experimental setting, RLVR improves pass@1 on MBPP test by up to 13 percentage points under proposed combined reward configuration. However, we find that reward shaping can induce systematic behavioral shifts: using only static-analysis penalties may bias the policy toward shorter completions that reduce lint errors without reliably improving functional correctness. In contrast, combined rewards mitigate this degeneration and yield more stable trade-offs between correctness and style constraints. Overall, our results highlight that RLVR effectiveness for code generation is highly sensitive to reward design and optimization granularity, and that diagnostics beyond pass@1, including generation length, Ruff severity profiles, and execution error types are useful for identifying failure modes.

</details>


### [17] [Neurodiversity in Agile Teams: Obstacles and Inclusion Barriers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30555v1)
*Lars Struck,Christian Veenaas,Robert Wiedekind,Joshua Riechmann,Maria Rauschenberger,Philipp Diebold,Simone Dogu,Michael Neumann*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过混合方法探索了敏捷软件开发中神经多样性包容的现状，发现团队实践碎片化，组织障碍如僵化结构和缺乏意识限制了包容，提出需灵活条件和定制支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经多样性在工作场所的重要性日益被认可，但敏捷团队中如何有效包容神经多样性开发者尚不清楚，存在研究空白。

Method: 混合方法：网络内容分析（Reddit和LinkedIn）结合11次半结构化专家访谈（来自德国某企业神经多样性网络）。

Result: 团队合作实践高度碎片化，依赖个体适应；敏捷实践可促进参与，但僵化结构、刻板印象和一刀切方法破坏包容；组织意识和调整不足。

Conclusion: 敏捷实践有助于包容，但受限于僵化结构和低意识；需灵活条件和定制支持以发挥神经多样性优势。

中文摘要：背景：神经多样性日益被视为工作场所多样性的一个宝贵维度。然而，在敏捷软件开发团队中，团队合作实践与神经多样性员工包容之间的相互作用仍未得到充分探索。目标：本研究旨在探讨敏捷软件开发中的团队合作质量如何在神经多样性背景下当前被实践和讨论，并识别阻碍有效包容神经多样性开发者的组织障碍。方法：我们采用混合方法，结合了涵盖Reddit和LinkedIn的网络内容分析，以及来自德国某组织企业神经多样性网络的11次半结构化专家访谈。结果：分析显示，团队合作实践高度碎片化，由个体适应而非共享标准所塑造。虽然敏捷实践和支持工具可以促进神经多样性的参与，但僵化的结构、刻板印象和一刀切的方法往往会破坏包容性。组织意识和定制调整仍然不足。结论：敏捷实践可以促进包容性团队合作，但其益处受到僵化的组织结构和有限的神经多样性意识的制约。利用神经多样性的优势需要灵活的组织条件和定制的支持。

Original abstract: Context: Neurodiversity is increasingly recognized as a valuable dimension of workplace diversity. However, in agile software development teams, the interplay between teamwork practices and the inclusion of neurodivergent employees remains underexplored. Objective: The study aims to explore how teamwork quality in agile software development is currently practiced and discussed in the context of neurodiversity, and to identify organizational barriers that hinder the effective inclusion of neurodivergent developers. Method: We applied a mixed-method approach combining a web content analysis covering Reddit and LinkedIn with 11 semi-structured expert interviews from a corporate neurodiversity network in a German organization. Results: The analysis shows that teamwork practices are highly fragmented and shaped by individual adaptation rather than a shared standard. While agile practices and supportive tools can enable neurodivergent participation, rigid structures, stereotypes, and one-size-fits-all approaches often undermine inclusion. Organizational awareness and tailored adjustments remain insufficient. Conclusion: Agile practices can promote inclusive teamwork, yet their benefits are constrained by rigid organizational structures and limited awareness of neurodiversity. Harnessing neurodiverse strengths demands flexible organizational conditions and tailored support.

</details>


### [18] [AI-PROPELLER: Warehouse-Scale Interprocedural Code Layout Optimization with AlphaEvolve](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00131v1)
*Chaitanya Mamatha Ananda,Rajiv Gupta,Mircea Trofin,Aiden Grossman,Sriraman Tallam,Xinliang David Li,Amir Yazdanbakhsh*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AI-PROPELLER通过代理工作流将Propeller扩展为细粒度过程间代码布局优化器，在实际硬件上测量性能，实现显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后链接优化器仅限于过程内技术，未充分利用过程间布局的潜力，且由于搜索空间和复杂语义，细粒度过程间布局在实践中未得到验证。

Method: 使用Magellan代理工作流，将编译器启发式演变为细粒度过程间优化器，并通过在实际硬件上执行布局变体测量性能计数器来提供精确奖励信号，进行进化调优。

Result: 在多个基准测试（包括大型仓库规模应用）上，相比最先进的FDO和PLO，实现0.23%到1.6%的性能提升。

Conclusion: AI-PROPELLER首次实现了对工业级大型应用进行细粒度过程间代码布局优化，并取得了显著性能提升。

中文摘要：后链接优化器（PLO），如Propeller和BOLT，已经证明精确的、基于profile的代码布局可以从高度优化的二进制文件中提取显著的性能提升。然而，这些系统目前仅限于过程内技术，留下了过程间布局的全局潜力尚未被充分挖掘。由于组合爆炸的搜索空间和复杂的调用返回语义难以建模，过程间代码布局历来困难。因此，细粒度过程间布局的性能潜力在实践中尚未得到证明。AI-PROPELLER使用Magellan，一个代理工作流，它将Propeller中的编译器启发式演变为细粒度的过程间优化器，并微调生成的策略超参数。为了确保高保真度，我们放弃了近似的静态成本模型，代理工作流生成多个布局变体，并在实际硬件上执行以测量真实性能计数器，为进化循环提供精确的奖励信号。AI-PROPELLER在多个基准测试上进行了评估，包括大型仓库规模应用，实验显示在已经使用最先进的FDO和PLO优化的情况下，性能提升为0.23%到1.6%，这对于实际二进制文件是显著的。这是首次在工业环境中对大型仓库规模应用进行细粒度过程间代码布局优化。

Original abstract: Post-link optimizers (PLOs) such as Propeller and BOLT have demonstrated that precise, profile-guided code layout can extract significant performance gains from heavily optimized binaries. However, these systems are currently restricted to intraprocedural techniques, leaving the global potential of interprocedural layout largely untapped. Interprocedural code layout is historically difficult due to a combinatorially intractable search space and complex call-return semantics that are challenging to model. Consequently, the performance potential of fine-grained interprocedural layout remains unproven in practice. AI-PROPELLER uses Magellan, an agentic workflow that evolves the compiler heuristic in Propeller into a fine-grained interprocedural optimizer and fine-tunes the resulting policy hyperparameters. To ensure high-fidelity, we move away from approximate static cost models and the agentic workflow generates multiple layout variants that are executed on actual hardware to measure real performance counters, providing a precise reward signal for the evolutionary loop. AI-PROPELLER has been evaluated on several benchmarks including large warehouse-scale applications and experiments show performance improvements of 0.23% to 1.6% optimized with state-of-the-art FDO and PLO which is significant for real-world binaries. This is the first time ever that large warehouse-scale applications in industrial settings have been optimized with fine-grained interprocedural code layout.

</details>


### [19] [Can AI be Easy? Lessons Learned from the EZR.py Toolkit](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03640v1)
*Tim Menzies,Srinath Srinivasan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过阅读和重构代码构建了400行的EZR工具包，在120+表格SE优化任务上，其性能与SHAP、LIME、SMAC3等相当或更好，且速度更快、数据需求更少，证明了小统一工具包的价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反驳‘开发者不再需要阅读代码’的观点，尤其在表格SE优化任务中，认为阅读和重构代码仍能产生洞见。

Method: 构建EZR.py工具包（400行，无重度依赖），集成朴素贝叶斯、k均值聚类、CART、模拟退火、局部搜索、主动学习、互补贝叶斯文本挖掘等算法；通过在120+任务上的测试评估性能。

Result: EZR与SHAP、LIME、SMAC3、FASTREAD性能相当或更好，运行速度比SMAC3快500倍，使用数量级更少的标记数据，且能从少于十个变量构建树。

Conclusion: 在表格SE优化中，阅读和重构代码是有用的方法，小型统一工具包可以匹敌甚至超越大型库。

中文摘要：最近的许多媒体报道声称开发者不再需要阅读代码。我们不同意这种观点，至少在表格形式的软件工程（SE）优化任务领域内：这些任务包含x和y值的行，其中y值的获取成本高昂。作为证据，我们展示了400行的EZR.py，一个Python工具包（无重度依赖），实现了朴素贝叶斯、k均值聚类、分类与回归树、模拟退火、局部搜索、主动学习以及互补贝叶斯文本挖掘相关性过滤，用于表格SE数据。EZR是通过反复阅读和重构AI工具以简化并统一它们而构建的。结果表明，许多看似不同的学习算法在剥离到核心后几乎相同：经典算法各自只需几行代码，而最先进的主动学习器大约只需要80行。在MOOT仓库中的120多个表格SE优化任务上进行测试，这些微小的工具性能与最先进的解释工具（SHAP、LIME）、SMAC3优化器和基于SVM的文本挖掘过滤器（FASTREAD）相当或更好，同时比SMAC3快500倍，使用数量级更少的标记数据，并且在有数千个变量时也能从少于十个变量构建树。我们得出结论，在表格SE优化范围内，阅读和重构代码是一种产生洞察的有用方法，小型统一工具包可以匹敌大型库。EZR在开源许可下可用。通过\textsf{pip install ezr}安装；示例数据在\textsf{github.com/timm/moot}。

Original abstract: Much recent press claims that developers no longer need to read code. We disagree, at least within the domain of tabular software-engineering (SE) optimization tasks: rows of $x$ and $y$ values where the $y$ values are expensive to obtain.
  As evidence we present 400 lines of EZR.py, a Python toolkit (no heavy dependencies) that implements Naive Bayes, $k$-means clustering, classification and regression trees, simulated annealing, local search, active learning, and complementary-Bayes text-mining relevance filtering for tabular SE data. EZR was built by repeatedly reading and refactoring AI tools to simplify and unify them. The result demonstrates that many seemingly different learning algorithms are nearly the same once stripped back to their core: classical algorithms collapse to a few lines each, and a state-of-the-art active learner fits in roughly 80 lines.
  Tested on the 120+ tabular SE optimization tasks in the MOOT repository, these tiny tools perform as well as or better than state-of-the-art explanation tools (SHAP, LIME), the SMAC3 optimizer, and SVM-based text-mining filters (FASTREAD), while running 500$\times$ faster than SMAC3, using orders of magnitude less labelled data, and building trees from fewer than ten variables even when thousands are available.
  We conclude that, within the scope of tabular SE optimization, reading and refactoring code is a useful method of generating insight, and small unified toolkits can rival large libraries.
  EZR is available under an open-source license. Install via \textsf{pip install ezr}; example data at \textsf{github.com/timm/moot}.

</details>

### [20] [GTA: Generating Long-Horizon Tasks for Web Agents at Scale](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29218v1)
*Tenghao Huang,Kung-Hsiang Huang,Prafulla Kumar Choubey,Yilun Zhou,Muhao Chen,Jonathan May,Chien-Sheng Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出大规模web agent长程任务生成框架，可迁移至代码agent任务生成。

TL;DR: 提出GTA框架，通过爬取、检索生成和自动质量控制自动创建网络智能体的多跳任务基准，揭示人机性能差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网络智能体基准依赖手动构建或昂贵有偏的自动生成，缺乏过程监督，限制了对多跳跨页面任务的训练和评估。

Method: GTA框架：整合爬取、基于检索的种子生成、上下文内生成和自动质量控制，解耦爬取与生成，基于站点图强制组合性，通过确定性重放和系统验证确保密集监督。

Result: 在50多个网站（电子商务、政府、论坛、新闻）上实例化，覆盖多语言和多跳任务，基准揭示人类与智能体之间显著的性能差距。

Conclusion: 形式化多跳网络智能体任务生成，提出高效验证的自动数据创建流水线，发布具有可重复评估的动态基准。

中文摘要：网络智能体将语言模型与浏览和工具使用能力相结合，展现出作为开放网络助手的潜力。然而，由于缺乏可扩展的过程级监督，其进展日益受限。现有的基准测试大部分是手动构建的，仅提供粗略的开始-目标注释，没有中间轨迹，而最近的自动生成工作仍然昂贵、有偏见且肤浅。这些限制阻碍了对必须泛化到现实、多跳、跨页面任务的智能体的可靠训练和评估。我们引入了一个可扩展框架GTA，它整合了爬取、基于检索的种子生成、上下文内生成和自动质量控制，以生成与现实任务配对的可执行轨迹。该设计将爬取与生成分离以提高效率，将任务锚定在站点图上以强制组合性，并通过确定性重放和系统验证确保密集监督。我们在50多个网站上实例化了该流水线，涵盖电子商务、政府、论坛和新闻，具有多语言和多跳覆盖。由此产生的基准测试揭示了人类与智能体之间显著的性能差距，并实现了详细的诊断。我们的贡献有三方面：(i) 形式化多跳网络智能体任务生成，(ii) 提出一种高效且经过验证的自动数据创建流水线，(iii) 发布一个具有可重复评估的动态基准测试。

Original abstract: Web agents, which couple language models with browsing and tool-use capabilities, show promise as open web assistants. Yet progress is increasingly limited by the lack of scalable, process-level supervision. Existing benchmarks are largely manually constructed, providing only coarse start-goal annotations without intermediate trajectories, while recent automatic generation efforts remain expensive, biased, and shallow. These limitations prevent reliable training and evaluation of agents that must generalize to realistic, multi-hop, cross-page tasks. We introduce a scalable framework, GTA, that integrates crawling, retrieval-based seeding, in-context generation, and automated quality control to produce realistic tasks paired with executable trajectories. This design decouples crawling from generation for greater efficiency, grounds tasks in the site graph to enforce compositionality, and ensures dense supervision through deterministic replays and systematic validation. We instantiate the pipeline on over 50 websites covering e-commerce, government, forums, and news, with multilingual and multi-hop coverage. The resulting benchmark reveals a significant human-agent performance gap and enables detailed diagnostics. Our contributions are three-fold: (i) formalizing multi-hop web-agent task generation, (ii) proposing an efficient and validated pipeline for automatic data creation, and (iii) releasing a dynamic benchmark with reproducible evaluation.

### [21] [BenchTrace: A Benchmark for Testing Reflection Ability and Controlled Evolution in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29225v1)
*Jiahao Huang,Fei Cheng,Junfeng Jiang,Zefan Yu,Akiko Aizawa*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估LLM agent自我进化能力，含反思与故障避免，直接相关agent评测。

TL;DR: BenchTrace是一个评估LLM智能体自我进化能力的基准，通过反思评估和进化评估，发现模型反思通过率低且存在遗忘和负迁移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估仅测量任务得分，无法反映反思质量，且依赖智能体自身回合，无法针对特定失败模式。

Method: 构建包含1,821个标注回合的BenchTrace数据集，设计反思评估（探测失败识别）和进化评估（测试失败回避），并提出FAR指标。

Result: Qwen3-32B和GPT-4.1在反思评估通过率低于30%，诊断是瓶颈；进化评估中自我进化方法提升FAR，但存在遗忘和负迁移；仅完全正确反思与高FAR强相关。

Conclusion: BenchTrace揭示了当前自我进化方法的具体局限性，提供了受控、模型无关的定向评估框架。

中文摘要：自我进化智能体通过反思过去的失败来不断改进，但现有的评估存在两个方面的局限性：它仅测量任务得分，因而反思质量不得而知；并且它依赖于智能体自身的回合运行，无法针对特定的失败模式。我们提出了BenchTrace，一个用于评估大语言模型智能体自我进化能力的基准。BenchTrace构建于一个包含1,821个标注回合的快照-反思数据集之上，涵盖六种不同的任务，并包括一个通过针对性问答任务探测失败识别能力的反思评估，以及一个测试过去失败经验是否能在受控自我进化模拟中转化为回避行为的进化评估。基于BenchTrace，我们提出了失败避免率（FAR），这是一个新的评估指标，衡量智能体成功避免目标失败实例的测试用例比例。使用Qwen3-32B和GPT-4.1进行的实验表明，两个模型在反思评估上的端到端通过率均低于30%，其中诊断是主要瓶颈。进化评估显示，自我进化方法通常比非进化基线提高了FAR，但随着噪声回合的积累，智能体会遗忘早期经验，并且智能体无法将其反思泛化到特定情境之外，导致跨任务情境的负迁移。我们的相关性分析进一步揭示，只有完全正确的反思才与较高的FAR强相关。BenchTrace揭示了当前自我进化方法的具体局限性，并提供了一个受控的、模型无关的定向评估框架。

Original abstract: Self-evolving agents improve over time by reflecting on past failures, but existing evaluation is limited in two ways: it measures only task scores, leaving reflection quality unknown, and it relies on agents' own episode runs, offering no mechanism to target specific failure patterns. We present \textbf{BenchTrace}, a benchmark for evaluating self-evolution ability in LLM agents. BenchTrace is built on a snapshot-reflection dataset of 1,821 annotated episodes spanning six diverse tasks, and comprises a \textbf{Reflection Evaluation} that probes failure identification through targeted QA tasks, and an \textbf{Evolution Evaluation} that tests whether past failure experience translates into avoidance behavior in a controlled self-evolution simulation. Building on BenchTrace, we propose \textbf{failure avoidance rate (FAR)}, a new evaluation metric measuring the fraction of test cases in which the agent successfully avoids the target failure instance. Experiments with Qwen3-32B and GPT-4.1 reveal that both models fall below a 30\% end-to-end pass rate on reflection evaluation, with diagnosis as the primary bottleneck. Evolution evaluation shows that self-evolution methods generally improve FAR over the non-evolving baseline, but agents forget early lessons as noise episodes accumulate, and agents fail to generalize their reflections beyond the specific context, causing negative transfer across task contexts. Our correlation analysis further reveals that only a fully correct reflection is strongly associated with higher FAR. BenchTrace exposes concrete limits of current self-evolution approaches and provides a controlled, model-agnostic framework for targeted evaluation.

</details>


### [22] [Rethinking Literature Search Evaluation: Deep Research Helps, and Human Citation Lists Are Not a Ground Truth](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29234v1)
*Gaurav Sahu,Laurent Charlin,Christopher Pal*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Deep Research检索pipeline，可作为检索agent方法，对agent工具使用有启发。

TL;DR: 通过深度研究管道将文献搜索召回率从<20%提升到>80%，并发现人类参考文献作为评估目标存在偏见（仅51%相关），而AI重排序器达到86-88%，提出多轴评估框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献搜索评估通常依赖人类参考文献列表作为真实标准，但其可靠性未知；同时传统API搜索召回率低，需要改进检索方法。

Method: 实现一个深度研究管道，处理完整查询论文并沿参考文献广度优先扩展检索；使用中性LLM作为评判者评估人类引用和AI重排序结果的相关性；在OpenAlex合著网络上分析引用偏差。

Result: 深度研究管道在RollingEval-Jun25上将召回率从<20%提升到>80%；仅51%的人类引用被判断为中度相关或更高，而最强AI重排序器为86-88%；人类引用直接合作者的可能性是AI的2.5倍。

Conclusion: 文献搜索评估不应依赖单一指标，而应联合报告召回率、主题相关性评分、排序列表多样性和合著距离诊断，以全面衡量引用质量。

中文摘要：我们从两个互补的角度研究大规模文献搜索：改进检索流程，以及将人类参考文献列表作为评估目标进行压力测试。首先，我们实现了一个深度研究（Deep Research）流程，该流程处理完整的查询论文，并沿其参考文献进行广度优先的检索结果扩展，结果表明其大幅优于仅基于API的搜索，在RollingEval-Jun25（一个包含250篇论文的文献搜索基准）上将召回率从低于20%提升至超过80%。其次，我们使用中立的LLM作为评判者，判断人类参考文献是否是该任务的可靠真实标准。我们发现了显著的局限性：只有51%的人类引用被判断为中度相关或更高，而最强的AI重排序器这一比例为86-88%。我们在OpenAlex合著网络上研究了这一差距，发现人类引用直接合作者的可能性是最佳AI重排序器的2.5倍。综合来看，我们的结果反对单轴文献搜索评估：召回率、主题相关性评分、排序列表多样性和合著距离诊断各自衡量引用质量的互补属性，应联合报告。

Original abstract: We study large-scale literature search from two complementary angles: improving the retrieval pipeline, and stress-testing the human reference list as an evaluation target. First, we implement a Deep Research pipeline that processes the full query paper and expands the retrieved results breadth-first along their bibliographies, and show that it substantially outperforms vanilla API-only search, raising recall on RollingEval-Jun25 (a 250-paper literature-search benchmark) from below 20% to above 80%. Second, we use a neutral LLM-as-a-judge to determine if human references are sound ground truth for the task. We find significant limitations: only 51% of human citations are judged moderately relevant or higher, against 86--88% for the strongest AI-based re-rankers. We study this gap on the OpenAlex co-authorship graph, finding that humans are 2.5x more likely than the best AI re-rankers to cite a direct collaborator. Together, our results argue against single-axis literature-search evaluation: recall, topical-relevance scoring, ranked-list diversity, and a co-authorship-distance diagnostic each measure complementary properties of citation quality and should be reported jointly.

</details>


### [23] [Provably Secure Agent Guardrail](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29251v1)
*Benlong Wu,Weiming Zhang,Kejiang Chen,Han Fang,Nenghai Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出可证明安全的agent guardrail，基于形式化验证，直接相关agent安全。

TL;DR: 提出ePCA框架，通过神经符号隔离架构强制智能体将意图形式化为逻辑约束，实现零攻击成功率和零误报率，解决大型语言模型智能体的安全下限问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防御架构依赖经验性语义护栏和概率性大模型裁决器，无法提供确定性的安全下限，难以应对复杂语义符号解耦攻击。

Method: 提出基于逻辑推理根本局限性的安全新范式，设计具有神经符号隔离架构的可执行证明约束动作（ePCA）框架，放弃对自然语言的语义信任，强制智能体将意图无损形式化为一级逻辑数学约束后再执行操作。

Result: 在宏观和微观二维动态对抗系统评估中，实现零攻击成功率和零误报率，计算延迟极低。

Conclusion: 为未来智能系统提供有条件的正式基础及工程范式，构建底层防御基础。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型从有界的生成引擎转变为具有广泛执行权限的智能体，人工智能失控引发了人工智能安全领域的根本性危机。现有防御架构严重依赖经验性的语义护栏和概率性大模型裁决器，这些机制在面对复杂的语义符号解耦攻击时，无法提供确定性的安全下限。为了克服这一经验性语义护栏困境，本文提出了一种基于逻辑推理根本局限性的智能体安全新范式。基于该范式，我们进一步引入了一种具有神经符号隔离架构的可执行证明约束动作（ePCA）框架。该框架放弃了对自然语言的语义信任，强制智能体在执行物理操作之前将其意图无损地形式化为一级逻辑数学约束。宏观和微观二维动态对抗系统的实证评估表明，我们的形式化验证机制在评估场景中实现了零攻击成功率和零误报率，且计算延迟极低。本研究为在显式系统假设下构建未来智能系统的底层防御基础提供了有条件的正式基础及工程范式。

Original abstract: As large language models transition from bounded generative engines to agents with expansive execution privileges, AI going out of control precipitates a fundamental crisis in artificial intelligence security. Existing defense architectures heavily rely on empirical semantic guardrails and probabilistic large model adjudicators, mechanisms that fail to provide deterministic security lower bounds when facing complex semantic symbol decoupling attacks. To overcome this empirical semantic guardrail dilemma, this paper proposes a new security paradigm for agents based on the fundamental limitations of logical reasoning. Based on this paradigm, we further introduce an executable Proof-Constrained Action (ePCA) framework with a neural symbolic isolation architecture. This framework abandons semantic trust in natural language, forcing agents to losslessly formalize their intentions into first-order logical mathematical constraints before performing physical operations. Empirical evaluations of macroscopic and microscopic two-dimensional dynamic adversarial systems demonstrate that our formal verification mechanism achieves zero attack success rate and zero false positive rate across the evaluated scenarios, with extremely low computational latency. This research provides a conditional formal foundation under explicit system assumptions and an engineering paradigm for constructing the underlying defense foundation for future intelligent systems.

### [24] [OpenClawBench: Benchmarking Process-side Anomalies in Real-world Agent Execution Trajectories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29253v1)
*Yibing Liu,Yangze Liu,Xiaolong Yin,Bin Wang,Chong Zhang,Hao Yin,Zhongyi Han*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 构建agent执行轨迹异常检测benchmark，关注过程监督与可靠性。

TL;DR: 本文提出结果-过程差距概念，构建OpenClawBench数据集和FullTax标注方法，实验表明成功评估忽略大量过程异常，并训练检测器取得较好效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估仅关注最终任务成功，忽略执行中的过程异常，导致问题被隐藏。

Method: 基于BFCL和OpenClaw构建31,264条轨迹数据集，提出FullTax进行结构化异常标注，包括多种标签；使用LoRA微调Gemma 3 12B检测器。

Result: 31,135条通过判据的执行中2,904条被标记为异常；检测器F1=0.729。

Conclusion: OpenClawBench将日志转化为可审计监督，支持可靠性研究。

中文摘要：任务成功可能掩盖实际智能体执行中的过程异常。一个智能体可能通过最终任务判据，但依然累积了未解决的歧义、不安全的外部写入、被忽略的错误、弱承诺或能力边界过度承诺。我们将这种不匹配称为“结果-过程差距”，并引入OpenClawBench，这是一个用于测量和监督实际智能体执行过程中过程侧异常的大规模数据集。OpenClawBench基于6个源模型产生的BFCL驱动的OpenClaw会话构建，包含31,264条带注释的轨迹。它将任务判据结果与结构化的过程证据对齐。FullTax将对齐后的轨迹转换为结构化的异常监督：二元标签、支持证据、起始/跨度定位、严重性、可恢复性以及一个5类异常分类体系。借助OpenClawBench，我们使结果-过程差距可测量。在31,135次通过判据的执行中，仍有2,904条在FullTax下被标记为过程异常。这些结果表明，仅基于成功的评估遗漏了实际智能体执行中一类具体的过程侧故障。在高质量FullTax监督池上训练的LoRA微调Gemma 3 12B检测器，在更干净标签的保留测试集上达到了二元F1=0.729。OpenClawBench将实际智能体执行日志转化为可审计、可重复使用的监督，用于研究、诊断和操作监控运行时智能体可靠性。

Original abstract: Task success can hide process anomalies in real-world agent executions. An agent may pass the final task oracle while still accumulating unresolved ambiguity, unsafe external writes, ignored errors, weakly grounded commitments, or capability-boundary overcommitment. We study this mismatch as the Outcome-Process Gap and introduce OpenClawBench, a large-scale dataset for measuring and supervising process-side anomalies in real agent execution processes. OpenClawBench is built from BFCL-driven OpenClaw sessions produced by 6 source models and contains 31,264 annotated trajectories. It aligns task-oracle outcomes with structured process evidence. FullTax converts the aligned trajectories into structured anomaly supervision: binary labels, supporting evidence, onset/span localization, severity, recoverability, and a 5-class anomaly taxonomy. Using OpenClawBench, we make the Outcome-Process Gap measurable. Among 31,135 oracle-passing executions, 2,904 are still labeled process-anomalous under FullTax. These results show that success-only evaluation misses a concrete class of process-side failures in real agent executions. A LoRA-fine-tuned Gemma 3 12B detector trained on the high-confidence FullTax supervised pool reaches binary F1=0.729 on the cleaner-labels held-out test split. Together, OpenClawBench turns real agent execution logs into auditable and reusable supervision for studying, diagnosing, and operationally monitoring runtime agent reliability.

</details>


### [25] [Harmonizing Real-Time Constraints and Long-Horizon Reasoning: An Asynchronous Agentic Framework for Dynamic Scheduling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29262v1)
*Shijie Cao,Yuan Yuan,Jing Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出异步agent框架用于动态调度，双流架构解耦实时执行与LLM推理，通用agent架构可迁移

TL;DR: RACE-Sched通过异步双流架构将LLM推理与实时调度解耦，实现了动态FJSP的高效求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在动态FJSP中难以兼顾实时响应与全局优化，且LLM推理延迟与工业控制系统的实时要求冲突。

Method: 提出RACE-Sched框架，包含反应式流（低延迟符号启发式）和深思熟虑流（LLM合成/验证/演化规则），通过沙盒测试和原子更新确保安全，并利用语义规则库增强可迁移性。

Result: 在GEN-Bench、MK-Bench和JMS-Bench上，RACE-Sched性能优于深度强化学习和LLM基线。

Conclusion: RACE-Sched成功协调了实时约束与长期推理，为动态FJSP提供了高质量且鲁棒的解决方案。

中文摘要：动态柔性作业车间调度问题（DFJSP）需要在即时响应随机干扰和全局优化生产目标之间进行权衡。传统的优先级规则不足以灵活处理复杂干扰，而基于学习的方法则常常牺牲可解释性或无法跨问题规模泛化。尽管大型语言模型（LLM）提供了高级推理能力以弥合这一差距，但其巨大的推理延迟与工业控制系统的毫秒级决策周期不兼容。为了解决这一冲突，我们提出了RACE-Sched，一种异步基于智能体的框架，通过双流架构将策略执行与逻辑推理解耦。反应式流执行低延迟符号启发式规则以实现实时调度，而并行的深思熟虑流则利用LLM来合成、验证和演化这些规则。候选规则在沙盒中经过严格测试，并通过原子更新部署，确保安全且不阻塞控制循环。此外，语义规则库索引了已验证的启发式规则，用于基于检索的初始化，从而增强跨问题规模的可迁移性。在GEN-Bench、MK-Bench和JMS-Bench上的广泛评估表明，RACE-Sched优于领先的深度强化学习和其他基于LLM的基线。该方法协调了实时约束与长期推理，实现了卓越的解决方案质量和稳健的动态事件适应。

Original abstract: The Dynamic Flexible Job Shop Scheduling Problem (DFJSP) necessitates a trade-off between instant reaction to stochastic disturbances and global optimization of production goals. Conventional priority rules are insufficiently flexible to handle complex disruptions, whereas learning-based approaches often compromise interpretability or fail to generalize across problem scales. Although Large Language Models (LLMs) offer advanced reasoning capabilities to bridge this gap, their substantial inference latency is incompatible with the millisecond-level decision cycles of industrial control systems. To resolve this conflict, we introduce RACE-Sched, an asynchronous agent-based framework that decouples policy execution from logical reasoning via a dual-stream architecture. The Reactive Stream executes low-latency symbolic heuristics to enable real-time dispatching, while the parallel Deliberative Stream leverages an LLM to synthesize, validate, and evolve these rules. Candidate rules undergo rigorous testing in a sandbox and are deployed via atomic updates, ensuring safety without blocking the control loop. Additionally, a semantic rule repository indexes validated heuristics for retrieval-based initialization which enhances transferability across problem scales. Extensive evaluations on GEN-Bench, MK-Bench, and JMS-Bench demonstrate that RACE-Sched outperforms leading Deep Reinforcement Learning and other LLM-based baselines. This approach harmonizes real-time constraints with long-horizon reasoning to achieve superior solution quality and robust adaptation to dynamic events.

### [26] [Indexing the Unreadable: LLM-Native Recursive Construction and Search of Service Taxonomies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29270v1)
*Wei Zheng,Yang Yan,Yiyang Shao,Jinyang Li,Zeze Chang,Yukuang Jia,Qiming Mao,Chihyung Wang,Jingbin Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 面向agent的服务发现，提出渐进式层次分类实现上下文管理，直接相关agent工具使用

TL;DR: 提出A2X渐进式服务发现方案，通过层次化分类和逐层检索解决LLM在大量服务下的上下文稀缺问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在服务发现中面临上下文窗口限制和'中间迷失'问题，导致有效上下文稀缺无法随服务数量扩展。

Method: 利用LLM自动将注册服务组织成层次化分类法，查询时逐层遍历，使得每次LLM调用只处理与查询高度相关的小候选集。

Result: 相比全上下文转储，A2X以1/9的提示令牌成本提升6.2个点的命中率；相比基于嵌入的基线，命中率提升20个点以上。

Conclusion: 通过解耦有效上下文稀缺性与注册库大小，显著降低令牌消耗并提高检索准确性。

中文摘要：互联网代理（IoA）时代正在形成：LLM代理有望通过编排快速增长的大量模型上下文协议（MCP）服务器、代理到代理（A2A）端点、可复用技能和其他LLM可调用服务来实现用户目标。然而，LLM面临与这种机制的结构性不匹配：有效上下文是一种稀缺资源，不随服务数量扩展。将数千个服务描述连接到一个提示中会溢出上下文窗口，即使窗口足够大，模型也会系统地忽略长输入中间部分的信息，即被广泛记录的“中间迷失”现象。这从根本上是一个服务发现中的上下文管理问题。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种LLM原生的渐进式披露方案及其具体实现A2X（面向任何事物的代理到代理服务发现）：一个LLM驱动的管道，自动将注册的服务组织成层次化分类法，并在查询时逐层遍历，使得每次LLM调用只看到一个与用户查询高度相关的小候选集。这解耦了有效上下文稀缺性与注册库大小，显著减少了令牌消耗，同时提高了检索准确性。与全上下文转储相比，A2X在仅九分之一的提示令牌成本下获得了6.2个点的命中率提升；与最先进的开源基于嵌入的基线相比，A2X将命中率提高了20个点以上。

Original abstract: The era of the Internet of Agents (IoA) is taking shape: LLM agents are expected to fulfill user goals by orchestrating fast-growing populations of Model Context Protocol (MCP) servers, Agent-to-Agent (A2A) endpoints, reusable skills, and other LLM-callable services. Yet LLMs face a structural mismatch with this regime: effective context is a scarce resource that does not scale with the number of services. Concatenating thousands of service descriptions into a prompt overflows the context window, and even when the window is large enough, models systematically under-attend to information in the middle of long inputs, the well-documented Lost-in-the-Middle phenomenon. This is fundamentally a question of context management for service discovery. To address this, we propose an LLM-native progressive-disclosure scheme and its concrete instantiation, A2X (Agent-to-Anything service discovery): an LLM-driven pipeline that automatically organizes the registered services into a hierarchical taxonomy and walks it layer by layer at query time, so that every LLM call sees only a small candidate set highly relevant to the user query. This decouples effective-context scarcity from registry size and significantly reduces token consumption while improving retrieval accuracy. Compared to full-context dumping, A2X achieves a 6.2-point Hit Rate gain at one-ninth the prompt-token cost; compared to the state-of-the-art open-source embedding-based baseline, A2X improves Hit Rate by more than 20 points.

</details>


### [27] [CoHyDE: Iterative Co-Training of LLM Rewriter & Dense Encoder for Tool Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29271v1)
*Vaishali Senthil,Ashutosh Hathidara,Sebastian Schreiber*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 针对agent工具检索的联合训练方法，有效提升检索准确性，直接相关agent工具使用

TL;DR: 提出CoHyDE，迭代协同训练稠密编码器和LLM重写器，显著提升工具检索性能，尤其对模糊查询改进明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对比编码器微调和HyDE查询扩展方法各有缺陷，无法同时处理形式良好和模糊查询。

Method: CoHyDE迭代过程：编码器用重写器生成的目录风格假设性描述通过InfoNCE重新训练，重写器用DPO基于编码器检索分数进行偏好对齐，双方预热后循环训练。

Result: 在ToolBench约10k工具子集上，CoHyDE标准查询NDCG@5提升+2.5 pp，模糊查询提升+6.3 pp，最难模糊查询提升+8 pp；消融实验证实协同训练是关键。

Conclusion: CoHyDE有效解决LLM代理工具检索的语言鸿沟，特别提升模糊查询的检索性能。

中文摘要：从大型API目录中检索工具是LLM代理的核心瓶颈：用户查询以口语化、通常欠规范的语言出现，而目录使用技术性API词汇，没有固定的编码器能够单独弥合这一鸿沟。两种主要的训练方法——对比编码器微调和冻结LLM的HyDE风格查询扩展——从相反的两端解决这个问题，并在互补的方向上失败：微调后的编码器在查询的表面形式已经匹配目录时表现优异，但在不匹配时崩溃；而零样本HyDE对欠规范查询更具鲁棒性，但生成不了解目录的假设性描述，当查询形式良好时检索性能下降。我们提出了CoHyDE，一种迭代过程，将稠密编码器和LLM重写器训练为单一的协同进化系统：编码器使用重写器生成的目录风格假设性描述通过InfoNCE进行重新训练，重写器通过DPO根据编码器的检索分数进行偏好对齐，双方在循环开始前对工具目录进行预热。在ToolBench目录的约10k工具子集上，三轮CoHyDE在标准查询上比最强的单组件基线提高+2.5个点的NDCG@5，在保留的模糊查询上提高+6.3个点，在最难的模糊级别上增益高达+8个点。消融实验证实协同训练是关键因素：单独使用任一组件都无法在形式良好和模糊查询上匹配CoHyDE，在模糊查询上损失高达-8个点。

Original abstract: Tool retrieval over large API catalogs is a core bottleneck for LLM agents: user queries arrive in colloquial, often underspecified language, while the catalog uses technical API vocabulary that no fixed encoder can bridge on its own. The two dominant training approaches, contrastive encoder fine-tuning and HyDE-style query expansion with a frozen LLM, address this problem from opposite ends and fail in complementary directions: the fine-tuned encoder excels when the query's surface form already matches the catalog but collapses when it does not, while zero-shot HyDE is more robust to underspecified queries yet generates catalog-unaware hypothetical descriptions that degrade retrieval when queries are well-formed. We introduce CoHyDE, an iterative procedure that trains the dense encoder and the LLM rewriter as a single co-evolving system: the encoder is retrained with InfoNCE on catalog-style hypothetical descriptions produced by the rewriter, and the rewriter is preference-aligned via DPO against the encoder's retrieval scores, with both sides warm-started on the tool catalog before the loop begins. On a ~10k tool subset of the ToolBench catalog, three rounds of CoHyDE improve over the strongest single-component baseline by +2.5 pp NDCG@5 on standard queries and +6.3 pp on held-out vague queries, with gains as large as +8 pp on the hardest vague tier. Ablations confirm that co-training is the key ingredient: using either component in isolation fails to match CoHyDE on both well-formed and vague queries, with losses of up to -8 pp on vague queries.

</details>


### [28] [Rubric-Guided Process Reward for Stepwise Model Routing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29310v1)
*Shenghao Ye,Yu Guo,Zhengheng Li,Shuangwu Chen,Jian Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出步骤级模型路由框架，使用过程奖励，可迁移到多agent路由或选择

TL;DR: 提出RoRo框架，通过规则指导的过程奖励优化逐步模型路由，在推理任务中提升准确性和成本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将路由建模为过程但仅用结果奖励监督，无法评估中间路由决策，导致性能和泛化不足。

Method: 收集多样路由轨迹，基于结果、成本和过程质量构建偏好对；交替训练Rubricor生成评估规则和Judge评分；结合过程与结果奖励，通过GRPO优化路由策略。

Result: 在五个推理基准的相同和跨模型设置下，RoRo始终优于强基线，实现更好的准确性和成本权衡。

Conclusion: RoRo是一种有效的逐步模型路由方法，通过过程奖励显著提升路由性能与泛化能力。

中文摘要：逐步模型路由通过将每个推理步骤分配给合适的模型来提高大型推理模型（LRM）的效率。最近的方法将路由建模为顺序决策过程，并使用强化学习训练路由器。然而，尽管他们将路由建模为过程，他们仍然使用结果奖励来监督路由器。这种奖励仅反映最终答案的正确性，无法评估中间路由决策，这会削弱性能和泛化能力。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了RoRo，一种基于规则的过程奖励框架，用于逐步模型路由。RoRo首先收集多样的路由轨迹，并基于结果、成本和过程质量构建偏好对。然后，它通过交替优化训练一个Rubricor来生成查询特定的评估规则，以及一个Judge来在此规则下对路由轨迹进行评分。由此得到的过程奖励与结果奖励结合，通过GRPO优化路由策略。在五个推理基准上的实验，包括同族和跨族设置，表明RoRo始终优于强基线，并实现了更好的准确性和成本权衡。

Original abstract: Stepwise model routing improves the efficiency of Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) by assigning each reasoning step to a suitable model. Recent methods formulate routing as a sequential decision process and train the router with reinforcement learning. However, although they model routing as a process, they still supervise the router with outcome rewards. Such rewards only reflect final answer correctness and fail to evaluate intermediate routing decisions, which can weaken performance and generalization. To address this gap, we propose RoRo, a rubric-guided process reward framework for stepwise model routing. RoRo first collects diverse routing trajectories and constructs preference pairs based on outcome, cost, and process quality. It then trains a Rubricor to generate a query-specific evaluation rubric and a Judge to score routing trajectories under this rubric through alternating optimization. The resulting process rewards are combined with outcome rewards to optimize the routing policy via GRPO. Experiments on five reasoning benchmarks under both same-family and cross-family settings show that RoRo consistently outperforms strong baselines and achieves better accuracy and cost trade-offs.

</details>


### [29] [PassNet: Scaling Large Language Models for Graph Compiler Pass Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29357v1)
*Yiqun Liu,Yingsheng Wu,Ruqi Yang,Enrong Zheng,Honglei Qiu,Sijun He,Tai Liang,Jingjing Wu,Yuhan Zhou,Yiwei Zhang,Dongyan Chen,Weihan Yi,Xinqi Li,Siqi Bao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM生成编译器pass，直接相关自动代码优化

TL;DR: PassNet是一个基于LLM的编译器通证生成生态系统，通过数据集和基准测试展示了LLM在编译器优化中的潜力，并验证了微调小模型可接近前沿性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有张量编译器在长尾子图上性能不佳，且LLM优化工作局限于独立核生成，缺乏与编译器流水线集成的结构化通证生成方法。

Method: 提出PassNet，包含大规模计算图数据集PassNet-Dataset和基准测试PassBench，采用错误感知加速分数ES_t作为评估指标，并设计了分层完整性防御。

Result: 最佳LLM在PassBench上聚合性能落后TorchInductor 37%，但单个子图上可高达3倍加速；微调小模型在约4000个轨迹上获得2.67倍改进，接近前沿模型。

Conclusion: LLM能力足够，但一致性是瓶颈；PassNet作为实时训练基础设施可有效提升LLM驱动的编译器优化性能。

中文摘要：现代张量编译器（如TorchInductor）在主流模型上实现了显著的加速，但在长尾工作负载上面临系统性的性能瓶颈——我们的分析显示，43%的真实世界子图在默认编译下会出现端到端性能下降。虽然LLM为实现自动化优化提供了一条路径，但现有工作主要集中在独立的核生成上。我们认为，通证生成——即LLM编写可直接集成到编译器流水线中的结构化图变换——是更合适的抽象。为此，我们提出PassNet，这是首个用于基于LLM的编译器通证生成的大规模生态系统，包括：(1) PassNet-Dataset，包含来自10万个真实世界模型的超过1.8万个独特计算图；(2) PassBench，包含200个精心挑选的长尾可融合任务（共计2060个子图），在错误感知加速分数（ES_t）——一个统一了正确性、稳定性和性能的指标——下进行评估，并配备分层完整性防御以防止LLM的系统性滥用。实验表明，PassBench既具有高度的区分性，又真正未达到饱和：最佳前沿模型在聚合性能上落后TorchInductor 37%，但在单个子图上，LLM可实现对同一编译器的高达3倍加速——这表明瓶颈在于一致性，而非能力。在仅约4000个PassNet轨迹上微调一个小模型即可获得2.67倍的改进，接近前沿模型性能，证明了巨大的提升空间，并验证了PassNet作为推进LLM驱动编译器优化的实时训练基础设施的有效性。所有数据、基准和工具均已公开。

Original abstract: Modern tensor compilers such as TorchInductor deliver substantial speedups on mainstream models, yet face a systematic performance ceiling on long-tail workloads -- our profiling shows that 43% of real-world subgraphs experience end-to-end slowdowns under default compilation. While LLMs offer a path toward automated optimization, existing efforts focus on standalone kernel generation. We argue that pass generation -- where LLMs author structured graph transformations that integrate directly into compiler pipelines -- is the more appropriate abstraction. We propose PassNet, the first large-scale ecosystem for LLM-based compiler pass generation, comprising: (1) PassNet-Dataset, over 18K unique computational graphs from 100K real-world models; and (2) PassBench, 200 curated long-tail fusible tasks (comprising 2,060 subgraphs in total) evaluated under the Error-aware Speedup Score (ES_t) -- a metric unifying correctness, stability, and performance -- with layered integrity defenses against systematic LLM exploitation. Experiments reveal that PassBench is both highly discriminative and genuinely unsaturated: the best frontier model trails TorchInductor by 37% in aggregate, yet on individual subgraphs LLMs achieve up to 3x speedup over the same compiler -- indicating that the bottleneck is consistency, not capability. Fine-tuning a small model on merely ~4K PassNet trajectories yields a 2.67x improvement approaching frontier-model performance, demonstrating substantial headroom and validating PassNet as live training infrastructure for advancing LLM-driven compiler optimization. All data, benchmarks, and tooling are publicly available.

Selection reason: 交互式ASR agentic修正框架，可迁移至coding agent反馈循环

TL;DR: 提出Agentic ASR闭环框架，通过多轮交互细化ASR输出，并引入S^2ER语义评估指标，实验证明迭代交互显著降低语义错误。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单遍ASR难以纠正关键语义错误，且词级指标无法反映语义问题，亟需交互式范式。

Method: 将交互式ASR形式化为多轮细化任务，提出Agentic ASR框架（单遍ASR+语义纠正+意图路由+推理编辑），并设计S^2ER指标和交互式仿真系统。

Result: 在多语言等基准上，迭代交互持续降低语义错误，S^2ER增益远超WER/CER；人机对齐和消融验证了语义判断器的可靠性和框架鲁棒性。
