中文摘要：自动语音识别（ASR）是人机交互的核心组成部分，也是基于LLM的助手和代理日益重要的前端。然而，大多数当前的ASR系统仍然遵循单遍范式，这与人类交流中通过迭代澄清和细化来解决误解的方式不一致。这种不匹配使得一旦发生关键语义错误就很难纠正。同时，词级别指标如WER或CER无法充分反映这一问题。为了解决这些限制，我们将交互式ASR公式化为多轮细化任务，并提出了Agentic ASR，一个闭环框架，结合了单遍ASR前端与语义纠正、意图路由和基于推理的编辑。我们进一步引入了句子级语义错误率（S^2ER），一种基于LLM的语义评估指标，以及交互式仿真系统，用于可扩展和可重复的基准测试。在多语言、命名实体密集和代码切换基准上的实验表明，迭代交互持续减少语义错误，在S^2ER上的增益远大于传统词级别指标。人机对齐和消融研究进一步验证了语义判断器的可靠性和所提出框架的鲁棒性。代码可在https://interactiveasr.github.io/获取，实时演示可在https://i-asr.sjtuxlance.com/获取。

Original abstract: Automatic speech recognition (ASR) is a core component of human--computer interaction and an increasingly important front-end for LLM-based assistants and agents. However, most current ASR systems still follow a single-pass paradigm, which is poorly aligned with human communication, where misunderstandings are resolved through iterative clarification and refinement. This mismatch makes it difficult to correct meaning-critical errors once they occur. Meanwhile, token-level metrics such as WER or CER cannot adequately reflect such a problem. To address these limitations, we formulate \emph{Interactive ASR} as a multi-turn refinement task and propose \textbf{Agentic ASR}, a closed-loop framework that combines a single-pass ASR front-end with semantic correction, intent routing, and reasoning-based editing. We further introduce the \textbf{Sentence-level Semantic Error Rate} ($S^2ER$), an LLM-based semantic evaluation metric, together with an \textbf{Interactive Simulation System} for scalable and reproducible benchmarking. Experiments on multilingual, named-entity-intensive, and code-switching benchmarks show that iterative interaction consistently reduces semantic errors, with much larger gains in $S^2ER$ than in conventional token-level metrics. Human--AI alignment and ablation studies further validate the reliability of the semantic judge and the robustness of the proposed framework. The code is available at: https://interactiveasr.github.io/ and the live demo is available at https://i-asr.sjtuxlance.com/

### [32] [The Curse of Helpfulness: Inverse Scaling Law in Robustness to Distractor Instructions via DistractionIF](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29491v1)
*Zeli Su,Zhankai Xu,Tianlei Chen,Longfei Zheng,Xiaolu Zhang,Jun Zhou,Wentao Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究LLM对干扰指令的鲁棒性，涉及agent/RAG任务的逆缩放，方法可迁移

TL;DR: 本文提出DistractionIF基准，发现LLM在参考文本干扰下存在反向缩放现象，并使用GRPO强化学习提升鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在RAG等系统中需处理含语义噪声的参考文本，现有模型易将噪声误读为指令，缺乏相关鲁棒性评估。

Method: 构建DistractionIF基准，通过实验观察缩放效应，结合困惑度分析机制，并采用GRPO强化学习恢复决策边界。

Result: 模型越大鲁棒性越差，性能下降达30%；GRPO将鲁棒性提升15.5%且不影响通用指令跟随。

Conclusion: 揭示了参考接地任务中的鲁棒性差距，验证了强化学习在实现数据-指令分离方面的有效性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地部署在智能体和检索增强生成（RAG）系统中，在这些系统中，它们必须对外部提供的参考文本执行用户指定的任务。实际上，这种上下文通常是非结构化的，并且混杂着良性但类似指令的语义噪声，例如编辑评论和系统跟踪，这些应严格被视为数据。我们引入了DistractionIF，一个旨在评估参考文本中此类干扰指令鲁棒性的基准。在一系列广泛的模型中，我们观察到一致的反向缩放现象：更大的模型通常鲁棒性更差，随着规模增加，性能下降高达30个百分点。从机制上讲，我们的困惑度分析表明，缩放侵蚀了鲁棒和分心行为之间的概率边界，使模型越来越倾向于将噪声过度解释为指令。为了解决这个问题，我们证明了强化学习，特别是组相对策略优化（GRPO），可以恢复这个边界，在不损害通用指令跟随能力的情况下将鲁棒性提高高达15.5%。我们的发现突显了在参考接地任务中关键的指令跟随鲁棒性差距，并确立了强化学习作为在规模上强制执行严格数据-指令分离的有前途的途径。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in agentic and retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems, where they must execute user-specified tasks over externally provided reference text. In practice, such context is often unstructured and contaminated with benign but instruction-like semantic noise, such as editorial comments and system traces, which should be treated strictly as data. We introduce DistractionIF, a benchmark designed to evaluate robustness against such distractor instructions in reference text. Across a broad range of models, we observe a consistent inverse scaling phenomenon: larger models are often less robust, with performance dropping by up to 30 points as scale increases. Mechanistically, our perplexity analysis reveals that scaling erodes the probabilistic boundary between robust and distracted behaviors, making models increasingly prone to over-interpreting noise as instructions. To address this, we demonstrate that reinforcement learning, specifically Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), can restore this boundary, improving robustness by up to 15.5% without compromising general instruction-following capability. Our findings highlight a critical instruction-following robustness gap in reference-grounded tasks and establish reinforcement learning as a promising path for enforcing strict data-instruction separation at scale.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现智能体层面规则遵守脆弱、依赖结构支撑；评估层面不同环境排行榜有效性差异大，失败密集环境混淆鲁棒性与战略能力。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）正越来越多地被部署为交互式智能体，但它们在长时间交互中的社交和战略推理能力仍然知之甚少。现有评估依赖于静态情景或单一游戏基准，无法捕捉真实多智能体环境所要求的持续、多方面的推理。我们引入了Mindgames，这是一个用于LLM智能体的多游戏竞技场和评估平台，它操作化了与“心智理论”相关的互补推理需求：隐藏信息下的信念归因、通过重复战略交互进行对手建模、知识不对称下的合作推理以及社交演绎中的持续欺骗。基于TextArena构建，Mindgames提供了统一的交互界面、基于TrueSkill的评分以及跨四个游戏环境的完整轨迹记录。我们通过在一次主要AI会议上举办的2025年竞赛周期实例化了Mindgames，该竞赛评估了来自76个团队的944个提交智能体，涉及四个游戏：Colonel Blotto、Iterated Prisoner's Dilemma、Codenames和Secret Mafia。我们的分析揭示了智能体层面和评估层面的局限性：脆弱的规则遵守仍然是一个主要瓶颈，顶级系统反复依赖明确的结构支撑，并且排行榜的有效性在不同环境之间存在显著差异。特别是，失败密集的环境可能奖励对对手错误的鲁棒性，与战略能力同等重要，Secret Mafia在此周期中表现出明显的错误-生存混淆。我们发布了一个包含29,571个多智能体游戏的数据集，带有回合级观察、动作和奖励，以及MG-Ref，一个确定性的离线锦标赛协议，该协议使用与本分析相同的错误归因视角，将新智能体与一个由排名靠前、低错误的Stage II提交组成的冻结参考池进行评分。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as interactive agents, yet their capacity for social and strategic reasoning over extended interaction remains poorly understood. Existing evaluations rely on static vignettes or single-game benchmarks that cannot capture the sustained, multi-faceted reasoning that real-world multi-agent settings demand. We introduce Mindgames, a multi-game arena and evaluation platform for LLM agents that operationalizes complementary reasoning demands relevant to ``theory of mind'': belief attribution under hidden information, opponent modeling through repeated strategic interaction, cooperative inference under knowledge asymmetries, and sustained deception in social deduction. Built on TextArena, Mindgames provides a unified interaction interface, TrueSkill-based rating, and full trajectory logging across four game environments. We instantiate Mindgames through a 2025 competition cycle hosted at a major AI conference, which assessed 944 submitted agents from 76 teams across four games: Colonel Blotto, Iterated Prisoner's Dilemma, Codenames, and Secret Mafia. Our analysis surfaces both agent-level and evaluation-level limitations: brittle rule adherence remains a major bottleneck, top-performing systems repeatedly rely on explicit structural scaffolding, and leaderboard validity differs sharply across environments. In particular, failure-heavy environments can reward robustness to opponent errors as much as strategic ability, with Secret Mafia exhibiting a pronounced error-survival confound in this cycle. We release a dataset of 29,571 multi-agent games with turn-level observations, actions, and rewards, together with MG-Ref, a deterministic offline tournament protocol that scores new agents against a frozen reference pool of top-ranked, low-error Stage~II submissions under the same error-attribution lens used in this analysis.

### [34] [DeepSurvey: Enhancing Analytical Depth and Citation Reliability in Automated Survey Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29522v1)
*Ziyue Yang,Da Ma,Hanqi Li,Zijian Wang,Tiancheng Huang,Zijian Hu,Chenrun Wang,Yunzhe Zhang,Xiaobao Wu,Kai Yu,Lu Chen*

TL;DR: DeepSurvey通过从全文提取结构化要点、建模论文关系、融合代码分析增强深度，并采用引文图扩展、证据约束引用和多粒度智能体细化提升可靠性，在自动综述生成中实现了最高的内容质量和引用准确性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: DeepSurvey从全文提取结构化要点，通过聚类和比较分析建模跨论文关系，集成代码仓库分析；结合引文图扩展与混合过滤进行主题检索，强制证据约束的引用分配，并采用多粒度智能体细化验证引用-声明一致性。

Result: DeepSurvey取得最高内容分数8.644/10，引用质量上召回率和精确率分别比最强基线提升12.3%和9.3%，跨领域性能下降更小（0.14 vs 0.22-0.69），领域专家偏好率83.3%整体质量、100%内容深度。

Conclusion: DeepSurvey在自动综述生成中显著提升了内容深度和引用可靠性，其表现优于现有系统甚至人工撰写，并具有良好的跨领域泛化能力。

中文摘要：随着科学文献的快速增长，自动化综述生成已成为AI科学家和人类研究者的关键能力。然而，现有系统存在分析深度有限的问题，这源于对摘要的依赖和孤立的论文处理，以及由于不精确的检索和后验引用导致的不可靠引用，从而产生肤浅的综述并可能误导研究者。我们提出了DeepSurvey，一个解决这两个问题的智能体系统。为了增强深度，DeepSurvey从全文论文中提取结构化要点，通过聚类和比较分析建模论文间关系，并集成代码仓库分析以恢复实现细节。为了加强可靠性，它结合引文图扩展与混合过滤进行主题聚焦检索，强制实施证据约束的引用分配，并部署多粒度智能体细化以验证引用与声明的一致性。实验表明，DeepSurvey取得了最高的内容分数（8.644/10）和引用质量（召回率和精确率分别比最强基线高出12.3%和9.3%），跨领域泛化更稳健（CS到非CS性能下降0.14，对比基线0.22至0.69），并且领域专家更倾向于选择它而非人工撰写的综述（整体质量83.3%，内容深度100%）。

Original abstract: As scientific literature grows rapidly, automated survey generation has become a key capability for AI scientists and human researchers. However, existing systems suffer from limited analytical depth due to reliance on abstracts and isolated paper processing, and unreliable citations from imprecise retrieval and post-hoc grounding, producing superficial surveys and may mislead researchers. We present DeepSurvey, an agentic system that addresses both. To enhance depth, DeepSurvey extracts structured keynotes from full-text papers, models cross-paper relationships through clustering and comparative analysis, and integrates code-repository analysis to recover implementation-level details. To fortify reliability, it combines citation-graph expansion with hybrid filtering for topic-focussed retrieval, enforces evidence-constrained citation assignment, and deploys multi-granularity agentic refinement to validate citation-claim alignment. Experiments show that DeepSurvey achieves the highest content score (8.644/10) and citation quality (12.3% and 9.3% recall and precision gains over the strongest baseline), generalizes more robustly across domains (0.14 vs 0.22 to 0.69 CS-to-non-CS drop), and is preferred over human-written surveys by domain experts (83.3% overall quality, 100% content depth).

### [35] [UI-KOBE: Knowledge-Oriented Behavior Exploration for Lightweight Graph-Guided GUI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29534v1)
*Yuxiang Chai,Han Xiao,Xinyu Fu,Jinpeng Chen,Rui Liu,Hongsheng Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 轻量级GUI agent框架，利用知识图谱指导规划，可迁移到代码agent的规划与知识复用。

TL;DR: UI-KOBE通过构建应用知识图谱指导轻量级移动GUI智能体，提升其任务执行能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有轻量级移动GUI智能体因模型容量有限，难以仅凭截图可靠地规划和执行端到端GUI任务。

Method: 提出UI-KOBE框架，先自主探索应用构建知识图谱（节点为UI状态，边为转换），运行时智能体根据当前截图识别节点并基于图选择动作。

Result: UI-KOBE减轻了端到端GUI规划负担，使轻量级模型更有效地执行移动GUI任务。

Conclusion: UI-KOBE为高效、可解释且隐私保护的设备端GUI智能体提供了实用方案。

中文摘要：移动GUI智能体的近期进展展示出自动化移动任务的强大潜力，但大多数有效系统仍依赖大型视觉语言模型进行截图理解和长期规划。可直接部署在移动设备上的小型GUI智能体在实际应用中更具吸引力，它们具有更低的推理成本和更好的敏感设备信息保护能力。然而，由于模型容量有限，这类轻量级智能体在仅凭截图进行端到端规划和执行GUI任务时仍然不可靠。我们提出了面向知识的行为探索框架（UI-KOBE），该框架通过可复用的应用特定图知识来改进轻量级移动GUI智能体。UI-KOBE首先自主探索移动应用并构建应用知识图谱，其中节点代表不同的UI状态，边代表可执行的状态转换。在运行时，轻量级GUI智能体将该图作为外部指导：给定用户任务和当前截图，它识别当前图节点，并选择与该节点相关的自循环动作、相邻转换、任务完成或回退自由动作。通过以应用特定的图指导支持运行时决策，UI-KOBE减轻了端到端GUI规划的负担，帮助轻量级模型更有效地执行移动GUI任务，为构建高效、可解释且保护隐私的设备端GUI智能体迈出了切实的一步。

Original abstract: Recent advances in mobile GUI agents have shown strong potential for automating mobile tasks, but most effective systems still depend on large vision-language models for screenshot understanding and long-horizon planning. Small GUI agents that can be deployed directly on mobile devices are more attractive for practical use, offering lower inference cost and better protection of sensitive on-device information. However, due to limited model capacity, such lightweight agents remain unreliable when planning and executing GUI tasks end-to-end from screenshots alone. We propose Knowledge-Oriented Behavior Exploration (\textbf{UI-KOBE}), a framework that improves lightweight mobile GUI agents with reusable app-specific graph knowledge. UI-KOBE first autonomously explores a mobile application and constructs an app knowledge graph, where nodes represent distinct UI states and edges represent executable transitions. At runtime, a lightweight GUI agent uses the graph as external guidance: given a user task and the current screenshot, it identifies the current graph node and selects among self-loop actions, neighboring transitions, task completion, or fallback free actions associated with that node. By supporting runtime decisions with app-specific graph guidance, UI-KOBE reduces the burden of end-to-end GUI planning and helps lightweight models perform mobile GUI tasks more effectively, offering a practical step toward efficient, interpretable, and privacy-conscious on-device GUI agents.

### [36] [Opt-Verifier: Unleashing the Power of LLMs for Optimization Modeling via Dual-Side Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29556v1)
*Haoyang Liu,Jie Wang,Boxuan Niu,Xiongwei Han,Yian Xu,Mingxuan Ye,Zijie Geng,Fangzhou Zhu,Tao Zhong,Mingxuan Yuan,Jianye Hao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM自动建模方法缺乏对生成模型的正确性验证，导致精度低。

Method: 提出双重验证框架，结构侧验证模型结构与问题描述一致，解侧验证解的合理性。

Result: 在流行基准上精度提升超过20%。

Conclusion: 双重验证显著提高自动建模的准确性，为LLM在运筹学中的应用提供了有效方案。

中文摘要：构建数学优化模型在运筹学中至关重要，但需要大量的人类专业知识。最近的进展利用大型语言模型（LLM）来自动化这一建模过程。然而，现有的工作往往难以验证生成的优化模型的正确性，没有检查约束条件和变量的合理性，也没有验证生成模型的解的有效性。这阻碍了后续的验证和修正步骤，从而严重损害了建模精度。为了解决这一挑战，我们提出了一种新颖的基于LLM的框架，具有从结构和解决方案两个角度进行双重验证（Opt-Verifier），从而提高建模精度。结构侧验证确保生成的优化模型的建模结构与原始问题描述一致，准确捕捉问题的约束条件和需求。同时，解侧验证解释和评估解的有效性，确认优化模型在逻辑和数学上是合理的。在流行基准上的实验表明，我们的方法在精度上实现了超过20%的提升。

Original abstract: Building mathematical optimization models is critical in operations research (OR), while it requires substantial human expertise. Recent advancements have utilized large language models (LLMs) to automate this modeling process. However, existing works often struggle to verify the correctness of the generated optimization models, without checking the rationality of the constraints and variables or the validity of solutions to the generated models. This hampers the subsequent verification and correction steps, and thus it severely hurts the modeling accuracy. To address this challenge, we propose a novel LLM-based framework with Dual-side Verification (Opt-Verifier) from both structure and solution perspectives, thereby improving the modeling accuracy. The structure-side verification ensures that the modeling structure of the generated optimization models aligns with the original problem description, accurately capturing the problem's constraints and requirements. Meanwhile, the solution-side verification interprets and evaluates the solutions' validity, confirming that the optimization models are logically and mathematically sound. Experiments on popular benchmarks demonstrate that our approach achieves over 20\% improvement in accuracy.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Original abstract: Parameterizing high-fidelity "digital twins" of batteries is a critical yet challenging inverse problem that hinders the pace of battery innovation. Prevailing methods formulate this as a black-box optimization (BBO) task, employing algorithms that are sample-inefficient and blind to the underlying physics. In this work, we introduce a new paradigm that reframes the inverse problem as a reasoning task, and present Battery-Sim-Agent, the first framework to deploy a Large Language Model (LLM) agent in a closed loop with a high-fidelity battery simulator. The agent mimics a human scientist's workflow: it interprets rich, multi-modal feedback from the simulator, forms physically-grounded hypotheses to explain discrepancies, and proposes structured parameter updates. On a systematically constructed benchmark suite spanning diverse battery chemistries, operating conditions, and difficulty levels, our agent significantly outperforms strong BBO baselines like Bayesian optimization in identifying accurate parameters. We further demonstrate the framework's capability in complex long-horizon degradation fitting tasks and validate its practical applicability on real-world battery datasets. Our results highlight the promise of LLM-agents as reasoning-based optimizers for scientific discovery and battery parameter estimation.

### [38] [ParaTool: Shifting Tool Representations from Context to Parameters](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29561v1)
*Zekai Yu,Qi Meng,Qizhi Chu,Yu Hao,Chuan Shi,Cheng Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ParaTool通过将每个工具参数化为独立模块，并动态集成，实现了无需上下文文档的工具调用，显著提升性能并降低计算复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具调用方法（如ICL和微调）存在推理开销大、幻觉风险高或无法内化工具细节等问题。

Method: 提出ParaTool框架，包含三个阶段：参数化工具预训练、软工具选择（门控网络动态聚合）和参数化工具微调。

Result: 在Stable ToolBench和BFCL上，ParaTool显著优于ICL基线，性能更优且计算复杂度更低。

Conclusion: ParaTool有效解决了工具调用中对上下文文档的依赖，提高了效率和可靠性。

中文摘要：工具调用通过使大型语言模型（LLMs）能够与外部可执行接口进行基于上下文的交互，从而扩展了它们的能力，支持与环境耦合的问题解决。然而，主流的上下文学习（ICL）方法通常将详细的工具文档和使用示例直接纳入上下文。这导致了随着上下文长度增长而产生的大量推理开销和更高的幻觉风险。相反，虽然基于微调的方法提高了通用的工具调用能力，但它们往往无法有效内化先前看到的工具的特定细节，从而仍然依赖于上下文文档。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了ParaTool，一个将每个工具投影到一组专用的、可加载的参数中的框架。通过配备这些参数化工具的动态集成，LLM可以在不依赖上下文文档或示例的情况下执行工具调用。具体来说，我们的方法包括三个阶段：（1）参数化工具预训练将不同工具的知识封装到独立的参数模块中；（2）软工具选择使用门控网络动态加权和聚合相关工具参数；以及（3）参数化工具微调联合更新工具参数以对齐训练和推理过程。在Stable ToolBench和BFCL上的实验表明，ParaTool显著优于强大的基于ICL的基线，在实现卓越性能的同时降低了计算复杂度。

Original abstract: Tool calling extends large language models (LLMs) by enabling grounded interaction with external executable interfaces, thereby supporting environment-coupled problem solving. However, mainstream in-context learning (ICL) approaches typically incorporate detailed tool documentation and usage examples directly into the context. This results in substantial inference overhead and heightened risks of hallucination as the context length grows. Conversely, while tuning-based methods improve general tool-calling capabilities, they often fail to effectively internalize the specific details of previously seen tools, thereby retaining a dependency on in-context documentation. To address these limitations, we propose ParaTool, a framework that projects each tool into a dedicated, loadable set of parameters. By equipping a dynamic integration of these parameterized tools, the LLM can perform tool calling without relying on in-context documents or examples. Specifically, our approach consists of three stages: (1) parametric tool pre-training encapsulates the knowledge of different tools into independent parameter modules; (2) soft tool selection employs a gating network to dynamically weigh and aggregate relevant tool parameters; and (3) parametric tool fine-tuning jointly updates tool parameters to align the training and inference processes. Experiments on Stable ToolBench and BFCL demonstrate that ParaTool significantly outperforms strong ICL-based baselines, achieving superior performance while reducing computational complexity.

### [39] [Planning with the Views](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29563v4)
*Kangrui Wang,Linjie Li,Zhengyuan Yang,Shiqi Chen,Zihan Wang,Li Fei-Fei,Jiajun Wu,Leonidas Guibas,Lijuan Wang,Manling Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: VLM视图规划框架，含自我探索与图蒸馏，通用规划方法可迁移到agent长程规划。

TL;DR: 提出ViewSuite基准发现VLM在多次视图规划中存在组合差距，通过自探索和视图图蒸馏框架将Qwen2.5-VL-7B性能从2.5%提升至47.8%，超越GPT-5.4 Pro和Gemini 3.1 Pro。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM在视图规划中存在关键差距：它们具备基本视图-动作知识，但无法在多次规划中组合这些知识，且随着视点距离增大差距扩大。

Method: 提出迭代框架，交替进行自探索和视图图蒸馏。自探索收集所有轨迹（无论结果）形成视图图，蒸馏该图产生多样化监督任务，重塑策略分布并克服稀疏奖励。

Result: Qwen2.5-VL-7B在交互式视图规划上从2.5%提升至47.8%，超过GPT-5.4 Pro（18.5%）和Gemini 3.1 Pro（21.4%）。

Conclusion: 自探索是使VLM在3D空间中主动推理和规划的有前途路径。

中文摘要：VLMs能否预测每个摄像机运动如何改变视角，并提前规划多个这样的运动？我们将这种能力称为视图规划，需要(1)理解单个动作如何改变视图，以及(2)在多次规划中组合许多这样的变换以识别目标视图。我们在我们提出的ViewSuite中探测这两种能力，ViewSuite是一个基于真实ScanNet场景的3D点云环境。在13个前沿VLM中，出现了一个关键的规划差距：它们具备基本的视图-动作知识，但无法在多次规划中组合这些知识，且随着视点距离增大，差距扩大。为了缩小这一差距，我们提出了一种迭代框架，该框架交替进行自探索和视图图蒸馏。关键洞察是，所有探索轨迹（无论其结果如何）共同形成一个视图图，该图紧凑地捕捉了场景中视点如何连接。将这个图蒸馏成多样化的监督任务重塑了策略分布，并克服了纯RL停滞的稀疏奖励问题。这使Qwen2.5-VL-7B在交互式视图规划上从2.5%提升到47.8%，超过了GPT-5.4 Pro（18.5%）和Gemini 3.1 Pro（21.4%）。自探索成为使VLM能够在3D空间中主动推理和规划的一条有前途的路径。代码和数据见https://viewsuite.github.io。

Original abstract: Can VLMs predict how each camera move changes the view, and plan many such moves ahead? We call this capability view planning, requiring (1)understanding how a single action transforms the view, and (2)composing many such transformations across multi-turn plans to identify a target view. We probe both abilities in our proposed ViewSuite, a 3D point-cloud environment on real ScanNet scenes. Across 13 frontier VLMs, a critical planning gap emerges: they possess basic view-action knowledge but fail to compose it across multi-turn plans, with the gap widening as viewpoint distance grows. To close this gap, we propose an iterative framework that alternates self-exploration with view graph distillation. The key insight is that all exploration trajectories, regardless of their outcome, collectively form a view graph that compactly captures how viewpoints connect across a scene. Distilling this graph into diverse supervised tasks reshapes the policy distribution and overcomes the sparse rewards that stall pure RL. This improves Qwen2.5-VL-7B from 2.5% to 47.8% on interactive view planning, surpassing GPT-5.4 Pro (18.5%) and Gemini 3.1 Pro (21.4%). Self-exploration emerges as a promising path toward VLMs that can actively reason and plan in 3D space. Code and Data are at https://viewsuite.github.io.

</details>


### [40] [DeepTool: Scaling Interleaved Deliberation in Tool-Integrated Reasoning via Process-Supervised Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29568v1)
*Yang He,Xiao Ding,Bibo Cai,Yufei Zhang,Kai Xiong,Zhouhao Sun,Bing Qin,Ting Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具集成推理方法缺乏对顺序工具调用过程中的深思熟虑和中间步骤的监督，导致性能受限。

Result: 在六个基准上显著提升Qwen2.5-7B性能，如AIME24从3.2%升至40.4%，HMMT25从0.0%升至28.6%。

Conclusion: DeepTool实现了性能与令牌效率的最佳平衡，验证了交错思考的有效性。

中文摘要：工具集成推理通过利用外部环境扩展了大型语言模型的能力。然而，现有方法在顺序工具调用过程中缺乏深思熟虑，而这对于战略规划和自我纠正是必需的。虽然强化学习缓解了这一问题，但传统的工具集成推理方法受到稀疏的基于结果的奖励的阻碍，无法监督中间推理步骤和工具调用。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了DeepTool，一种新的框架，它在每个回合的思考、行动和观察的交错过程中扩展了深思熟虑的思考。在DeepTool中，我们首先引入一个合成流水线，将扩展的思考演变为交错的轨迹，结合对抗性扰动以确保鲁棒性和自我纠正。其次，我们设计了基于GRPO的过程监督强化学习，该方法利用以行动为中心的过程奖励来加强中间交错的思考，并在每个回合强制执行精确的工具调用。大量实验表明，DeepTool取得了优越的性能，在六个基准测试上显著提升了Qwen2.5-7B（例如，AIME24：3.2% → 40.4%，HMMT25：0.0% → 28.6%）。此外，令牌成本效益分析证实了交错思考的效用，展示了DeepTool在性能和令牌效率之间的最佳平衡。

Original abstract: Tool-Integrated Reasoning (TIR) extends LLM capabilities by leveraging external environments. However, existing methods lack the deliberation during sequential tool invocation required for strategic planning and self-correction. While RL mitigates this, conventional approaches for Tool-Integrated Reasoning are hindered by sparse outcome-based rewards, failing to supervise intermediate reasoning steps and tool invocations. To address this, we propose DeepTool, a novel framework that scales deliberate thinking within the interleaved process of thinking, action, and observation at each turn. In DeepTool, we first introduce a synthesis pipeline that evolves extended thinking into interleaved trajectories, integrating adversarial perturbations to ensure robustness and self-correction. Secondly, we devise Process-Supervised Reinforcement Learning based on GRPO, which utilizes an Action-Centric Process Reward to reinforce intermediate interleaved thinking and enforce precise tool invocation at every turn. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DeepTool achieves superior performance, boosting Qwen2.5-7B significantly across six benchmarks (e.g., AIME24: 3.2% -> 40.4% and HMMT25: 0.0% -> 28.6%). Furthermore, the token cost-effectiveness analysis confirms the utility of interleaved thinking, demonstrating DeepTool's optimal balance between performance and token efficiency.

</details>

中文摘要：共创（即AI代理与人类交互以生成输出，例如艺术）这一话题近期获得了显著关注。然而，大多数研究聚焦于数字环境中的成人-人类交互。本文探索了一种新颖的游乐式共创场景，涉及儿童与大型语言模型通过实体棋盘游戏交互来创作书面故事。我们的目标是开发一个多智能体框架，能够生成适合年轻玩家的高质量叙事。我们方法的核心是一个迭代的作家-编辑过程，其中一个LLM生成故事，而另一个评估故事并提供改进反馈。通过一项涉及多个LLM的模拟研究，我们表明这种迭代交互在连续循环中持续提高了生成故事的感知质量。结果表明，在交互式故事讲述系统中，少量的改进步骤可能足以实现高质量的输出。

Original abstract: The topic of Co-creation, i.e., AI agents interacting with humans to generate outputs (e.g., art), has gained significant attention recently. ### [42] [Beyond Attack Success Rate: Temporal Logit Observability for LLM Safety Failures](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29629v1)
*Junyoung Park,Sunghwan Park,Seongyong Ju,Jaewoo Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM安全失败的时间诊断方法，可迁移至agent安全性评估与监控。

TL;DR: 提出时间logits可观测性（TLO）方法，通过监控解码时的服从-拒绝边际，将模型-攻击条件映射到二维平面，揭示相同ASR下攻击路径的差异，并导出早期停止规则有效减少越狱成功。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ASR无法区分导致相同有害输出的不同攻击路径，需要一种更细致的诊断方法来揭示失败的时间模式。

Method: TLO是一种训练-free诊断，通过监控解码过程中的服从-拒绝边际，将每个模型-攻击条件放置在经过校准的二维平面上。

Result: 在四个LLM和三种越狱范式下，TLO能区分具有相同ASR的攻击；基于TLO的早期停止规则将成功越狱削减超过一半，且无误报。

Conclusion: 安全评估应报告失败何时及如何展开，TLO使得从logits中观察这些信息成为可能。

中文摘要：攻击成功率（ASR）在生成结束时使用单个是/否标签评估每次越狱，告诉我们是否发生了失败，但没有说明失败是如何展开的。两种产生同等有害输出的攻击可能遵循完全不同的路径，而ASR无法区分它们。我们仅从logits中使这些隐藏路径变得可观察。时间logits可观测性（TLO）是一种无需训练的诊断方法，它监控解码过程中的服从-拒绝边际，并将每个模型-攻击条件放置在校准的二维平面上。通过设计，这个平面在ASR信息量最低的地方信息量最大：在那些因真正不同原因而成功的攻击中。在四个对齐LLM和三种越狱范式中，具有几乎相同ASR的攻击在平面上的点明显不同：同一模型可以通过不同的时间模式失败。在大多数条件下，几何形状与来自隐藏状态的拒绝方向探针对齐，一个模型展示了我们固定词汇方法的局限性。从TLO导出的简单早期停止规则将成功的越狱削减了一半以上，并且在普通良性查询上没有误报。安全评估应该报告失败何时以及如何展开，而不仅仅是是否发生。TLO使得前两个信息仅从logits中可观察。

Original abstract: Attack Success Rate (ASR) evaluates each jailbreak with a single yes/no label at the end of generation, telling us whether a failure happened but not how it unfolded. Two attacks that produce equally harmful outputs may have followed completely different paths, and ASR cannot tell them apart. We make those hidden paths observable from logits alone. Temporal Logit Observability (TLO) is a training-free diagnostic that watches a compliance-refusal margin during decoding and places each model-attack condition on a calibrated 2D plane. By design, this plane is most informative exactly where ASR is least informative: among attacks that succeed for genuinely different reasons. Across four aligned LLMs and three jailbreak paradigms, attacks with nearly identical ASR land at clearly different points on the plane: the same model can fail through different temporal patterns. The geometry matches refusal-direction probes from hidden states on most conditions, with one model showing the limit of our fixed-lexicon approach. A simple early-stop rule derived from TLO cuts successful jailbreaks by more than half, without false alarms on plain benign queries. Safety evaluation should report when and how a failure unfolds, not only whether it occurred. TLO makes the first two observable from logits alone.

</details>


### [43] [VikingMem: A Memory Base Management System for Stateful LLM-based Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29640v3)
*Jiajie Fu,Junwen Chen,Mengzhao Wang,Aoxiang He,Maojia Sheng,Xiangyu Ke,Yifan Zhu,Yunjun Gao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM应用的内存管理系统，涉及agent记忆管理与状态演化，对coding agent长程任务有启发。

TL;DR: 提出Memory Base范式和VikingMem系统，通过选择性提取、有状态演进和通用抽象，在长期记忆检索上提升30%效果并保持低延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆方法缺乏通用性，难以处理多样化下游任务，且依赖单一用例的提取提示。

Method: 提出Memory Base范式，包括选择性提取、有状态演进和通用抽象；实现VikingMem系统，采用事件和实体抽象、事件中心提取、基于主题时间线的时间压缩和时间加权召回。

Result: 在长期记忆基准上，VikingMem在记忆检索有效性上比基线提高30%，同时保持低延迟。

Conclusion: VikingMem有效解决了长期交互中的记忆管理挑战，具有通用性和高性能。

中文摘要：大型语言模型已经彻底改变了交互式应用；然而，它们的有限上下文窗口对维护有状态、长期交互构成了关键的数据管理挑战。现有的记忆方法通常依赖于简单的提取方法，导致记忆不完整，或者使用针对单一用例（如聊天机器人）的僵化、单一用途的记忆提取提示。因此，它们缺乏通用性，并且在多样化的下游任务中表现不佳。为弥补这一差距，我们引入了Memory Base，一种用于管理长期交互持久状态的新型数据管理范式。它的特点是三个核心原则：从原始信息流中选择性提取高价值记忆；固有的有状态性和演进，其中记忆内容被逐步总结、纠正和时间加权以优先考虑最近的交互；以及一种通用的抽象范式，旨在跨不同应用（包括教育、推荐和智能体记忆）实现稳健的可迁移性。在此基础上，我们提出了VikingMem，一个基于VikingDB向量引擎的端到端记忆库管理系统。VikingMem通过相互关联的事件和实体抽象来实现这一范式。它采用以事件为中心的记忆提取来选择性处理复杂的信息流，而实体则由事件动态更新以实现有状态的演进。通过基于主题时间线的时间压缩和时间加权召回，系统逐步产生高级摘要记忆，优先考虑最近的项目，并压缩和淡出较旧的项目。在长期记忆基准上的广泛评估表明，VikingMem在记忆检索有效性上比基线提高了30%，同时保持了交互式应用所需的低延迟。

Original abstract: Large Language Models have revolutionized interactive applications; however, their finite context windows pose a critical data management challenge for maintaining stateful, long-term interactions. Existing memory approaches often rely on simplistic extraction methods that lead to incomplete memories or use rigid, single-purpose memory extraction prompts tailored to a single use case, such as chatbots. Consequently, they lack generalizability and perform poorly across diverse downstream tasks. To bridge this gap, we introduce the Memory Base, a novel data management paradigm for managing the persistent state of long-term interactions. It is characterized by three core principles: selective extraction of high-value memories from raw information streams; inherent statefulness and evolution, where memory content is progressively summarized, corrected, and temporally weighted to prioritize recent interactions; and a generalizable abstraction paradigm designed for robust transferability across diverse applications, including education, recommendation, and agent memory. Building on this foundation, we present VikingMem, an end-to-end Memory Base Management System implemented on the VikingDB vector engine. VikingMem materializes this paradigm through interconnected event and entity abstractions. It features event-centric memory extraction to selectively handle complex information streams, while entities are dynamically updated by events to achieve stateful evolution. Using temporal compression via a topic-wise timeline and time-weighted recall, the system progressively produces high-level summary memories, prioritizes recent items, and compresses and fades older ones. Extensive evaluations on long-term memory benchmarks demonstrate that VikingMem outperformes baselines by up to 30% in memory retrieval effectiveness while maintaining the low latency essential for interactive applications.

### [44] [LLM-Evolved Domain-Independent Heuristics for Symbolic AI Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29649v2)
*Elliot Gestrin,Jendrik Seipp*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM进化启发式用于AI规划，涉及演化搜索与领域无关启发式，可迁移至自动代码优化中的启发式搜索。

TL;DR: 本文首次使用进化搜索和LLM生成领域无关的启发式算法，超越了人工设计的最高水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM可以为特定领域设计启发式算法，但尚无LLM生成的启发式算法能适用于任意规划任务，且人工设计启发式算法耗时费力。

Method: 使用LLM对C++编写的父启发式算法进行变异，通过MAP-Elites档案存储候选并评估适应度（结合覆盖率和求解时间），从盲启发式或FF启发式初始化，进行进化搜索。

Result: 最好的进化启发式在未见过的测试领域上解决的任务数超过最强基线，整个套件覆盖帕累托前沿；从盲启发式初始化优于从FF初始化；LLM推理努力影响编译成功率而非质量。

Conclusion: 该方法生成了可直接替换现有规划器的纯C++启发式算法，保证了搜索的正确性和完备性。

中文摘要：启发式搜索是符号化AI规划中的主导范式，最强的启发式算法是规划研究者数十年来工作的成果。最近的研究表明，大型语言模型（LLM）可以为各个规划领域设计启发式算法，但迄今为止，没有LLM生成的启发式算法能在任意规划任务上工作。在本文中，我们使用进化搜索来生成首个LLM生成的、超越人工设计最先进水平的领域无关启发式算法。我们让LLM对用C++编写的父启发式算法进行变异，将候选算法存储在以信息量和速度为键的MAP-Elites档案中，并通过结合覆盖率和求解时间计算适应度分数。为了将进化出的程序置于背景中，我们额外对一系列人工设计的启发式算法在其信息量-速度权衡上进行基准测试，据我们所知，这之前从未做过。在未见过的测试领域上，我们最好的进化启发式算法甚至比最强的基线解决了更多任务，我们的完整启发式套件覆盖了该权衡的帕累托前沿。我们还发现，从简单的盲启发式算法开始进化比从强大的FF启发式算法开始进化效果更好，即使最终程序本身是FF的变体；并且LLM的推理努力程度影响候选程序编译成功的频率远大于影响那些编译成功的程序的质量。由于进化出的程序是纯C++，它们可以作为即插即用的替代品插入现有规划器，并继承底层搜索的完备性和正确性保证。

Original abstract: Heuristic search is the dominant paradigm in symbolic AI planning, and the strongest heuristics are the result of decades of work by planning researchers. Recent work has shown that large language models (LLMs) can design heuristics for individual planning domains, but no LLM-generated heuristic has so far worked on arbitrary planning tasks. In this paper, we use evolutionary search to produce the first LLM-generated domain-independent heuristics that exceed the hand-engineered state of the art. We let an LLM mutate parent heuristics written in C++, store candidates in a MAP-Elites archive keyed on informedness and speed and calculate fitness scores by blending coverage with solving time. To place the evolved programs in context, we additionally benchmark a broad set of hand-engineered heuristics on their informedness-speed tradeoff, which to our knowledge has not been done before. On unseen testing domains, our best evolved heuristic solves more tasks than even the strongest baseline, with our full heuristic suite spanning the Pareto frontier of said tradeoff. We also find that seeding evolution from the trivial blind heuristic outperforms seeding from the strong FF heuristic, even when the resulting program is itself an FF variant, and that LLM reasoning effort affects how often candidates compile much more than the quality of those that do. Because the evolved programs are plain C++, they slot into existing planners as drop-in replacements and inherit the soundness and completeness guarantees of the underlying search.

### [45] [PTCG-Bench: Can LLM Agents Master Pokémon Trading Card Game?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29653v1)
*Dongdong Hua,Yifei Sun,Renhong Huang,Feng Gao,Chunping Wang,Yang Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent在复杂策略游戏中的基准，涉及agent评估与自我进化，对coding agent长程任务评测有参考。

TL;DR: 提出PTCG-Bench基准，评估LLM在复杂游戏中的决策和自我进化能力，发现自我进化困难且对框架敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体基准未能充分捕捉战略性和不断演变的决策场景，需要更好的基准来评估自主智能体。

Method: 构建基于宝可梦集换式卡牌游戏的PTCG-Bench基准，包含两个评估层面（单环境决策和自我进化），并加入模块化框架消融实验。

Result: LLM智能体能够实现非平凡的游戏表现，但持续稳定的自我进化仍具挑战性，且表现对框架设计敏感。

Conclusion: PTCG-Bench将促进未来对框架感知和自我进化智能体的研究。

中文摘要：面对一个策略复杂的棋盘游戏，人类玩家可以在几轮游戏后快速学会制定策略。自主智能体在现实交互环境中也需要类似的能力，然而现有的智能体基准测试往往未能充分捕捉这种战略性和不断演变的决策场景。我们提出了PTCG-Bench，这是一个基于宝可梦集换式卡牌游戏（PTCG）的基准测试，它在两个互补层面评估LLM智能体：（1）它们在单一复杂环境中的决策表现，（2）它们通过积累经验进行自我进化的能力。我们还加入了一个模块化框架消融实验，以更好地解释智能体表现，而不将其与模型能力混淆。我们的实验表明，尽管LLM智能体能够实现非平凡的游戏表现，但持续稳定的自我进化仍然具有挑战性，并且表现对框架设计敏感。我们希望PTCG-Bench能促进未来在现实交互环境中对框架感知和自我进化智能体的研究。

Original abstract: Given a strategically complex board game, human players can quickly learn to devise strategies after playing a few rounds. Autonomous agents require similar capabilities in realistic interactive environments, yet existing agent benchmarks often fail to fully capture such strategic and evolving decision-making scenarios. We present PTCG-Bench, a benchmark built on the Pok'{e}mon Trading Card Game (PTCG) that evaluates LLM agents at two complementary levels: (1) their decision-making performance within a single complex environment, and (2) their ability to self-evolving through accumulated experience. We further include a modular harness ablation to better interpret agent performance without conflating it with model capability. Our experiments show that, although LLM agents can achieve non-trivial gameplay performance, sustained and stable self-evolution remains challenging, and performance is sensitive to harness design. We hope that PTCG-Bench will facilitate future research on harness-aware and self-evolving agents in realistic interactive environments.

### [46] [TRACE: Toulmin-based Reasoning Assessment through Constructive Elements for LLM CoT Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29656v1)
*Yundong Kim,Heyoung Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: CoT推理过程评估方法，可用于agent推理质量监控，但相关性较弱。

TL;DR: 提出TRACE指标，通过整合图尔敏论证理论和弗拉维尔元认知框架分析思维链推理过程，实验显示与基准准确性强相关，并可作为有效的强化学习奖励信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估LLM开放式输出指标忽略推理过程，仅关注结果准确性或表面统计，需要评估推理结构。

Method: 提出TRACE指标，结合图尔敏论证理论和弗拉维尔元认知框架，分析CoT推理过程中论点的构建。

Result: 在26.3K QA样本上，TRACE与基准准确性相关系数r=0.74；作为RL奖励信号优于仅准确性的基线。

Conclusion: 逻辑合理的推理导致更高质量的答案，TRACE可作为评估开放式输出的补充指标。

中文摘要：评估大型语言模型（LLMs）的开放式输出仍然具有挑战性，因为缺乏真实答案。现有指标依赖于最终答案的准确性或表面统计量，而忽略了推理过程本身。我们引入了TRACE（基于图尔敏论证模型的结构性推理评估），一种分析思维链（CoT）推理过程的指标。TRACE不是判断结果，而是通过整合图尔敏的论证理论和弗拉维尔的元认知框架来检查论点是如何构建的，以评估推理结构。在7个推理模型的26.3K QA样本上的实验显示，与基准准确性的强相关性（r=0.74）。此外，TRACE作为强化学习奖励信号有效，优于仅依赖准确性的基线。这些结果共同表明，逻辑合理的推理会导致更高质量的答案。因此，TRACE作为评估开放式输出的补充指标。代码可在https://github.com/hyyangkisti/trace获取。

Original abstract: Evaluating open-ended outputs from large language models (LLMs) remains challenging due to the absence of ground truth. Existing metrics rely on final-answer accuracy or surface-level statistics, leaving the reasoning process itself unexamined. We introduce TRACE (Toulmin-based Reasoning Assessment through Constructive Elements), a metric that analyzes Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning processes. Rather than judging outcomes, TRACE inspects how arguments are constructed by integrating Toulmin's argumentation theory with Flavell's metacognitive framework to assess reasoning structure. Experiments on 26.3K QA samples across 7 reasoning models show strong correlation with benchmark accuracy (r=0.74). Furthermore, TRACE is effective as a reinforcement learning reward signal, outperforming accuracy-only baselines. Together, these results indicate that logically sound reasoning leads to higher-quality answers. TRACE thus serves as a complementary metric for evaluating open-ended outputs. Code is available at https://github.com/hyyangkisti/trace.

</details>


### [47] [GRASP: Gated Regression-Aware Skill Proposer for Self-Improving LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29668v1)
*Johannes Moll,Jean-Philippe Corbeil,Jiazhen Pan,Martin Hadamitzky,Daniel Rueckert,Lisa Adams,Keno Bressem*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 通用自改进agent方法，通过技能库编辑防止回归，可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: GRASP通过带门控和回归预算的技能库编辑，显著提升了LLM代理在结构化环境中的可靠性，并跨模型和领域泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我改进方法在累积自然语言指导时未检查保留先前正确行为，导致修复一个轨迹可能破坏另一个。

Method: GRASP将代理改进视为对有限技能库的序列编辑，每个候选技能只有在硬回归预算下在平衡保留集上产生净改进时才被接受。

Result: 在MedAgentBench上，GRASP将gpt-oss-120b从40.6%提升至88.8%，超过最强基线21.0点，并改善其他模型17.2-40.3点；消融实验表明增益来自比较提议生成、接受门和回归预算。

Conclusion: GRASP通过谨慎的技能接纳机制有效防止回归，并具备跨领域和跨模型迁移能力，且更强模型技能可提升弱模型而反之不成立。

中文摘要：在结构化环境中运行的LLM代理以操作而非对话的方式失败，其可靠性依赖于环境的程序性知识。先前的自我改进方法积累自然语言指导，但不检查每个新项是否保留了先前正确的行为，因此修复一条轨迹的笔记可能会静默地回归另一条。我们引入了GRASP（门控回归感知技能提议器），它将代理改进视为对有限技能库的一系列编辑，只有在硬回归预算下在平衡的保留探针上产生净改进时，才接纳每个候选技能。我们在两个基于FHIR的临床基准上评估了GRASP在五个基础模型（gpt-oss-120b、DeepSeek V4 Flash、Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite、GPT-4.1、GPT-5.4）上的表现。在MedAgentBench上，GRASP将gpt-oss-120b从40.6%提升到88.8%，比五个自我改进基线中最强的高出21.0个百分点，并将其他每个基础模型提高了17.2到40.3个百分点。消融实验将增益归因于比较性提议生成、接受门和硬回归预算，而非技能编写本身，因为未经验证的技能编写不比不使用技能更好。该机制泛化到临床领域之外，在四个非临床环境中的三个上改进了代理，仅在动作空间开放式的环境中保持持平。冻结的技能库可以跨模型转移，其中来自更强模型的技能改进较弱的执行者超出了它们自身学习的效果，而反过来则不行，这种不对称性是任何无门控基线都无法复现的。

Original abstract: LLM agents acting in structured environments fail in operational rather than conversational ways, and reliability depends on procedural knowledge of the environment. Prior self-improvement methods accumulate natural-language guidance without checking that each new item preserves previously correct behavior, so a note that fixes one trajectory can silently regress another. We introduce GRASP (Gated Regression-Aware Skill Proposer), which treats agent improvement as a sequence of edits to a bounded skill library, admitting each candidate only if it produces a net improvement on a balanced held-out probe under a hard regression budget. We evaluate GRASP across five base models (gpt-oss-120b, DeepSeek V4 Flash, Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite, GPT-4.1, GPT-5.4) on two FHIR-based clinical benchmarks. On MedAgentBench, GRASP lifts gpt-oss-120b from 40.6% to 88.8%, exceeds the strongest of five self-improvement baselines by 21.0 points, and improves every other base model by 17.2 to 40.3 points. Ablations attribute the gain to comparative proposal generation, the acceptance gate, and the hard regression budget rather than to skill writing itself, which without validation is no better than using no skills. The mechanism generalizes beyond the clinical domain, improving agents on three of four non-clinical environments and remaining flat only where the action space is open-ended. Frozen libraries transfer across models, where skills from a stronger model improve weaker executors beyond what they learn for themselves while the reverse does not, an asymmetry that no ungated baseline reproduces.

### [48] [Notation Matters: A Benchmark Study of Token-Optimized Formats in Agentic AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29676v2)
*Lorenz Kutschka,Bernhard Geiger*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 优化agent系统中结构化数据表示法，减少token开销，直接提升agent效率。

TL;DR: 评估TOON和TRON两种令牌优化格式在端到端Agentic系统中的表现，TRON减令牌27%且准确率下降少于14个百分点，TOON减18%但有多轮解析和并行调用问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JSON在Agentic AI系统中令牌效率低，需要更紧凑的替代格式，但现有评估局限于孤立任务，未在端到端循环中验证。

Method: 在四个代理基准和五个开源LLM上，将输入和输出压缩解耦，独立评估TOON和TRON的理解与生成性能。

Result: TRON最多减令牌27%，准确率下降≤14pp；TOON最多减18%，准确率下降9pp，但多轮解析失败且并行调用输出崩溃。

Conclusion: TRON是可行的JSON替代方案，TOON有局限，需进一步优化处理多轮和并行场景。

中文摘要：在Agentic AI系统中，大型语言模型消耗工具模式和执行结果，并发出作为结构化数据的工具调用。这种交换的默认语言JSON是为应用程序间交换而设计的，而不是为了令牌效率，因此其结构元素带来了大量的令牌开销。最近的工作提出了令牌优化的替代方案，如TOON（面向令牌的对象表示法）和TRON（令牌精简对象表示法），作为更紧凑的替代方案，但这些格式仅在孤立的理解或生成任务上进行了评估。因此，它们的令牌减少在端到端代理循环中是否成立仍然是一个悬而未决的问题。我们在四个代理基准（BFCL、MCPToolBenchPP、MCP-Universe、StableToolBench）和五个开放权重的LLM上评估了TOON和TRON，将输入压缩与输出压缩解耦，以独立测量理解和生成。TRON将令牌减少高达27%，准确率在JSON基线的14个百分点以内。TOON实现了高达18%的减少，类似地牺牲了9个百分点的准确率，但在多轮解析失败上进一步级联，并且对大多数模型使并行工具调用输出崩溃。代码可在https://github.com/lkutschka/notation-matters获取。

Original abstract: Large language models in Agentic AI systems consume tool schemas and execution results and emit tool invocations as structured data. The default language for that exchange, JSON, was designed for application-to-application interchange rather than token efficiency, so its structural elements impose substantial token overhead. Recent work proposes token-optimized alternatives such as TOON (Token-Oriented Object Notation) and TRON (Token Reduced Object Notation) as more compact replacements, but these formats have been evaluated only on isolated comprehension or generation tasks. Whether their token reductions hold inside end-to-end agentic loops therefore remains an open question. We evaluate TOON and TRON on four agentic benchmarks (BFCL, MCPToolBenchPP, MCP-Universe, StableToolBench) and five open-weight LLMs, decoupling input compression from output compression to measure comprehension and generation independently. TRON reduces tokens by up to 27% with accuracy within 14pp of the JSON baseline. TOON achieves up to 18% reduction at a similar 9pp accuracy cost, but additionally cascades on multi-turn parsing failures and collapses parallel tool-call output for most models. The code is available at: https://github.com/lkutschka/notation-matters

</details>


### [49] [Reliable Reasoning with Large Language Models via Preference-Based Maximum Satisfiability](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29687v1)
*Pedro Orvalho,Marta Kwiatkowska,Guillem Alenyà,Felip Manyà*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM+MaxSAT混合推理，代码生成与约束求解，可迁移至agent规划与验证。

TL;DR: 提出LLM生成代码编码偏好MaxSAT问题并由精确求解器求解的混合推理方法，在偏好推理任务上显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在处理多约束和用户定义偏好的优化任务时表现不佳，而这类任务在机器人等领域很常见。

Method: LLM生成Python代码，将自然语言问题编码为偏好MaxSAT问题，由精确MaxSAT求解器求解，并通过独立验证确保正确性。

Result: 该方法在多个偏好推理任务上实现超过80%的接受率，显著高于直接回答、思维链等基线。

Conclusion: LLM驱动的代码生成结合偏好MaxSAT可实现求解器可验证的优化，并在独立参考语义下大幅提升正确性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）擅长理解自然语言，但在涉及多个约束和用户定义偏好的优化任务中表现不佳，这些任务在机器人等领域很常见。我们提出了一种混合推理方法，其中LLM通过代码生成将推理外部化。给定自然语言问题描述，LLM生成Python代码，将用户定义的约束和偏好编码为基于偏好的最大可满足性（MaxSAT）问题，然后由精确的MaxSAT求解器求解。为确保正确性，模型生成的代码返回的解决方案会针对规范MaxSAT编码独立验证其可行性和最优性，从而允许不同的编码和多个最优解。我们使用开源和闭源LLM在三类基于偏好的推理任务上评估了我们的方法，并将其与使用相同模型的直接回答、思维链和程序思维基线进行比较。虽然这些基线很少产生可行解，但基于MaxSAT的流水线实现了显著更高的接受率，在某些情况下超过80%。我们的结果表明，LLM驱动的代码生成与基于偏好的MaxSAT相结合，能够针对生成的编码实现求解器可验证的优化，并在独立验证的参考语义下显著提高正确性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) excel at understanding natural language but struggle with optimisation tasks involving multiple constraints and user-defined preferences, which commonly arise in domains such as robotics. We propose a hybrid reasoning approach in which LLMs externalise reasoning through code generation. Given a natural language problem description, an LLM generates Python code that encodes user-defined constraints and preferences as a preference-based Maximum Satisfiability (MaxSAT) problem, which is then solved by an exact MaxSAT solver. To ensure correctness, solutions returned by the model-generated code are independently verified for feasibility and optimality against a canonical MaxSAT encoding, allowing for different encodings and multiple optimal solutions. We evaluate our approach using both open-source and closed-access LLMs on three families of preference-based reasoning tasks, and compare it against direct-answer, chain-of-thought, and program-of-thought baselines using the same models. While these baselines rarely produce feasible solutions, the MaxSAT-based pipeline achieves substantially higher acceptance rates, in some cases exceeding 80%. Our results demonstrate that LLM-driven code generation combined with preference-based MaxSAT enables solver-verifiable optimisation with respect to generated encodings, and substantially improves correctness under independently verified reference semantics.

</details>


### [50] [Beyond Trajectory Rewards: Step-level Credit Assignment for Agentic Search via Graph Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29697v1)
*Yuchen Liu,Yingjie Feng,Lixiong Qin,Jiasi Chen,Jianing Yu,Sheng Gao,Sheng Yang,Weiran Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 步骤级过程奖励方法，用于agentic search，可迁移至coding agent's credit assignment。

TL;DR: 提出基于图距离的步骤级奖励GDCR和步骤优势策略优化SAPO，有效提升智能体搜索性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有轨迹级奖励无法量化步骤贡献，步骤级奖励依赖昂贵树采样，需要更高效的方法。

Method: 将世界知识视为潜在图，定义GDCR奖励基于实体到答案节点的图距离，并提出SAPO将步骤优势与轨迹优势结合。

Result: 在四个基准测试上验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: GDCR和SAPO能有效提升智能体搜索的步骤级奖励效率，验证了基于图先验的合理性。

中文摘要：在智能体搜索中，轨迹级别的结果奖励无法量化单个步骤的行为贡献，而现有的步骤级奖励方法通常依赖于昂贵的树采样。我们将世界知识视为潜在的世界图，每个信息搜索任务视为潜在任务图中的搜索，其中有效的步骤应使图朝着答案节点前进。基于这一先验，我们提出图距离贡献奖励（GDCR），这是一种步骤级过程奖励，根据训练时实体关系图中新检索和新引用实体到答案节点的距离对其进行评分。我们进一步提出步骤优势策略优化（SAPO），它将GDCR转化为步骤级优势，并与轨迹级结果优势相结合。在四个具有挑战性的基准测试上的实验验证了我们方法的有效性。

Original abstract: In Agentic Search, trajectory-level outcome rewards fail to quantify the behavioral contributions of individual steps, while existing step-level reward methods typically rely on costly tree sampling. We view world knowledge as a latent world graph and each IS task as search within a latent task graph, where effective steps should make graph progress toward the answer node. Based on this prior, we propose Graph-Distance Contribution Reward (GDCR), a step-level process reward that scores newly-retrieved and newly-cited entities by their distance to the answer node in a training-time Entity-Relation (ER) graph. We further propose Step Advantage Policy Optimization (SAPO), which converts GDCR into step-level advantages and combines them with trajectory-level outcome advantages. Experiments on four challenging benchmarks validate the effectiveness of our method.

Original abstract: The impressive performance of generalist large language models (LLMs) such as GPT and Claude in healthcare raises a critical question: will domain-specific medical specialist models become obsolete? We propose HetMedAgent, a heterogeneous medical multi-agent framework that enables conflict-aware evidence fusion, uncertainty-based clinician intervention triggering, and adaptive threshold calibration. Experiments on three real-world clinical decision-making tasks demonstrate that the synergy between generalist LLMs and domain-specific specialist models significantly outperforms using either type of model alone, validating the irreplaceable value of specialist models in modality-specific analysis. HetMedAgent represents a shift from building medical LLMs or foundation models to multi-agent collaboration, achieving a balance between general reasoning capabilities and domain-specific precision.

### [52] [Croissant Tasks: A Metadata Format for Reproducible Machine Learning Evaluations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29786v1)
*Omar Benjelloun,Leonardo Martins Bianco,Isabelle Guyon,Thanh Gia Hieu Khuong,Jonathan Lebensold,Sebastian Lobentanzer,Luis Oala,Benedictus Kent Rachmat,Ihsan Ullah,Peyman Vahidi,Joaquin Vanschoren*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 可重现ML评估元数据格式，支持agent自动化评估

TL;DR: 提出Croissant Tasks元数据格式，将任务实现细节抽象为高层规范，通过LLM自动化改编现有基准，让自主智能体生成可复现流水线，实现概念可复现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习可复现性差，现有方法依赖人工且难以扩展，需要自动化、概念层面的可复现方案。

Method: 设计Croissant Tasks规范解耦任务与实现；开发LLM流水线自动将现有基准转换为该格式；评估自主智能体基于规范生成完整流水线的能力。

Result: 自主智能体能成功利用Croissant Tasks规范从头生成功能正确且准确的复现流水线。

Conclusion: Croissant Tasks为机器学习自动化与概念可复现性提供了新基础，有望替代脆弱的源代码复用模式。

中文摘要：可复现性是科学方法的基础，但在机器学习中仍然是一个关键挑战。影响因素包括不明确的执行细节和脆弱的软件环境。以人为中心的补救措施（如检查表和手动验证）有所帮助，但需要大量努力且难以扩展。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了Croissant Tasks：一种声明式的、机器可操作的元数据格式，将低层实现细节抽象为高层规范。这种格式实现了概念上的可复现性：通过独立的、由智能体生成的实现来验证声明，而不是脆弱的源代码复制。我们贡献了：(1) Croissant Tasks规范，正式将任务问题与解决方案解耦；(2) 一种自动化的LLM流水线，将现有基准测试改编为此格式；(3) 实证验证表明，自主智能体可以摄入这些规范，从头生成功能准确的可复现流水线。我们设想这种格式作为机器学习中自动化和概念可复现性的新基础。

Original abstract: Reproducibility is fundamental to the scientific method, yet remains a critical challenge in machine learning. Contributing factors include underspecified execution details and brittle software environments. Human-centric remedies, such as checklists and manual verification, help but require intensive effort and fail to scale. To address this, we introduce Croissant Tasks: a declarative, machine-actionable metadata format that abstracts low-level implementation details into high-level specifications. This format enables conceptual reproducibility: verifying claims via independent, agent-generated implementations rather than brittle source code replication. We contribute: (1) the Croissant Tasks specification, formally decoupling task problem from solution; (2) an automated LLM pipeline that retrofits existing benchmarks into this format; and (3) empirical validation showing autonomous agents can ingest these specifications to generate functional, accurate reproduction pipelines from scratch. We envision this format as a new foundation for automated and conceptual reproducibility in machine learning.

### [53] [MEMENTO: Leveraging Web as a Learning Signal for Low-Data Domains](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29795v1)
*Ashutosh Ojha,Vinay Aggarwal,Ashutosh Srivastava,Siddharth Yedlapati,Yaman K Singla,Jitendra Ajmera*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将网络作为学习信号的agent框架，包含记忆与探索策略

TL;DR: MEMENTO通过将网络视为学习信号，利用自适应探索树和双通道记忆，在低数据专业领域实现了显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低数据学习方法仍依赖标注或伪标注数据，而人类通过自主网络交互获取知识，因此需要一种能从网络交互中学习、无需额外训练的框架。

Method: 提出MEMENTO框架，包含会话内的自适应探索树（AET）进行迭代网络探索，以及跨会话的双通道记忆（陈述性知识和程序性知识分离），使代理从网络交互轨迹中学习可重用策略和专业知识。

Result: 在销售自动化和法律研究任务上，MEMENTO相比ReAct基线分别提升25.6%和36.5%。

Conclusion: 在数据稀缺场景下，网络可以成为获取任务特定专业知识的可扩展学习源。

中文摘要：现实世界的任务通常缺乏大规模标注数据集，这激励了大量关于低数据场景下学习的研究。然而，现有方法如少样本提示、指令调整和合成数据生成，仍然将标注或伪标注数据作为主要学习信号。相比之下，人类从业者通过重复、自主地与开放网络互动来获取专业知识，逐步改进领域知识和搜索策略。我们提出MEMENTO，一个将网络视为学习信号而非无状态检索接口的框架。MEMENTO在两个层面运作：在每个会话内，它通过自适应探索树（AET）进行迭代网络探索，该树将任务分解为不断演变的问题并反思中间发现；跨会话时，它通过双通道记忆积累经验，将陈述性知识（事实）与程序性知识（搜索策略）分离。这种设计使代理能够从网络交互轨迹中学习可重用的研究策略和领域专业知识，而无需额外的模型训练。我们在两个低数据专业领域：销售自动化和法律研究上评估MEMENTO。我们的实证结果显示，与基于ReAct的基线相比，性能持续提升（销售自动化提升25.6%，法律研究提升36.5%），表明在数据稀缺场景下，网络可以成为获取任务特定专业知识的一个可扩展学习源。

Original abstract: Real-world tasks often lack large labeled datasets, motivating extensive work on learning in low-data regimes. However, existing approaches such as few-shot prompting, instruction tuning, and synthetic data generation, continue to treat labeled or pseudo-labeled data as the primary learning signal. In contrast, human practitioners acquire expertise through repeated, self-directed interaction with the open web, progressively refining both domain knowledge and search strategies. We propose MEMENTO, a framework that treats the web as a learning signal rather than a stateless retrieval interface. MEMENTO operates at two levels: within each session, it conducts iterative web exploration via an Adaptive Exploration Tree (AET) that decomposes tasks into evolving questions and reflects on intermediate findings; across sessions, it accumulates experience through dual-channel memory, separating declarative knowledge (facts) from procedural knowledge (search strategies). This design enables agents to learn reusable research strategies and domain expertise from trajectories of web interaction without additional model training. We evaluate MEMENTO on two low-data professional domains: sales automation and legal research. Our empirical results show consistent improvements in performance over ReAct based baselines (+25.6% on sales automation and 36.5% on legal research), demonstrating that the web can serve as a scalable learning source for acquiring task-specific expertise in data-scarce settings.

### [54] [SkillsInjector: Dynamic Skill Context Construction for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29794v1)
*Yanchao Li,Wanhao Liu,Ben Gao,Jiaqing Xie,Zhehong Ai,Na Zou,Yuqiang Li,Tianfan Fu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 动态技能上下文构建，优化agent工具使用与注入

TL;DR: SkillsInjector通过两阶段自适应方法（上下文规划器和集合感知渲染器）优化技能注入的选择、数量和呈现方式，在多个基准上显著提升LLM智能体的任务完成性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将技能注入视为静态步骤，使用固定标准选择技能、预先设定预算且不改变描述，导致注入更多技能可能降低性能，因为技能暴露、数量和呈现方式均影响下游效果。

Method: 提出SkillsInjector，包含两个阶段：1）上下文规划器学习基于执行的技能偏好，自适应确定每个任务的技能数量；2）集合感知渲染器根据共注入邻居定制所选技能的描述呈现。

Result: 在tau2-bench、SkillsBench和ALFWorld上，SkillsInjector分别比最强基线提高3.9、6.1和7.3个百分点，消融实验证实各组件均有贡献。

Conclusion: 技能增强型智能体应优化注入上下文本身，包括技能选择、自适应预算和集合感知呈现，以提升任务完成效果。

中文摘要：LLM智能体现在利用不断增长的技能库来处理复杂任务。然而，注入更多技能并不总能提升任务完成效果，甚至可能降低性能。现有方法仍将技能注入视为静态步骤，使用固定标准选择技能，提前设定预算，且不改变描述。我们认为这种静态处理会削弱技能的效用，因为暴露哪些技能、包含多少技能以及如何呈现它们都会影响下游性能。我们提出SkillsInjector，一种两阶段自适应方法，联合解决这些决策。首先，上下文规划器学习基于执行的技能偏好，并为每个任务自适应地确定技能数量。然后，集合感知渲染器根据技能与共注入邻居的相对关系，定制所选描述的呈现方式。在tau2-bench、SkillsBench和ALFWorld上，SkillsInjector取得了最高分，分别比最强基线提高了3.9、6.1和7.3个百分点。消融研究表明，技能选择、自适应预算和集合感知渲染各自贡献了增益。这些结果表明，技能增强型智能体受益于优化注入的上下文本身。代码将在发表后发布。

Original abstract: LLM agents now draw on growing skill libraries to handle complex tasks. However, injecting more skills does not always improve task completion and can even degrade it. Existing methods still treat skill injection as a static step, selecting skills with fixed criteria, fixing the budget in advance, and leaving descriptions unchanged. We argue that this static treatment can undermine the utility of skills, because which skills are exposed, how many are included, and how they are presented all affect downstream performance. We propose SkillsInjector, a two-stage adaptive method that jointly addresses these decisions. First, a context planner learns execution-grounded skill preferences and admits an adaptive number of skills for each task. A set-aware renderer then tailors how selected descriptions are presented relative to their co-injected neighbors. Across tau2-bench, SkillsBench, and ALFWorld, SkillsInjector achieves the highest score, improving over the strongest baseline by 3.9, 6.1, and 7.3 percentage points, respectively. Ablation studies show that skill selection, adaptive budgeting, and set-aware rendering each contribute to the gain. These results show that skill-augmented agents benefit from optimizing the injected context itself. Code will be released upon publication

</details>


### [55] [SAAS: Self-Aware Reinforcement Learning for Over-Search Mitigation in Agentic Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29796v3)
*Yunbo Tang,Chengyi Yang,Shiyu Liu,Zhishang Xiang,Zerui Chen,Qinggang Zhang,Jinsong Su*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自我感知RL减少搜索过度，提升agent搜索效率

TL;DR: 提出SAAS框架，通过动态自我意识减少过度搜索并保持准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体搜索系统缺乏自我意识，导致盲目搜索和过度搜索，造成高延迟和成本。

Method: SAAS包括三个组件：搜索边界建模（对比搜索禁用/启用轨迹）、边界感知奖励（轨迹级惩罚抑制冗余搜索）、分阶段优化（顺序课程优先推理）。

Result: 实验表明SAAS大幅减少过度搜索同时保持准确性。

Conclusion: SAAS通过动态自我意识有效调控搜索行为，降低计算成本。

中文摘要：智能体搜索使大语言模型能够通过迭代推理和外部搜索解决复杂的多跳问题。尽管有效，但这些系统在实践中常面临关键限制：智能体未能识别自身的知识边界，在内部知识足够时盲目触发搜索，即使收集到足够证据也未能终止搜索。缺乏自我意识导致严重的过度搜索，产生大量推理延迟和过高的计算成本。为此，我们提出SAAS，一种新颖的强化学习框架，旨在培养动态自我意识，在不牺牲准确性的前提下精确调控搜索行为。SAAS引入了三个关键组件：(i) 搜索边界建模机制，通过对比禁用搜索与启用搜索的轨迹，识别演化策略下的搜索边界；(ii) 边界感知奖励模块，将这种边界意识转化为轨迹级惩罚，抑制不必要和冗余的搜索；(iii) 分阶段优化策略，利用顺序课程优先考虑推理而非搜索正则化，从而避免奖励作弊。大量实验表明，SAAS在保持准确性的同时大幅减少了过度搜索。我们的代码和实现细节已发布在https://github.com/XMUDeepLIT/SAAS。

Original abstract: Agentic search enables LLMs to solve complex multi-hop questions through iterative reasoning and external search. Despite the effectiveness, these systems often suffer from a critical limitation in practice: agents fail to recognize their own knowledge boundaries, blindly triggering searches when internal knowledge suffices and failing to terminate search even when adequate evidence has been collected. The lack of self-awareness leads to severe \textbf{over-search}, incurring substantial inference latency and prohibitive computational cost. To this end, we propose SAAS, a novel RL framework designed to cultivate dynamic self-awareness that precisely regulates search behavior without compromising accuracy. SAAS introduces three key components: (i) a search boundary modeling mechanism, which identifies the search boundary under the evolving policy by contrasting search-disabled and search-enabled rollouts; (ii) a boundary-aware reward module, which translates this boundary awareness into trajectory-level penalties, suppressing unnecessary and redundant searches; and (iii) a stage-wise optimization strategy, which leverages a sequential curriculum to prioritize reasoning over search regularization, thereby avoiding reward hacking. Extensive experiments demonstrate that SAAS substantially reduces over-search, while maintaining accuracy. Our code and implementation details are released at https://github.com/XMUDeepLIT/SAAS.

</details>

中文摘要：现代开放世界智能体（如OpenClaw）展现出强大的跨环境执行能力，但也带来了广泛的新安全风险源。同时，先进的前沿AI模型大幅降低了攻击门槛，使得当前的智能体对齐框架不足以应对实际部署。为应对这些新兴威胁，我们提出了一种轻量级且可扩展的智能体安全对齐框架。具体而言，我们更新了智能体安全分类法，以适应Codex和OpenClaw执行场景中的新兴风险。我们进一步构建了一个基于分类法引导的数据引擎，并采用影响函数净化方法，仅使用约1k样本训练轻量级AgentDoG 1.5变体（0.8B、2B、4B和8B参数），达到了与领先闭源模型（如GPT-5.4）相当的性能。基于AgentDoG 1.5，我们构建了一个高效的智能体安全SFT和RL训练环境，将Docker级环境中的部署开销降低了两个数量级。最后，我们将AgentDoG 1.5部署为无需训练的在线护栏，用于实时安全审核。大量实验结果表明，AgentDoG 1.5在多样且复杂的交互式智能体场景中达到了最先进的性能。所有模型和数据集均已开源。

Original abstract: Modern open-world agents such as OpenClaw exhibit powerful cross-environment execution capabilities yet introduce broad new safety risk sources. Meanwhile, advanced frontier AI models drastically lower attack barriers, rendering current agent alignment frameworks inadequate for real-world deployment. To tackle these emerging threats, we propose a lightweight and scalable agent safety alignment framework. Specifically, we update the agent safety taxonomy to accommodate emergent risks from Codex and OpenClaw execution scenarios. We further build a taxonomy-guided data engine with influence-function purification to train lightweight AgentDoG 1.5 variants (0.8B, 2B, 4B, and 8B parameters) using only around 1k samples, achieving comparable performance with leading closed-source models (e.g., GPT-5.4). Based on AgentDoG 1.5, we construct a highly efficient agentic safety SFT and RL training environment, which reduces deployment overhead in Docker-level environments by two orders of magnitude. Finally, we deploy AgentDoG 1.5 as a training-free online guardrail for real-time safety moderation. Extensive experimental results indicate that AgentDoG 1.5 achieves state-of-the-art performance in diverse and complex interactive agentic scenarios. All models and datasets are openly released.

### [57] [OptSkills: Learning Generalizable Optimization Skills from Problem Archetypes via Cluster-Based Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29829v1)
*Haochen Yang,Ke Zhao,Mengyuan Ma,Xingyu Lu,Xiangfeng Wang,Hong Qian*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于原型的优化建模agent，与自动代码优化方向相关

TL;DR: 提出OptSkills，一种基于原型的技能学习与推理智能体系统，通过聚类问题原型、探索多样化解法并提炼工作流技能，提升了优化建模与求解的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法泛化能力有限，对表面叙事变化敏感，主要依赖案例级经验复用，难以适应变化或新兴的问题类型。

Method: 系统根据问题潜在原型进行聚类；在每个聚类内探索多样化建模范式和求解器配置；将成功轨迹蒸馏为可重用的工作流级技能；利用新轨迹改进现有技能或扩展技能库。

中文摘要：利用大型语言模型（LLM）从自然语言中自动制定和解决优化问题已成为自动化优化的一种高效范式。然而，现有方法仍然表现出有限的泛化能力：它们对表面叙事变化敏感，主要在案例级别复用经验，并且难以适应变化或新兴的问题类型。我们提出OptSkills，一种面向原型的技能学习和推理智能体系统，用于优化建模和求解。为了提高鲁棒泛化能力，我们的系统根据问题的潜在原型而非表面叙事对问题进行聚类。为了提高分布内泛化能力，它在每个聚类内探索多样化的建模范式和求解器配置，然后将成功轨迹提炼为可重用的工作流级技能。为了提高分布外泛化能力，它利用新获得的轨迹改进现有技能或扩展技能库。我们的系统在包含多种问题类型和场景的数据集上实现了68.27%的最先进微平均准确率。此外，在MIPLIB-NL（一个极具挑战性的大规模高维基准测试）上，它达到了26.91%的准确率，比DeepSeek-V3.2-Thinking高出4.53%。在Nano-CO上进行技能学习后，它在OOD NLCO基准测试上达到了72.79%。代码和技能可在https://github.com/fujiwaranoM0kou/OptSkills获取。

Original abstract: Leveraging Large Language Models (LLMs) to automatically formulate and solve optimization problems from natural language has emerged as an efficient paradigm for automated optimization. However, existing methods still exhibit limited generalization: they are sensitive to superficial narrative variations, reuse experience mainly at the case level, and struggle to adapt to shifted or emerging problem types. We propose OptSkills, an archetype-centric skill learning and reasoning agent system for optimization modeling and solving. To improve robust generalization, our system clusters problems by their underlying archetypes rather than surface narratives. To improve in-distribution generalization, it explores diverse modeling paradigms and solver configurations within each cluster, then distills successful trajectories into reusable workflow-level skills. To improve out-of-distribution generalization, it refines existing skills or expands the skill library using newly obtained trajectories. Our system achieves a state-of-the-art micro-averaged accuracy of 68.27% on datasets encompassing diverse problem types and scenarios. In addition, on MIPLIB-NL, a highly challenging large-scale and high-dimensional benchmark, it achieves 26.91% accuracy, outperforming DeepSeek-V3.2-Thinking by 4.53%. After skill learning on Nano-CO, it reaches 72.79% on the OOD NLCO benchmark. Code and skills are available at https://github.com/fujiwaranoM0kou/OptSkills.

### [58] [Redundant or Necessary? A Benchmark for Detecting Redundant Steps in Agent Trajectories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29893v1)
*Minyang Hu,Bo Yang,Zhinuo Zhou,Jiachen Liang,Guo Jiahao,Yiyang Yin,Xiongwei Han*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 检测agent轨迹冗余步骤的benchmark，直接提升代码优化agent效率

TL;DR: 提出了冗余步骤检测的新研究方向，构建了RedundancyBench基准，评估了三种方法，最佳方法仅达到24.88%的检测得分，表明任务复杂且需进一步研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估协议只关注任务成功，忽视了执行效率，而代理轨迹中常包含消耗资源但贡献少的冗余步骤。

Method: 提出冗余步骤检测任务，构建RedundancyBench基准，包含带步骤贡献标签的轨迹；开发并评估了三种代表性方法。

Result: 最佳方法检测冗余步骤得分仅24.88%，部分方法甚至差于随机猜测。

Conclusion: 冗余步骤检测具有挑战性，需要进一步研究。

中文摘要：基于LLM的代理已经通过多步推理和工具使用在解决复杂任务方面展示了强大的能力。然而，现有的评估协议主要关注任务成功，忽略了代理行为的一个关键方面：执行效率。在实践中，代理轨迹通常包含冗余步骤，这些步骤消耗大量资源但对任务完成的贡献很小。在这项工作中，我们提出并定义了一个新的研究领域：代理轨迹的冗余步骤检测。为了支持这一倡议，我们引入了RedundancyBench，这是一个新的基准，包含多样化的任务和精心注释的轨迹，其中每一步都根据其对任务完成的贡献进行标记。利用RedundancyBench，我们开发并评估了3种代表性方法，以判断轨迹中的某一步是冗余还是必要的。我们的结果表明，即使是表现最好的方法在检测冗余步骤方面也只达到了24.88%的得分，而有些方法的表现不如随机猜测。这些结果突显了该任务的复杂性以及在该领域进一步研究的必要性。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents have demonstrated strong capabilities in solving complex tasks through multi-step reasoning and tool use. However, existing evaluation protocols primarily focus on task success, overlooking a critical aspect of agent behavior: execution efficiency. In practice, agent trajectories often contain redundant steps that consume substantial resources while contributing little to task completion. In this work, we propose and formulate a new research area: \textbf{redundant step detection} for agent trajectories. To support this initiative, we introduce \textbf{RedundancyBench}, a new benchmark that contains diverse tasks with carefully annotated trajectories, where each step is labeled according to its contribution to task completion. Using RedundancyBench, we develop and evaluate 3 representative methods to answer whether a step within trajectory is redundant or necessary. Our results show that even the best-performing method achieves only 24.88\% score in detecting redundant steps, while some methods perform worse than random guessing. These results highlight the task's complexity and the need for further research in this area. \footnote{Code and dataset in this paper are both available in \href{https://anonymous.4open.science/r/RedundancyBench}{https://anonymous.4open.science/r/RedundancyBench}.}

</details>


### [59] [Make LLM Learn to Synthesize from Streaming Experiences through Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29940v1)
*Zhenlin Hu,Yan Wang,Zhen Bi,Zihao Xue,Bingyu Zhu,Longtao Huang,Xiongtao Zhang,Zeyu Yang,Zhixuan Chu,Jungang Lou*

Selection reason: LLM从流式经验中学习合成数据，涉及经验迁移和自我改进，属于通用agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出StreamSynth设置和SynLearner框架，实现跨任务顺序合成数据生成的经验积累与迁移，实验证明其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有合成数据生成研究将任务孤立处理，未探索模型能否从历史任务中积累经验并迁移至未来任务以提升合成性能。

Method: 引入StreamSynth设置（任务顺序到达）；提出SynLearner框架，通过探索多样合成模式、学习反馈及平衡质量与多样性，使模型在任务流中获取可重用经验。

Result: 多基准实验表明，SynLearner能有效利用早期任务经验提升后期任务合成性能，展现一致的跨任务可迁移性。

Conclusion: 合成数据生成可视为经验驱动过程，能从任务流中受益；StreamSynth设置可行，为未来研究提供方向。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）已被广泛用于合成数据生成，显著降低了标注成本。然而，大多数现有研究将合成视为一组孤立的任务，忽略了一个更根本的问题：模型能否通过积累过去任务的经验并将其迁移到未来任务中来学习合成？在这项工作中，我们引入了StreamSynth，这是一种新的设置，其中合成任务按顺序到达，历史任务的经验为未来合成提供信息信号。为了解决这一设置，我们提出了SynLearner，这是一个通用框架，使合成模型能够在任务流中获取可重用的合成经验。SynLearner不是独立地为每个任务生成数据，而是鼓励模型探索多样化的合成模式，从反馈中学习，并在任务演化过程中平衡样本质量与集合级别的多样性。跨多个基准的大量实验表明，SynLearner有效地利用了早期任务的经验来提高后期任务的合成性能，表现出一致的跨任务可迁移性。这些发现为StreamSynth的可行性提供了证据，并凸显了合成数据生成作为一个经验驱动过程可以从任务流中受益。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have been widely adopted for synthetic data generation, significantly reducing annotation costs. However, most existing studies treat synthesis as a set of isolated tasks and overlook a more fundamental question: whether a model can learn to synthesize by accumulating experience from past tasks and transferring it to future ones. In this work, we introduce StreamSynth, a new setting in which synthesis tasks arrive sequentially and experience from historical tasks provides informative signals for future synthesis. To address this setting, we propose SynLearner, a general framework that enables synthesis models to acquire reusable synthesis experience over a task stream. Instead of generating data independently for each task, SynLearner encourages the model to explore diverse synthesis patterns, learn from feedback, and balance sample quality with set-level diversity as tasks evolve. Extensive experiments across multiple benchmarks show that SynLearner effectively leverages experience from earlier tasks to improve synthesis performance on later ones, exhibiting consistent cross-task transferability. These findings provide evidence for the feasibility of StreamSynth and highlight synthetic data generation as an experience-driven process that can benefit from task streams.

Original abstract: We present AutoformBot, a multi-agent system for building an Autoformalized Textbook Library At Scale (Atlas) in Lean 4. We apply our methods to a corpus of 26 open-access textbooks spanning analysis, algebra, topology, combinatorics, and probability, producing Atlas: a verified library of over 45,000 Lean 4 declarations and 500 thousand lines of code. We release two artifacts: (i) AutoformBot, the open-source multi-agent framework; and (ii) Atlas, the resulting formal library. Our results suggest that autoformalizing the core content of graduate-level mathematics at scale is now economically and technically feasible. This opens the door to the automated verification of both human- and machine-generated mathematics at a research level.

### [61] [Compass: Navigating Global Marine Lead Data Integration through Expert-Guided LLM Agent](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29966v1)
*Yiming Liu,Bin Lu,Meng Jin,Ziyuan Sang,Shuo Jiang,Lei Zhou,Xinbing Wang,Chenghu Zhou,Jing Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原位观测成本高且稀疏，大量历史数据埋藏在论文中，人工提取不可扩展，通用LLM缺乏领域知识导致输出不可靠。

Method: 采用专家引导的适配方法，通过知识树增强的LLM智能体框架Compass，将复杂任务分解为可验证步骤，引导推理，无需微调即可从论文中提取数据。

Result: 从超过23万篇论文中成功提取3,751条新铅记录，建立最大综合海洋铅数据库，准确率92%，扩展了东海和南大洋等区域的覆盖。

Conclusion: 专家引导的智能体可有效弥合通用LLM与科学领域之间的差距，实现地球科学中可扩展的数据发现。

中文摘要：海洋铅（Pb）及其同位素是海洋环流和人为污染的关键示踪剂，然而原位观测仍然成本高昂且稀疏。尽管存在大量历史记录，但它们深埋于学术论文的非结构化内容中，形成了无法进行综合分析的数据孤岛。人工提取不可扩展，而通用大型语言模型（LLM）缺乏必要的领域知识，导致幻觉和科学上无效的输出。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了一种专家引导的适配方法，使LLM无需微调即可执行严格的科学数据提取。我们通过Compass框架实现了该方法，该框架是一个由海洋科学家共同设计的知识树增强的LLM智能体框架，它将复杂任务分解为可验证的步骤，引导智能体的推理以确保科学有效性。将Compass应用于超过230,000篇相关开放获取论文的语料库，我们成功提取了3,751条此前未整合的铅记录。这项努力建立了迄今为止最大的综合海洋铅数据库。除标准指标外，Compass通过多层次验证展现了卓越的可靠性，经专家人工验证确认准确率达到92%。新整合的数据扩展了先前采样不足区域（如东海和南大洋）的覆盖范围，为未来的科学发现提供了丰富的数据基础。我们发布了一个交互式可视化平台以促进开放科学访问。我们的工作表明，专家引导的智能体可以有效弥合通用LLM与高风险科学领域之间的差距，实现地球科学中可扩展的数据发现。

Original abstract: Marine lead (Pb) and its isotopes are critical tracers for ocean circulation and anthropogenic pollution, yet in-situ observations remain costly and sparse. While vast historical records exist, they lie buried within the unstructured content of academic papers, creating "data silos" inaccessible to comprehensive analysis. Manual extraction is unscalable, while general-purpose Large Language Models (LLMs) lack the necessary domain-specific knowledge, leading to hallucinations and scientifically invalid outputs. To address this, we introduce an expert-guided adaptation approach that enables LLMs to perform rigorous scientific data extraction without fine-tuning. We operationalize this approach through Compass, an LLM agent framework enhanced by a Knowledge Tree co-designed with marine scientists, which decomposes complex tasks into verifiable steps, guiding the agent's reasoning to ensure scientific validity. Deploying Compass across a corpus of over 230,000 relevant open-access papers, we successfully extract 3,751 previously unincorporated Pb records. This effort establishes the largest integrated marine Pb database to date. Beyond standard metrics, Compass demonstrates superior reliability through multi-layered validation, achieving 92% accuracy as confirmed through expert manual verification. The newly integrated data expand coverage in previously under-sampled regions such as the East China Sea and the Southern Ocean, providing an enriched data foundation for future scientific discoveries. We release an interactive visualization platform to facilitate open scientific access. Our work demonstrates that expert-guided agents can effectively bridge the gap between general-purpose LLMs and high-stakes scientific domains, enabling scalable data discovery in geosciences.

### [62] [Cookie-Bench: Continuous On-screen Key Interaction Evaluation for Web Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30000v2)
*Haoyue Yang,Zhangxiao Shen,Fan Ding,Hangting Lou,Yifeng Kou,Haoqing Yu,Jingyao Li,Zhengfan Wu,Siqi Bao,Jing Liu,Hua Wu*

TL;DR: 提出了一个无需参考、自主驱动、整体推理的WebDev评估框架，包括一个多领域基准测试（Cookie）和一个基于元认知监控的三阶段评估方法（Framename），实验表明与人类专家评分高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: Framename在Cookie上与专家人类评分高度一致，并揭示了13个前沿LLM在交互式网页生成上的显著提升空间。

Conclusion: 提出的评估体系（Cookie和Framename）有效且可靠，为无参考、自主驱动的WebDev评估提供了新范式，并能指导未来LLM在交互式网页生成上的改进。

中文摘要：前端网页代码已经成为每个前沿LLM发布的核心产品界面，但以开发速度评估这些交互式应用程序仍然成本高昂，因为像Arena这样由人类评判的排行榜无法扩展。现有的自动化代理通常依赖于参考实现、测试套件或严格的检查清单，并且往往会错过人类评审员在实时会话中进行的推理综合。我们提出了一种新的评估体系，该体系同时是无需参考的、自主驱动的和整体推理的，并通过两个工件实例化。\textbf{\dataname}是一个涵盖11个领域、54个叶子节点、1000个查询的WebDev基准测试，涵盖静态展示和交互式应用任务，在三个难度级别和三个目标语言组之间保持平衡，并编写简短提示以防止从流传的提示中回忆。\textbf{\framename}基于Flavell的元认知监控，将证据收集与判断分为三个阶段：静态感知通过被动观察形成初步印象；代理驱动交互自主探索应用程序，同时捕捉连续屏幕视频、音频和每步截图；动态评分仅在证据链完整后才给出整体功能和美学的判断，并附带结构化的失败归因。在\dataname上，\framename与专家人类评分高度一致，同时揭示了13个前沿LLM在交互式网页生成上的显著提升空间。\noindenthttps://anonymous.4open.science/r/Cookie-3CE/

Original abstract: Front-end web code has become a core product surface for every frontier LLM release, yet evaluating these interactive applications at development speed remains costly because human-judged leaderboards like Arena do not scale. Existing automated proxies typically lean on reference implementations, test suites, or rigid checklists, and tend to miss the reasoned synthesis a human reviewer performs over a live session. We articulate a new evaluation regime that is simultaneously reference-free, autonomously driven, and holistically reasoned, and instantiate it through two artifacts. \textbf{\dataname} is an 11-domain, 54-leaf, 1,000-query WebDev benchmark spanning both static-presentation and interactive-application tasks, balanced across three difficulty tiers and three target-language groups, with briefs rewritten to resist recall from circulated prompts. \textbf{\framename}, grounded in Flavell's metacognitive monitoring, separates evidence accumulation from judgment across three stages: Static Perception forms a first impression from passive observation; Agent-Driven Interaction explores the application autonomously while capturing continuous screen video, audio, and per-step screenshots; Dynamic Scoring issues holistic functionality and aesthetics verdicts with structured failure attribution only after the evidence chain is complete. On \dataname, \framename aligns closely with expert human ratings while surfacing substantial headroom across 13 frontier LLMs on interactive web generation. \noindenthttps://anonymous.4open.science/r/Cookie-3CE/

### [63] [KairosAgent: Agentic Time Series Forecasting with Fused Semantic Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30002v1)
*Kun Feng,Ziwei Shan,Yuchen Fang,Yiyang Tan,Sihan Lu,Shuqi Gu,Lintao Ma,Xingyu Lu,Kan Ren*

TL;DR: 提出KairosAgent智能体框架，结合LLM推理和TSFM预测，通过动态工具调用增强数值理解和语义推理，并利用强化学习优化，实现零样本跨域多模态时间序列预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TSFMs缺乏语义理解和未来推理能力，LLMs缺乏数值理解和准确预测能力。

Method: 构建KairosAgent框架，包含LLM推理器和TSFM预测器，通过动态调用分析工具增强数值理解，推理结果融合到TSFM中，并采用强化学习范式（多轮细化、回合级信用分配）和高质量轨迹语料库。

Result: 在零样本预测任务上取得优越性能，有效利用预训练模型。

中文摘要：跨领域多模态时间序列预测是一项具有挑战性的任务，要求模型整合精确的数值理解、跨领域语义理解和有效的多模态融合。现有方法要么从头构建时间序列基础模型（TSFMs），要么利用预训练的大语言模型（LLMs）。然而，TSFMs往往忽视语义理解，缺乏进行面向未来的语义推理的能力，而LLMs在数值理解和准确的定量预测方面存在困难。为了克服这些限制，我们提出了KairosAgent，一种新颖的用于多模态时间序列预测的智能体框架，包括一个基于LLM的推理器和一个基于TSFM的预测器。KairosAgent通过动态调用分析工具来增强LLMs的数值理解和语义推理能力，从而统一文本推理和数值预测。推理结果随后融合到TSFM流水线中，实现更准确可靠的未来预测。为了进一步提高推理能力，我们整理了一个大规模的高质量轨迹语料库，以及一种基于强化学习的预测范式，具有多轮细化和回合级信用分配。实验表明，KairosAgent在最大化预训练LLMs和TSFMs效用的同时，实现了优越的零样本预测性能，为高效且可解释的时间序列智能体提供了一个有前景的方向。

Original abstract: Cross-domain multimodal time series forecasting is a challenging task, requiring models to integrate precise numerical comprehension, cross-domain semantic understanding, and effective multimodal fusion. Existing approaches either build Time Series Foundation Models (TSFMs) from scratch or leverage pretrained Large Language Models (LLMs). However, TSFMs often overlook semantic understanding and lack the ability to perform future-oriented semantic reasoning, and LLMs struggle with numerical comprehension and accurate quantitative forecasting. To overcome these limitations, we propose KairosAgent, a novel agentic framework for multimodal time series forecasting, including an LLM-based reasoner and a TSFM-based forecaster. KairosAgent unifies textual reasoning and numerical forecasting by dynamically invoking analytical tools to enhance the numerical understanding and semantic reasoning capabilities of LLMs. The reasoning results are subsequently fused into the TSFM pipeline, enabling more accurate and reliable future predictions. To further improve the reasoning, we curate a large-scale corpus of high-quality trajectories, alongside a reinforcement learning from forecasting paradigm with multi-turn refinement and turn-level credit assignment. Experiments demonstrate that KairosAgent achieves superior zero-shot forecasting performance while maximizing the utility of pretrained LLMs and TSFMs, presenting a promising direction for efficient and interpretable time series agents. The project page is at https://foundation-model-research.github.io/KairosAgent .

### [64] [RAISE: RAG Design as an Architecture Search Problem](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30029v1)
*Zhen Chen,Yibing Liu,Weihao Xie,Yu Liang,Peilin Chen,Shiqi Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: RAG架构搜索框架，涉及系统优化，可看作agent工具使用编排的元优化。

TL;DR: 提出RAISE框架用于RAG超参数优化，在多个数据集上评估13种算法，发现性能高度依赖任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通过启发式配置RAG系统阻碍了系统评估和可重复性，应形式化为RAG架构搜索问题。

Method: 引入RAISE框架，包含13种搜索算法，在标准化搜索空间和预算下，使用三个随机种子在七个文本和多模态数据集上评估。

Result: 优化性能高度任务依赖，无通用最优策略，一个数据集上的强方法不一定泛化到其他数据集。

Conclusion: RAISE为RAG超参数优化提供了公平、可重复和系统研究的共同实验基础。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）系统暴露了许多设计选择，涵盖查询重写、分块、检索深度、重排序和上下文压缩。在实践中，这些选择通常通过启发式方法配置，阻碍了跨设置的系统评估和可重复性。我们认为这一挑战最好被形式化为RAG架构搜索。为了支持对这一问题的可控和可重复研究，我们引入了RAG智能搜索引擎（RAISE），这是一个用于RAG超参数优化的综合框架和基准，它在标准化的搜索空间和预算下评估RAG管道的优化方法。RAISE实现了13种搜索算法，并使用三个随机种子在七个公开文本和多模态数据集上评估它们。我们的实验表明，优化性能高度依赖于任务：在一个数据集上表现良好的方法可能无法在其他数据集上一致泛化，这警示人们不要将聚合排名解释为普遍优越策略的证据。RAISE为RAG超参数优化的公平、可重复和系统研究提供了一个共同的实验基础。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems expose numerous design choices spanning query rewriting, chunking, retrieval depth, reranking, and context compression. In practice, these choices are often configured through heuristics, hindering systematic evaluation and reproducibility across settings. We argue that this challenge is best formulated as RAG architecture search. To support controlled and reproducible study of this problem, we introduce the RAG Intelligence Search Engine (RAISE), a comprehensive framework and benchmark for RAG hyperparameter optimization, which evaluates optimization methods for RAG pipelines under standardized search spaces and budgets. RAISE implements 13 search algorithms and evaluates them across seven public text and multimodal datasets using three random seeds. Our experiments show that optimization performance is highly task-dependent: methods that perform strongly on one dataset may not generalize consistently across others, cautioning against interpreting aggregate rankings as evidence of universally superior strategies. RAISE provides a common experimental substrate for fair, reproducible, and systematic research on RAG hyperparameter optimization.

</details>


### [65] [Domain-Specific Data Synthesis for LLMs via Minimal Sufficient Representation Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30039v2)

Method: DOMINO框架采用归纳范式，结合提示调整与对比解缠目标，从参考样本中学习最小充分领域表示，并利用该表示引导生成领域对齐的合成数据。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在通用能力方面取得了显著进展，并通过在领域特定数据上进行微调，在特定领域实现了强大性能。然而，获取目标领域的高质量数据仍然是一个重大挑战。现有的数据合成方法遵循演绎范式，严重依赖于以自然语言表达的明确领域描述和精心的提示工程，这限制了它们在领域难以描述或正式阐述的现实场景中的适用性。在这项工作中，我们通过归纳范式解决了领域特定数据合成这一未被充分探索的问题，其中目标领域仅通过一组参考示例来定义，特别是在领域特征难以用自然语言表达的情况下。我们提出了一个新颖框架DOMINO，它从参考样本中学习最小的充分领域表示，并利用它来指导领域对齐的合成数据的生成。DOMINO将提示调整与对比解缠目标相结合，以分离领域级别的模式与样本特定的噪声，从而在保留核心领域特征的同时减轻过拟合。理论上，我们证明了DOMINO扩展了合成数据分布的支持范围，确保了更大的多样性。在实验上，在领域定义隐含的具有挑战性的编码基准测试中，使用DOMINO合成的数据进行微调，在强大的指令调优基线上将Pass@1准确率提高了高达4.63%，证明了其有效性和鲁棒性。这项工作建立了领域特定数据合成的新范式，使得无需手动提示设计或自然语言领域规范即可实现实用且可扩展的领域适应。

Original abstract: Large Language Models have demonstrated remarkable progress in general-purpose capabilities and can achieve strong performance in specific domains through fine-tuning on domain-specific data. However, acquiring high-quality data for target domains remains a significant challenge. Existing data synthesis approaches follow a deductive paradigm, heavily relying on explicit domain descriptions expressed in natural language and careful prompt engineering, limiting their applicability in real-world scenarios where domains are difficult to describe or formally articulate. In this work, we tackle the underexplored problem of domain-specific data synthesis through an inductive paradigm, where the target domain is defined only through a set of reference examples, particularly when domain characteristics are difficult to articulate in natural language. We propose a novel framework, DOMINO, that learns a minimal sufficient domain representation from reference samples and leverages it to guide the generation of domain-aligned synthetic data. DOMINO integrates prompt tuning with a contrastive disentanglement objective to separate domain-level patterns from sample-specific noise, mitigating overfitting while preserving core domain characteristics. Theoretically, we prove that DOMINO expands the support of the synthetic data distribution, ensuring greater diversity. Empirically, on challenging coding benchmarks where domain definitions are implicit, fine-tuning on data synthesized by DOMINO improves Pass@1 accuracy by up to 4.63\% over strong, instruction-tuned backbones, demonstrating its effectiveness and robustness. This work establishes a new paradigm for domain-specific data synthesis, enabling practical and scalable domain adaptation without manual prompt design or natural language domain specifications.

### [66] [Learning to Choose: An Empowerment-Guided Multi-Agent System with semantic communication for Adaptive Method Selection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30042v1)
*Geremy Loachamín-Suntaxi,Robert Lazar,Dimitrios G. Giovanis,Ioannis G. Kevrekidis,Eleni D. Koronaki*
