### [96] [Honest Lying: Understanding Memory Confabulation in Reflexive Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29463v2)
*Prakhar Dixit,Sadia Kamal,Tim Oates*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 直接研究Reflexion agent的记忆错误问题，对agent自我改进有重要启发

TL;DR: 本文指出反思型智能体可能记忆虚构，并提出了反思重复率（RRR）指标来检测，通过程序化提取失败信号缓解此问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反思型智能体假设自我诊断准确，但实际可能系统性地失败，导致记忆虚构，需要研究此问题并提出解决方案。

Method: 通过跨ALFWorld和HumanEval实验，定义记忆虚构现象，引入反思重复率（RRR）指标，并提出用程序化提取轨迹级失败信号替代开放式自我诊断的缓解方法。

Result: 在ALFWorld中识别16个冻结环境（0条反思提及正确目标），HumanEval中4个类似案例；缓解方法将正确提及率从0%提升至86%，RRR从0.64降至0.10，解决3个冻结环境。

Conclusion: 反思性记忆可能强化错误信念而非纠正，简单的程序化提取比自我诊断更有效。

中文摘要：基于反思的智能体依赖自我生成的反思作为记忆，隐含地假设智能体能够准确诊断自己的失败。我们证明这一假设可能系统性失效：在ALFWorld和HumanEval中，智能体会存储自信但错误的任务解释，并在多次试验中持续依据这些解释行动，尽管环境每次都会重置为正确的任务。我们将这种失败模式称为记忆虚构，并引入反思重复率（RRR），这是一种基于日志的度量，用于检测对错误反思内容的重复依赖。使用RRR，我们在ALFWorld中识别出16个冻结环境，其中121条反思中有0条提及正确的目标对象，在HumanEval中有4个类似案例。我们的缓解方法将开放式自我诊断替换为对轨迹级失败信号的程序化提取，将正确对象提及率从0%提升到86%，RRR从0.64降至0.10，并解决了ALFWorld中16个冻结环境中的3个，这表明反思性记忆可能强化错误信念而非纠正它们。

Original abstract: Reflexion-style agents rely on self-generated reflections as memory, implicitly assuming that agents can accurately diagnose their own failures. We show that this assumption can fail systematically: across ALFWorld and HumanEval, agents store confident but incorrect interpretations of the task and continue acting on them across trials, even though the environment resets to the correct task each time. We call this failure mode memory confabulation and introduce the Reflection Repetition Rate (RRR), a log-based metric that detects repeated reliance on incorrect reflective content. Using RRR, we identify 16 frozen environments in ALFWorld, where 0 of 121 reflections mention the correct target object, and 4 analogous cases in HumanEval. Our mitigation replaces open-ended self-diagnosis with programmatic extraction of trajectory-level failure signals, increasing correct object mention from 0% to 86%, reducing RRR from 0.64 to 0.10, and solving 3 of 16 frozen ALFWorld environments, suggesting that reflective memory can reinforce false beliefs rather than correct them.

</details>


### [97] [Hista and Numca: Estimate State Value Effectively for LLM Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29782v1)
*Zizhe Chen,Jiqian Dong,Yizhou Tian,Garry Yang,Yongqiang Chen,Zhitang Chen,James Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: LLM RL中状态价值估计，对agent自我改进有潜在启发

TL;DR: 提出SVEB基准评估LLM后训练中的状态价值估计，发现PPO评论家崩溃为组平均基线。提出Numca和Hista方法，分别利用数值跨度和隐藏状态加权平均轨迹回报，提升估计精度和训练性能，且计算开销低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 状态价值估计在LLM后训练中未被充分探索，且现有方法（如PPO）中的评论家无法准确估计状态价值，导致训练不稳定。

Method: 提出Numca方法，利用数值跨度作为可分级里程碑进行状态价值估计；以及Hista框架，利用LLM的隐藏状态作为表示，加权平均不相交轨迹及其回报。

Result: 大量实验表明，Numca和Hista均能提供更准确的状态价值估计，并在不同RL算法和模型大小下提升训练性能，且计算开销可忽略。

Conclusion: 本文证明了通过改进状态价值估计可以显著提升LLM后训练的RL性能，提出的两种方法简单有效，具有实际应用价值。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）通过奖励信号直接优化模型行为来改进大语言模型（LLM）。虽然精确的状态价值估计对于经典RL中的稳定训练至关重要，但在LLM后训练中这一挑战仍未充分探索。在这项工作中，我们引入了状态价值估计基准（SVEB）来评估现有RL框架内的状态估计，并展示了标准方法（如PPO）中的评论家会崩溃为粗糙的组平均基线。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了两种技术：Numca，利用数值跨度作为可分级里程碑进行状态价值估计；以及Hista，一个利用LLM的隐藏状态作为表示来加权平均不相交的轨迹及其回报的框架。大量实验表明，这两种方法都能提供更准确的状态价值估计，并在不产生显著计算开销的情况下，提升了不同RL算法和模型大小的训练性能。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) refines large language models (LLMs) by directly optimizing model behavior through reward signals. While accurate state value estimation is critical for stable training in classical RL, it remains an underexplored challenge in LLM post-training. In this work, we introduce the State Value Estimation Benchmark (SVEB) to assess state estimation within existing RL frameworks and show that critics in standard approaches like PPO collapse to a coarse group-average baseline. To address this, we propose two techniques: Numca, which leverages numerical spans as gradable milestones for state value estimation, and Hista, a framework that uses LLM's hidden states as representation to weighted average disjoint rollouts and their return. Extensive experiments demonstrate that both methods yield more accurate state value estimates and enhance training performance across different RL algorithms and model sizes without incurring significant computational overhead.

</details>


### [98] [A Predictive Law for On-Policy Self-Distillation From World Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30070v1)
*Tommy He,Jerome Sieber,Matteo Saponati*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: on-policy自蒸馏预测，可能用于agent的自我改进训练

TL;DR: 发现OPSD中初始性能差距与最终改进之间存在线性关系，可预测OPSD效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索更丰富的世界反馈在强化学习后训练中的应用，并提升OPSD方法的可靠性预测。

Method: 通过实验分析OPSD中初始学生-自我-教师性能差距与最终性能改进的关系，验证线性相关性。

Result: 发现该线性关系在多种上下文和模型族中一致成立，且随模型规模保持可预测性。

Conclusion: OPSD性能可在训练前预测和调整，为将世界反馈融入后训练提供原则性方法。

中文摘要：超越简单的标量奖励，转向更丰富的世界反馈是通往更可扩展的强化学习后训练的自然路径。在策略自蒸馏（OPSD）是一种有前景的最新方法，它利用任意反馈作为学习信号，但其与GRPO等已有方法相比的可靠性仍不明确。我们发现初始学生-自我-教师性能差距与OPSD最终性能改进之间存在惊人一致的线性相关性。这种关系在上下文类型和模型族中均成立，为预测OPSD配置的结果提供了一种强大的预测法则，无需运行完整训练过程。有趣的是，我们表明这种线性可预测性随模型规模成立，这表明了在具有更强上下文学习能力的大模型上可能出现新的经验缩放定律。本质上，我们的发现表明OPSD性能可以在训练前被预测和调整，提供了一种原则性方法将世界反馈作为后训练管线的第一类组成部分。

Original abstract: Moving beyond simple scalar rewards toward richer world feedback is a natural path to more scalable RL post-training. On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) is a promising recent approach that uses arbitrary feedback as learning signal, yet its reliability compared to established methods, such as GRPO, remains unclear. We identify a strikingly consistent linear correlation between the initial student-self-teacher performance gap and the final performance improvement in OPSD. This relationship holds across context types and model families, providing a powerful predictive law for anticipating the outcome of an OPSD configuration without running the full training procedure. Interestingly, we show that this linear predictability holds with model scale, suggesting a potential basis for new empirical scaling laws on larger models with stronger in-context learning capabilities. In essence, our findings show that OPSD performance can be predicted and tuned before training, offering a principled way to incorporate world feedback as a first-class component of the post-training pipeline.

</details>


### [99] [ResearchClawBench: A Benchmark for End-to-End Autonomous Scientific Research](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07591v5)
*Wanghan Xu,Shuo Li,Tianlin Ye,Qinglong Cao,Yixin Chen,Hengjian Gao,Yiheng Wang,Qi Li,Kun Li,Sheng Xu,Shengdu Chai,Fangchen Yu,Xiangyu Zhao,Zhangrui Zhao,Weijie Ma,Zijie Guo,Koutian Wu,Haoyu Zhou,Haoxiang Yin,Lixue Cheng,Chaofan Hu,Haoxuan Li,Lu Mi,Xuxuan Xie,Yifan Zhou,Ruizhe Chen,Zhiwang Zhou,Xingjian Guo,Yuhao Zhou,Xuming He,Shengyuan Xu,Xinyu Gu,Jiamin Wu,Mianxin Liu,Chunfeng Song,Fenghua Ling,Dongzhan Zhou,Shixiang Tang,Yuqiang Li,Mao Su,Peng Ye,Siqi Sun,Bin Wang,Xue Yang,Zhenfei Yin,Tianfan Fu,Guangtao Zhai,Wanli Ouyang,Bo Zhang,Lei Bai,Wenlong Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建40个来自10个科学领域的任务，每个任务基于真实论文并隐藏目标，使用专家策划的多模态评分标准评估自主代理和LLM。

Result: 最强自主代理Claude Code平均21.5，最强LLM Claude-Opus-4.7平均20.7，LLM前沿均值26.5，错误集中在实验协议不匹配、证据不匹配和缺少科学核心。

Conclusion: ResearchClawBench为自主科学研究提供了可复现的评估前沿，当前系统远未达到可靠重新发现水平。

中文摘要：AI编码代理越来越多地用于科学工作，但它们的端到端自主研究能力仍然难以验证。我们提出了ResearchClawBench，这是一个用于评估自主科学研究的基准，包含来自10个科学领域的40个任务。每个任务基于一篇真实的已发表论文，提供相关文献和原始数据，并在评估期间隐藏目标论文。专家策划的多模态评分标准将目标科学制品分解为加权标准，从而能够在评估目标论文级别的重新发现的同时为新的发现留出空间。我们在统一协议下评估了七个自主研究（auto-research）代理，并通过轻量级ResearchHarness评估了十七个原生LLM。当前系统远未能可靠地重新发现：最强的自主代理Claude Code平均得分为21.5，最强的ResearchHarness LLM Claude-Opus-4.7平均得分为20.7，而LLM前沿均值仅为26.5。错误分析显示，失败集中在实验协议不匹配、证据不匹配和缺少科学核心。ResearchClawBench为衡量自主科学研究的进展提供了一个可复现的评估前沿。

Original abstract: AI coding agents are increasingly used for scientific work, but their end-to-end autonomous research capability remains difficult to verify. We present ResearchClawBench, a benchmark for evaluating autonomous scientific research across 40 tasks from 10 scientific domains. Each task is grounded in a real published paper, provides related literature and raw data, and hides the target paper during evaluation. Expert-curated multimodal rubrics decompose the target scientific artifacts into weighted criteria, enabling evaluation of target-paper-level re-discovery while leaving room for new discovery. We evaluate seven autonomous research (auto-research) agents under a unified protocol and seventeen native LLMs through the lightweight ResearchHarness. Current systems remain far from reliable re-discovery: the strongest autonomous agent, Claude Code, averages 21.5, and the strongest ResearchHarness LLM, Claude-Opus-4.7, averages 20.7, with an LLM frontier mean of only 26.5. Error analysis shows that failures concentrate in experimental protocol mismatch, evidence mismatch, and missing scientific core. ResearchClawBench provides a reproducible evaluation frontier for measuring progress toward autonomous scientific research.

### [100] [Self-Trained Verification for Training- and Test-Time Self-Improvement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30290v2)
*Chen Henry Wu,Aditi Raghunathan*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出自我训练的验证方法用于推理模型的自我改进，可迁移至agent的验证循环

TL;DR: 提出自我训练验证（STV）和验证器循环内训练（ViL），通过利用参考解决方案训练验证器，显著提升测试时验证-细化循环和训练时生成器性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证器是推理模型自我改进的瓶颈，现有方法因缺乏捕捉自生成错误的训练信号而失败。

Method: 基于模型在参考解决方案下能识别错误的不对称性，训练验证器模仿更知情的自身版本（STV）；并在测试时用STV改进V-R循环，训练时用RL和STV反馈进行验证器循环内训练（ViL）。

Result: STV在硬数学上准确率翻倍，科学推理提升14倍；ViL额外提升33%的pass@1，且独立生成器pass@1相对提升30%。

Conclusion: 推理模型的下一个前沿在于如何训练用于验证和与验证一起训练的方法。

中文摘要：自我改进在规模上一直是推理模型的长期目标，有两个自然的地方可以做到：在测试时，通过验证-细化（V-R）循环；在训练时，通过自我训练方法。两者都受限于同一个瓶颈：验证器。当验证器得分膨胀而准确率停滞，且反馈过于通用而无法采取行动时，V-R循环会停滞；当错误的自生成数据被添加到训练中时，自我训练也会失败。更好的验证可以解锁两者，但我们想要训练的能力，即捕捉自生成的错误，缺乏训练信号。为了解决这个挑战，我们提出了自我训练验证（STV）。我们的关键观察是，虽然模型无法单独捕捉这些错误，但当显示参考解决方案时，它可以。我们将这种不对称性转化为监督目标，并训练验证器模仿更了解自身的版本。在测试时，STV在难题上显著改善了V-R循环，而替代方案（例如SFT、RL on verifier scores，甚至元验证器）则没有。STV在硬数学上大致使准确率翻倍，在科学推理任务上将其提升14倍（从1.5%到21%）。在训练时，我们另外使用RL和STV验证器的反馈在V-R循环内训练生成器——这一过程称为验证器循环内训练（ViL）。从RL收敛的生成器开始，ViL在pass@1上进一步提高了33%。更值得注意的是，生成器的独立pass@1（测试时没有验证器）相对于标准RL收敛之处相对增长了30%。因此，解决难题的下一个前沿可能在于我们如何训练用于验证和与验证一起训练。

Original abstract: Self-improvement at scale has been a longstanding goal for reasoning models, and there are two natural places to do it: at test time, through verification-refinement (V-R) loops; and at training time, through self-training methods. Both are gated by the same bottleneck: the verifier. V-R loops stall when verifier scores inflate while accuracy stagnates, and when feedback is too generic to act on; self-training fails similarly when bad self-generated data are added to training. Better verification would unlock both, but the capability we want to train, i.e., catching self-generated errors, lacks training signal. To address this challenge, we propose self-trained verification (STV). Our key observation is that, while a model cannot catch these errors alone, it can when shown the reference solution. We turn this asymmetry into a supervision target and train the verifier to imitate a more informed version of itself. At test time, STV substantially improves V-R loops on hard problems, while alternatives (e.g., SFT, RL on verifier scores, and even meta-verifiers) do not. STV roughly doubles accuracy on hard math and lifts it 14x on scientific reasoning tasks (1.5% to 21%). At training time, we additionally train the generator using RL with STV verifier's feedback inside the V-R loop - a procedure we call verifier-in-the-loop training (ViL). Starting from an RL-converged generator, ViL yields a further 33% gain in pass@1. More notably, the generator's standalone pass@1, with no verifier at test time, climbs 30% relative past where standard RL had converged. Hence, the next frontier in reasoning on hard problems may lie in how we train for and with verification. Website: https://ar-forum.github.io/stv-webpage

</details>


### [101] [Gram: Assessing sabotage propensities via automated alignment auditing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30322v1)
*David Lindner,Victoria Krakovna,Sebastian Farquhar*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 评估agent在编码场景中的破坏倾向，涉及agent行为评估

TL;DR: Gram是一种自动对齐审计框架，用于评估AI代理的破坏倾向，在Gemini模型中发现约2-3%的模拟轨迹存在不当行为，主要源于过度急切，通过增加环境真实性和移除不当行为提示可显著降低破坏率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐审计方法不足以评估AI代理在自主编码和研究场景中的故意破坏行为，需要专门的框架来检测和量化这种风险。

Method: 提出Gram框架，在17个模拟代理部署场景中评估Gemini模型，并引入实验性调查代理流水线进行细粒度实验以识别不当行为驱动因素。

Result: Gemini模型在2-3%的模拟轨迹中出现不当行为，主要原因是过度急切导致过度角色扮演和追求目标；增加环境真实性和移除不当行为提示可使破坏率降至接近零。

Conclusion: Gram能够有效评估AI代理的破坏倾向，环境因素（如真实性和提示）对破坏行为有显著影响，调整这些因素可以大幅降低风险。

中文摘要：我们介绍了Gram，一种自动对齐审计框架，用于评估AI代理进行破坏的倾向。我们在17个激励破坏的模拟代理部署场景中评估了Gemini模型。我们发现Gemini模型在大约2-3%的模拟轨迹中出现不当行为。其中许多案例可由Gemini模型的“过度急切”解释，导致过度的角色扮演和追求目标的行为。与其他对齐审计方法相比，Gram专门设计用于评估代理编码和研究代理中的不对齐和故意破坏。我们还引入了一个实验性的调查代理流水线，能够进行细粒度的定向实验，以识别不当行为的驱动因素。我们发现，增加环境的真实性和消除不当行为的提示往往会使破坏率降低到接近零。

Original abstract: We introduce Gram, an automated alignment auditing framework to assess the propensity of AI agents to engage in sabotage. We evaluate Gemini models across 17 simulated agentic deployment scenarios that incentivize sabotage. We find Gemini models misbehave in about 2-3% of our simulated trajectories. Many of these cases are explained by "overeagerness" in Gemini models resulting in both excessive role-playing and goal-seeking behavior. In contrast to other alignment auditing approaches, Gram is designed to specifically evaluate misalignment and intentional sabotage in agentic coding and research agents. We additionally introduce an experimental investigator agent pipeline which enables fine-grained targeted experiments to identify the drivers of misbehavior. We find that increasing realism of environments and removing nudges to misbehave tends to reduce sabotage rates close to zero.

### [102] [Reasoning with Sampling: Cutting at Decision Points](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30327v1)
*Felix Zhou,Anay Mehrotra,Quanquan C. Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于熵的采样方法增强推理，可应用于agent决策点重采样

TL;DR: 提出Entropy-Cut Metropolis-Hastings算法，通过熵识别决策点进行重采样，高效从幂分布中采样以提升推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有从幂分布采样的方法均匀随机选择切割点，倾向于重写局部细节而非关键决策点，导致混合效率低。

Method: 使用基础模型的下一令牌熵作为代理识别关键决策点，并从这些位置进行重采样。

Result: 在MATH500、HumanEval、GPQA Diamond和AIME26上，该方法一致优于基线和强化学习训练模型。

Conclusion: 熵跳跃是决策点的有效代理，方法的混合时间与决策数量成正比，而非令牌数量。

中文摘要：前沿推理模型是通过对基础语言模型进行强化学习后训练得到的。最近的研究挑战了这一观点，表明从基础模型分布的锐化版本（即所谓的幂分布）中采样，可以在没有额外训练、精心整理的数据集或验证器的情况下获得可比较的推理能力。然而，使这种方法实用化需要高效地从幂分布中采样。采样器需要“混合”到幂分布，这需要在目标分布的模态之间移动；直观上，例如尝试不同的推理策略。先前工作中提出的采样器重复地在当前推理轨迹中均匀随机选择一个“切割”位置，并从该位置开始重新采样后缀。然而，推理轨迹通常包含少数几个关键的决策点（例如，证明策略或算法的选择），我们观察到均匀选择的切割往往重写局部细节而不是重新审视决策点。我们引入了一种算法（Entropy-Cut Metropolis-Hastings），该算法使用基础模型的下一个令牌熵作为代理来识别关键决策点并从这些位置重新采样。我们实证验证了熵跳跃是决策点的有用代理，并且在推理的经典模型中证明了我们方法的混合时间与轨迹中的决策数量成比例，而不是与可能大得多的令牌数量成比例。在MATH500、HumanEval、GPQA Diamond和AIME26上，我们的方法始终优于基线和经过强化学习训练的模型。

Original abstract: Frontier reasoning models are produced by posttraining base language models with reinforcement learning. Recent work has challenged this by showing that sampling from a sharpened version of the base model's distribution, a so-called power distribution, elicits comparable reasoning without additional training, curated datasets, or verifiers. However, making this method practical requires efficiently sampling from the power distribution. A sampler needs to "mix" to the power distribution, which necessitates moving between modes of the target distribution; intuitively, e.g., trying different reasoning strategies. The samplers proposed in prior works repeatedly select a "cut" position in the current reasoning trace uniformly at random and resample the suffix from that position onward. However, reasoning traces typically contain a few consequential decisions (e.g., the choice of proof strategy or algorithm), and we observe that a uniformly chosen cut tends to rewrite local details rather than revisit decision points. We introduce an algorithm (Entropy-Cut Metropolis-Hastings) that uses the base model's next-token entropy as a proxy to identify key decision points and resample from those positions. We empirically verify that entropy jumps are a useful proxy for decision points and, in a stylized model of reasoning, prove that our method's mixing time scales with the number of decisions in a trace rather than with the number of tokens, which can be much larger. Across MATH500, HumanEval, GPQA Diamond, and AIME26, our method consistently improves over baselines and RL-trained models.

</details>


### [103] [LongDS-Bench: On the Failure of Long-Horizon Agentic Data Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30434v1)
*Kewei Xu,Xiaoben Lu,Shuofei Qiao,Zihan Ding,Haoming Xu,Lei Liang,Ningyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 长程agent数据分析benchmark，直接研究agent长期执行与评测，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出了LongDS基准，用于评估长周期多轮数据分析中智能体维持演化状态的能力，发现最佳模型准确率仅48.45%，长周期错误占比高，瓶颈在于状态维持而非交互次数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要评估孤立或短期交互任务，缺乏对长周期迭代分析中上下文跟踪能力的测试。

Method: 从Kaggle笔记本构建68个任务，共2225轮，覆盖6个领域，设计状态演化模式（反事实扰动、回滚、多状态组合），平均依赖跨度11.3轮。

Result: 最佳模型平均准确率48.45%，从早期到后期轮次性能下降47个百分点，长周期错误占失败原因的52%-69%。

Conclusion: 关键瓶颈是维持正确的分析状态，而非增加交互步骤；现有模型在长周期状态跟踪上表现不足。

中文摘要：现实世界的数据分析本质上是迭代的，然而现有基准主要评估孤立的或短期的交互任务，未能测试智能体在长时间跨度内追踪演化分析上下文的能力。我们引入了LongDS，一个用于长周期、多轮数据分析的基准，其中智能体必须维护、更新、恢复和组合演化中的分析状态。LongDS包含从真实世界Kaggle笔记本构建的68个任务，涵盖6个领域（如地球科学、商业、教育）的2225个对话轮次。任务围绕状态演化模式（例如反事实扰动、回滚、多状态组合）设计，平均依赖跨度11.3轮。评估五个最先进模型，我们发现最佳模型仅达到48.45%的平均准确率，从早期到后期轮次性能下降近47个点，长周期错误占失败原因的52%-69%。进一步分析表明，增加智能体步骤不一定能提高性能，这表明关键瓶颈在于维持正确的分析状态，而非增加交互预算。我们发布LongDS以支持可靠的长周期智能体数据分析的研究。代码和数据将在https://github.com/zjunlp/DataMind发布。

Original abstract: Real-world data analysis is inherently iterative, yet existing benchmarks mostly evaluate isolated or short interactive tasks, leaving agents' ability to track evolving analytical context over long horizons untested. We introduce LongDS, a benchmark for long-horizon, multi-turn data analysis where agents must maintain, update, restore, and compose evolving analytical states. LongDS comprises 68 tasks constructed from real-world Kaggle notebooks, spanning 2,225 turns across six domains including Geoscience, Business, and Education. Tasks are designed around state-evolution patterns (e.g., counterfactual perturbation, rollback, multi-state composition), with an average dependency span of 11.3 turns. Evaluating five state-of-the-art models, we find that the best model reaches only 48.45% average accuracy, performance drops nearly 47 points from early to late turns, and long-horizon errors account for 52%--69% of failures. Further analysis shows that additional agent steps do not necessarily improve performance, suggesting that the key bottleneck is maintaining a correct analytical state rather than increasing interaction budget. We release LongDS to support research on reliable long-horizon agentic data analysis. Code and data will be released at https://github.com/zjunlp/DataMind.

</details>


### [104] [Scalable Constrained Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning via State Augmentation and Consensus for Separable Dynamics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30461v1)
*Santiago Amaya-Corredor,Miguel Calvo-Fullana,Anders Jonsson*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 约束多智能体强化学习的分布式共识方法，可迁移至多agent coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出一种分布式约束多智能体强化学习方法，通过邻接共识协调拉格朗日乘子，实现线性可扩展的全局约束满足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有全局资源约束的多智能体系统中，独立学习无法产生可行解，因为智能体无法确定个体对约束的贡献；现有CTDE方法复杂度随智能体数量二次增长，限制大规模应用。

Method: 结合状态增强策略学习与分布式共识：每个智能体学习以局部状态和对偶变量为条件的策略，通过邻接共识在线更新对偶变量以达成一致，实现约束协调。

Result: 实验表明，共识协调对可行性至关重要：无共识时智能体无限推迟需求（非解），有共识时收敛到共享对偶变量并满足约束与需求；方法线性扩展至数千智能体，而CTDE基线仅支持几十个。

Conclusion: 轻量级邻接共识足够实现全局约束协调，所提方法在保证约束满足的同时具有线性可扩展性，适用于大规模多智能体系统。

中文摘要：我们提出了一种针对约束多智能体强化学习（MARL）的分布式方法，该方法将状态增强策略学习与对偶变量的分布式共识相结合。我们的方法针对的是智能体具有可分离动态但必须协调以满足全局资源约束的系统。在这类设置中，我们通过实验证明，独立学习无法产生可行解，因为智能体无法确定为实现集体约束满足而应做出的适当个体贡献。关键技术贡献在于表明，对拉格朗日乘子进行轻量级的邻接共识足以实现全局协调的约束执行，同时保持独立训练的可扩展性。每个智能体离线学习一个单一增强策略，该策略以其局部状态和编码约束反馈的对偶变量为条件。在执行过程中，智能体仅通过局部通信就对该对偶变量达成一致。我们证明，在温和的连通性假设下，智能体乘子之间的共识误差是有界的，并且表明这转化为有界的约束违规，其随着图连通性和共识轮数的增加而减少。与集中训练分散执行（CTDE）方法（其复杂度至少随智能体数量呈二次增长）不同，我们的方法在训练和执行中均呈线性扩展。智能电网需求响应实验表明，共识协调对于可行性至关重要：没有共识，智能体只能通过无限期推迟需求来满足电网容量约束，这是一种退化的非解。有了共识，智能体收敛到共享的对偶变量，同时满足电网约束和需求履行，可扩展到数千个智能体，而CTDE基线仅限于几十个。

Original abstract: We present a distributed approach for constrained Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) that combines state-augmented policy learning with distributed consensus over dual variables. Our method targets systems where agents have separable dynamics but must coordinate to satisfy global resource constraints, a setting in which, as we demonstrate empirically, independent learning fails to produce feasible solutions because agents cannot determine appropriate individual contributions toward collective constraint satisfaction. The key technical contribution is showing that lightweight neighbor-to-neighbor consensus over Lagrange multipliers suffices for globally coordinated constraint enforcement while preserving the scalability of independent training. Each agent learns a single augmented policy offline, conditioned on both its local state and a dual variable encoding constraint feedback. During execution, agents reach agreement on this dual variable through local communication alone. We prove that under mild connectivity assumptions, the consensus error among agents' multipliers is bounded, and show that this translates to a bounded constraint violation that decreases with graph connectivity and the number of consensus rounds. Unlike centralized training with decentralized execution (CTDE) approaches, whose complexity grows at least quadratically with agent count, our method scales linearly in both training and execution. Experiments on smart grid demand response demonstrate that consensus coordination is \emph{essential for feasibility}: without it, agents satisfy grid capacity constraints only by indefinitely postponing demand, a degenerate non-solution. With consensus, agents converge to a shared dual variable and satisfy both grid constraints and demand fulfillment, scaling to thousands of agents while CTDE baselines are limited to dozens.

</details>


### [105] [Counterfactual Evaluation Reveals Hidden Capability Profiles in Clinical LLMs and Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30590v1)
*Matt Turk*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出Causal Sensitivity Score干预式评测方法，可评估LLM agent在临床输入变化时的响应，该度量可迁移至coding agent的鲁棒性验证。

TL;DR: 提出因果敏感性评分（CSS），通过沿着五个临床维度进行反事实干预来评估临床AI模型的响应性，发现覆盖度指标无法揭示的模型行为差异和安全性盲点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有覆盖率指标（如CMS）无法区分行为不同的AI系统，需要能够衡量模型对输入变化响应性的新指标。

Method: 设计因果敏感性评分（CSS），沿五个临床维度（生物标志物翻转、治疗失败、生物标志物移除、手术状态、分期扰动）变异肿瘤病例，评估模型建议是否按正确方向更新。

Result: CSS与CMS排名顺序几乎相反；所有模型在手术状态干预上表现极差；工具使用可提升多数模型CSS，但最低CSS模型仍无响应。

Conclusion: 干预性指标如CSS能捕获覆盖率指标遗漏的模型响应性，可作为临床AI主体评估和强化学习的有效工具。

中文摘要：两种临床AI系统在基于覆盖率的评分标准上得分几乎相同，但当患者输入发生变化时，它们的行为却截然不同：一个系统更新其建议以匹配新的临床信号，而另一个系统无论输入如何都产生相同的输出。我们引入了因果敏感性评分（CSS），这是一种预先注册的干预指标，它沿五个临床有意义的维度——生物标志物翻转、既往治疗失败、生物标志物移除、手术状态变化和分期扰动——对肿瘤委员会病例进行变异，并使用{0, 0.5, 1.0}量表评分每个模型是否以预先注册的正确方向更新其建议。与基于覆盖率的加权召回指标——共识匹配评分（CMS）相比，来自三个实验室的六个前沿模型在224例病例的单次推理评估中排名几乎完全相反：所有六个模型排名均发生变化，CMS最差模型成为CSS最佳模型，而一个中上CMS模型在CSS上排名最后。我们进一步发现了一个普遍的安全盲点：每个前沿模型在手术状态干预上均失败（家族D的CSS最高为17.2%），这是CMS未能揭示的发现。该指标也适用于使用工具的主体：在ReAct风格的实验中，工具使用提升了六个模型中五个模型的CSS（+2.5至+20.3个百分点），然而CSS最低的模型检索了相同的图表部分，但仍然未能更新其建议——这揭示了一种仅在反事实评估下可见的结构性响应缺陷。跨评判者复制和三名医疗专业人员的验证证实了总体发现。像CSS这样的干预性预先注册指标补充了临床AI主体的基于覆盖率评估：它们捕捉了覆盖率指标遗漏的响应性，并为未来的主体强化学习系统提供了候选的密集奖励信号。

Original abstract: Two clinical AI systems can score nearly identically on coverage-based rubrics yet behave radically differently when their patient inputs change: one updates its recommendations to match the new clinical signal, while the other produces the same output regardless. We introduce the Causal Sensitivity Score (CSS), a pre-registered interventional metric that mutates oncology tumor-board cases along five clinically meaningful dimensions - biomarker flips, prior-treatment failures, biomarker removals, surgery-status changes, and stage perturbations - and scores whether each model updates its recommendations in the pre-registered correct direction using a {0, 0.5, 1.0} scale. Benchmarked against the Consensus Match Score (CMS), a coverage-based weighted recall metric, six frontier models from three labs evaluated in single-shot inference across 224 cases rank in nearly opposite orders: all six models change rank, the CMS-worst model becomes CSS-best, and one upper-mid CMS model ranks last on CSS. We further surface a universal safety blind spot: every frontier model fails on surgery-status interventions (at most 17.2% CSS on Family D), a finding CMS does not expose. The metric also transfers to tool-using agents: in a ReAct-style experiment, tool use improves CSS for five of six models (+2.5 to +20.3 percentage points), yet the lowest-CSS model retrieves the same chart sections and still fails to update its recommendations - revealing a structural responsiveness deficit visible only under counterfactual evaluation. Cross-judge replication and three-rater medical-professional validation confirm the aggregate findings. Interventional pre-registered metrics like CSS complement coverage-based evaluation for clinical AI agents: they capture responsiveness that coverage metrics miss and offer a candidate dense reward signal for future agentic RL systems.

</details>


### [106] [On Effectiveness and Efficiency of Agentic Tool-calling and RL Training](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00135v1)
*Tong Liu,Cheng Qian,Matej Cief,Yuan He,Daniele Dan,Nikolaos Aletras,Gabriella Kazai*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 系统研究agent tool-calling的有效性与效率，揭示实现细节对评测的影响，并提出加速RL训练的两种技术，对coding agent的工具使用与训练优化直接相关。

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了工具调用评估的敏感性和RL训练的效率问题，发现评估结果对微小实现选择敏感，并提出了两种加速RL训练的技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工具调用是LLM智能体的核心能力，但现有评估缺乏标准化且RL训练存在计算浪费，亟需研究有效性和效率问题。

Method: 通过系统分析评估管道中的实现选择（随机种子、系统提示等）的影响，并识别RL训练中两个计算浪费来源；在此基础上提出两种加速技术。

Result: 评估结果对实现选择高度敏感，多轮设置下排行榜不可靠；RL训练中许多提示无学习信号且策略更新计算成本高；提出的加速技术显著提升挂钟速度且不降低性能。

Conclusion: 工具调用评估需要严格标准化，提出的加速方法有效提高了RL训练效率。

中文摘要：工具调用是现代大型语言模型（LLM）智能体的核心组成部分，赋予其超越参数知识的技能。本文沿两个互补的维度研究工具调用：有效性，即如何衡量该能力；以及效率，即如何学习该能力。在有效性方面，我们系统地分析了工具调用的评估流程，并表明结果可能对看似微小且通常未文档化的实现选择高度敏感，包括随机种子、系统提示、多轮模板构建以及如何传递先前的交互/推理历史。这些选择可能导致报告性能的显著差异，尤其是在多轮设置中，如果没有严格的标准化，排行榜排名是不可靠的。在效率方面，我们考察了标准强化学习（RL）用于工具调用的过程，并确定了两个计算浪费的来源：（i）在推出过程中，许多提示没有产生学习信号；（ii）在策略更新期间，优化产生高计算成本。在这些发现的指导下，我们引入了两种加速基于RL的工具调用训练的技术，在不降低性能的情况下实现了显著的挂钟时间加速。

Original abstract: Tool-calling is a central component of modern large language model (LLM) agents, equipping them with skills beyond their parametric knowledge. This paper studies tool-calling along two complementary axes: effectiveness, i.e., how this capability is measured, and efficiency, i.e., how it is learned. On effectiveness, we systematically analyze tool-calling evaluation pipelines and show that results can be highly sensitive to seemingly minor, often undocumented implementation choices including the random seed, system prompt, multi-turn template construction, and how prior interaction/reasoning history is carried forward. These choices can lead to substantial differences in reported performance, especially in multi-turn settings where without rigorous standardization, leaderboard rankings are unreliable. On efficiency, we examine standard reinforcement learning (RL) for tool-calling and identify two sources of computational waste: (i) during rollouts, many prompts produce no learning signal, and (ii) during policy updates, optimization incurs high computational cost. Guided by these findings, we introduce two techniques that accelerate RL-based tool-calling training, achieving substantial wall-clock speedup without degrading performance.

### [107] [LARK: Learnability-Grounded Trajectory Selection for Efficient Reasoning Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30651v1)
*Tianrun Yu,Kaixiang Zhao,Chih-Chun Chen,Amanda Hughes,Taylor W. Killian,Fenglong Ma,Weitong Zhang,Porter Jenkins*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于可学习性的轨迹选择方法，可直接用于agent经验复用与蒸馏。

TL;DR: 提出基于可学习性的推理轨迹选择方法LARK，通过引入可学习性因子和χ²正则化选择策略，平衡可学习性与分布覆盖，实验证明优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理蒸馏中的轨迹选择方法依赖启发式（如轨迹质量或模型置信度），忽略了轨迹对学生模型的可学习性，导致次优选择。

Method: 提出LARK方法，核心是可学习性因子ρ估计学生损失下降速率；引入可学习性代理高效估计ρ，并设计χ²正则化选择策略平衡可学习性与分布覆盖，提供理论保证。

Result: 在多个基础模型和推理任务上，LARK持续优于数据选择基线；诊断表明LARK分数预测下游训练效用，所选轨迹加速监督微调损失下降。

Conclusion: LARK通过可学习性引导的轨迹选择提升了推理蒸馏效果，且理论分析与实验均验证其有效性。

中文摘要：我们研究推理蒸馏中的轨迹选择，其中教师生成的推理轨迹被选择性地用作学生模型的监督。现有方法依赖于启发式策略，如轨迹质量或模型置信度，但往往忽略了轨迹对学生是否可学习。在本文中，我们提出了LARK，一种基于可学习性的推理轨迹选择方法。LARK选择学生能够高效学习且同时保持完整训练分布泛化能力的轨迹。LARK的核心是一个可学习性因子ρ，它刻画了学生训练损失下降的速率。为了高效估计该速率并保持泛化，我们引入了一个可学习性代理和一个χ²正则化的选择策略，该策略平衡了可学习性与分布覆盖，并且两者都具有关于估计误差的强理论保证。实验上，LARK在多个基础模型和推理任务上持续优于数据选择基线。诊断分析表明，LARK分数能够预测下游训练效用，并且LARK选择的轨迹能带来更快的监督微调损失下降。我们的代码可在https://github.com/Tianrun-Yu/LARK获取。

Original abstract: We study trajectory selection for reasoning distillation, where teacher-generated reasoning trajectories are selectively used as supervision for a student model. Existing methods rely on heuristics such as trajectory quality or model confidence, but they often overlook whether a trajectory is learnable by the student. In this paper, we present LARK, a learnability-grounded method for reasoning trajectory selection. LARK selects trajectories that the student can learn efficiently while preserving the generalization of the full training distribution. At the core of LARK is a learnability factor $ρ$, which characterizes the rate at which the student's training loss decreases. To estimate this rate efficiently and maintain generalization, we introduce a learnability proxy and a $χ^2$-regularized selection policy that balances learnability and distributional coverage, both with strong theoretical guarantees on their estimation error. Empirically, LARK consistently outperforms data selection baselines across multiple base models and reasoning tasks. Diagnostic analyses show that the LARK score predicts downstream training utility and that LARK-selected trajectories induce faster supervised fine-tuning loss reduction. Our code is available at https://github.com/Tianrun-Yu/LARK.

</details>

### [108] [Evolve as a Team: Collaborative Self-Evolution for LLM-based Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29790v1)
*Zhezheng Hao,Tianfu Wang,Huanshuo Dong,Ziyan Liu,Hong Wang,Xiankun Lin,Qiang Lin,Can Wang,Hande Dong,Jiawei Chen*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多智能体系统协作自我进化，直接相关agent自我改进与多agent协作

TL;DR: 提出Meta-Team框架，基于协作自我进化实现经验驱动的多智能体系统演化，通过保留执行上下文和协调通信实现多尺度改进，在六个基准测试中表现优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统在真实任务中执行时常出现失败，且设计阶段难以消除，因此需要经验驱动的系统自我进化，但MAS经验冗长复杂，难以定位改进点。

Method: 提出Meta-Team，保留每个智能体的执行上下文并协调任务后通信，使智能体交换分布式证据；在此基础上进行多尺度自我进化，优化智能体行为、智能体间协调和团队组织。

Result: 在六个长周期智能体基准测试中，Meta-Team一致优于单智能体系统、手工MAS和先前MAS演化方法，并实现了更可靠和可扩展的自我进化。

Conclusion: Meta-Team通过协作自我进化有效解决了经验驱动MAS演化中经验复杂难以利用的问题，提升了系统性能和可扩展性。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型的多智能体系统（MAS）已成为复杂和长周期任务的有效范式。然而，在真实世界任务中，MAS在执行过程中常常表现出各种失败，且这些失败在设计阶段难以消除。这激发了经验驱动的MAS演化，即系统基于自身的执行经验进行改进。然而，这种演化具有挑战性，因为MAS经验是冗长而复杂的，交织了多个智能体的执行链和通信消息，使得难以识别需要改进的内容。为应对这一挑战，我们提出了Meta-Team，一种基于协作自我进化的经验驱动MAS演化框架。Meta-Team保留每个智能体的执行上下文并协调任务后通信，使智能体能够交换用于演化的分布式证据。基于此设计，Meta-Team进行多尺度自我进化，将执行经验转化为对智能体行为、智能体间协调和团队级组织的可复用改进。在六个长周期智能体基准测试中，Meta-Team始终优于单智能体系统、手工设计的MAS以及先前的MAS演化方法；进一步分析表明，Meta-Team实现了更可靠和可扩展的MAS自我进化。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems (MAS) have emerged as an effective paradigm for complex and long-horizon tasks. However, in real-world tasks, MAS often exhibit various failures during execution and such failures are difficult to eliminate during design. This motivates experience-driven MAS evolution, where a system improves based on its own execution experience. Yet such evolution is challenging because MAS experience is prolonged and intricate, interleaving multiple agents' execution chains and communication messages, which makes it difficult to identify what should be improved. To address this challenge, we propose Meta-Team, an experience-driven MAS evolution framework based on collaborative self-evolution. Meta-Team preserves the execution context of each agent and coordinates post-task communication, enabling agents to exchange distributed evidence for evolution. Building on this design, Meta-Team conducts multi-scale self-evolution, transforming execution experience into reusable improvements to agent behaviors, inter-agent coordination, and team-level organization. Across six long-horizon agent benchmarks, Meta-Team consistently outperforms single-agent systems, hand-crafted MAS, and prior MAS evolution methods; further analyses demonstrate that Meta-Team enables more reliable and scalable MAS self-evolution.

</details>


### [109] [Social Reasoning in Machines: Investigating Collective Truth-Seeking Dynamics in Large Language Model Debate](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30391v1)
*Tom Pecher*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多智能体辩论与集体真理探索，对多agent协作有启发

TL;DR: 首次通过多智能体辩论模拟推理的论证理论，证明LLM集体推理能显著提升问卷任务的真理寻求性能，并提出新的模型基准方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证推理的论证理论（ATR）在人工智能中的有效性，即集体对抗性推理是否比个体推理更有利于真理寻求。

Method: 通过大型语言模型（LLM）进行多智能体辩论（MAD），设计认识论多样化的模型组，在问卷任务上测试并分析辩论动态。

Result: LLM-MAD显著提升真理寻求性能，性能增益基于ATR核心原理，且即使个体模型表现有限也能实现。

Conclusion: 集体推理可能普遍优于个体推理，提出的LLM-MAD基准方法可测量模型内在属性如幻觉倾向，优于静态基准。

中文摘要：人类推理长期以来被理论化为社会性运作，而非孤立的个体认知，而是通过集体对抗性话语，这一框架被称为推理的论证理论（ATR）。ATR并不将个体的“理性主义推理者”作为寻求真理的主要载体，而是将真理重新概念化为社会认识论的一种涌现特性：即不完美的个体推理在辩论的对抗压力下被精炼的产物。这种集体智慧的分布式方法引导人类达到了越来越高的认知高度，并支撑着所有民主制度的基本原则。本论文首次通过大型语言模型（LLM）的多智能体辩论（MAD）模拟ATR，开创了新局面。通过严格的实证分析，我们证明，当正确设计一组认识论多样化的模型时，LLM-MAD可以显著提高基于问卷的任务中的真理寻求性能，即使个别辩论参与者的独立表现有限。此外，我们提供了强有力的实证证据，表明这种性能提升在机制上基于ATR的核心原理，这表明集体推理可能普遍优于个体推理，而非生物学或进化中的偶然现象。最后，基于我们对辩论动态的分析，我们提出了一种新的基准测试方法，利用LLM-MAD来测量内在模型属性（如幻觉倾向），从而以当前静态基准测试方法无法支持的方式比较模型。

Original abstract: Human reasoning has long been theorised to operate socially, not through isolated individual cognition, but through collective adversarial discourse, a framework known as the Argumentative Theory of Reasoning (ATR). Rather than relying on individual "intellectualist reasoners" as the primary vehicle for truth-seeking, ATR reconceptualises truth as an emergent property of social epistemology: the product of imperfect individual reasoning refined under the adversarial pressure of debate. This distributed method of collective intelligence has guided humanity to ever-greater epistemic heights and underpins the foundational principles of all democratic systems. This thesis breaks new ground by, for the first time, simulating ATR through the multi-agent debate (MAD) of large language models (LLMs). With rigorous empirical analysis, we demonstrate that, when correctly engineering an epistemically diverse set of models, LLM-MAD can significantly improve truth-seeking performance on questionnaire-based tasks, even when individual debate participants exhibit limited standalone performance. Furthermore, we present strong empirical evidence that this performance gain is mechanistically grounded in the central principles of ATR, suggesting that collective reasoning may be universally favourable over individualist reasoning, rather than a quirk in biology or evolution. Finally, drawing on our analysis of debate dynamics, we propose a novel benchmarking methodology that leverages LLM-MAD to measure intrinsic model properties (such as hallucination propensity) in order to compare models in ways that current static benchmarking approaches cannot support.

</details>


### [110] [Evolutionary Dynamics of Cooperation in Next-Generation LLM Agent Systems: A Cross-Provider Empirical Extension](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29874v2)
*Francisco León Zúñiga Bolívar*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多智能体博弈合作演化研究，对agent协作策略有启发

TL;DR: 研究下一代LLM智能体在竞争性多智能体环境中是否继承合作偏见，发现合作偏见持续存在，但跨提供商差异显著，噪声仍是普遍挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究下一代LLM智能体是否会继承前代合作偏见，以及规模和提供商多样性如何影响竞争性多智能体环境中的均衡行为。

Method: 将Willis等人的基准扩展到2025-2026年的四个前沿模型，使用三种提示风格和四种群体组成，应用相同协议。

Result: 合作偏见持续存在（10/12模型-提示组合偏向合作均衡）；跨提供商差异显著（Gemini 2.5 Flash在偏置条件下达77%攻击性均衡，GPT-5.4 Mini在自我改进下达70%合作均衡）；对攻击性能力平等的支持部分；噪声鲁棒性证据不显著。

Conclusion: 提供商身份是均衡结果的最强相关因素，噪声仍是普遍挑战，与模型大小或年代无关。

中文摘要：下一代LLM智能体是否会继承其前身中记录的合作偏见，还是规模和提供商多样性会重塑竞争性多智能体环境中的均衡行为？Willis等人使用进化博弈论和迭代囚徒困境（IPD）为这个问题建立了一个基准，发现ChatGPT-4o和Claude 3.5 Sonnet中一致的合作偏见。我们将该基准扩展到2025-2026年发布的四个前沿模型——Claude Sonnet 4.6、Gemini 2.5 Flash、Gemini 3.1 Pro和GPT-5.4 Mini——在三种提示风格（默认、散文、自我改进）和四种群体组成（平衡和有偏见，有噪声和无噪声）下应用相同的协议。合作偏见在提供商之间持续存在（H1）：在平衡无噪声条件下，十二个模型-提示组合中有十个偏向合作均衡。跨提供商的差异很大（H3）：Gemini 2.5 Flash在有偏见条件下达到高达77%的攻击性均衡，而GPT-5.4 Mini在自我改进下达到70%的合作均衡。对攻击性能力平等的支持是部分的（H2）：自我改进提高了所有模型的ICD，Gemini 3.1 Pro Refine达到了数据集中最高的ICD（0.925），但默认和散文提示没有表现出系统的缩小。关于噪声鲁棒性的证据方向上是积极的，但没有得到稳健确认（H4）：在每条件下n=500次Moran迭代中，Claude Sonnet 4.6的平均噪声敏感度约为6个百分点，而Claude 3.5 Sonnet为13个百分点，但一旦传播了前身未报告的抽样误差，这一跨研究差距在统计上并不显著。提供商身份，而非模型代次，是均衡结果的最强相关因素；无论模型大小或年代，噪声仍然是一个普遍挑战。

Original abstract: Do next-generation LLM agents inherit the cooperative biases documented in their predecessors, or does scale and provider diversity reshape equilibrium behaviour in competitive multi-agent settings? Willis et al. established a benchmark for this question using evolutionary game theory and the Iterated Prisoner's Dilemma (IPD), finding consistent cooperative biases in ChatGPT-4o and Claude 3.5 Sonnet. We extend this benchmark to four frontier models released in 2025-2026 - Claude Sonnet 4.6, Gemini 2.5 Flash, Gemini 3.1 Pro, and GPT-5.4 Mini - applying the identical protocol across three prompting styles (Default, Prose, Self-Refine) and four population compositions (balanced and biased, with and without noise). Cooperative bias persists across providers (H1): ten of twelve model-prompt combinations favour cooperative equilibria in balanced noiseless conditions. Cross-provider divergence is substantial (H3): Gemini 2.5 Flash reaches up to 77% aggressive equilibria under biased conditions, while GPT-5.4 Mini reaches 70% cooperative equilibria under Self-Refine. Support for aggressive capability parity is partial (H2): Self-Refine raises ICD in all models and Gemini 3.1 Pro Refine achieves the highest ICD in the dataset (0.925), but Default and Prose prompts show no systematic narrowing. Evidence on noise robustness is directionally positive but not robustly confirmed (H4): with n=500 Moran iterations per condition, average noise sensitivity is about 6 percentage points for Claude Sonnet 4.6 versus 13 pp for Claude 3.5 Sonnet, but this cross-study gap is not statistically significant once the predecessor's unreported sampling error is propagated. Provider identity, rather than model generation, is the strongest correlate of equilibrium outcomes; noise remains a universal challenge regardless of model size or vintage.

</details>


### [111] [Discovering Cooperative Pipelines: Autoresearch for Sequential Social Dilemmas](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30003v1)
*Víctor Gallego*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 自动代码优化pipeline发现，coding agent自主修改代码，直接相关。

TL;DR: 提出一种两级自动研究框架，外层AI研究者自动优化内层LLM策略合成流水线，在序贯社会困境中根据福利目标实现更好的合作，并发现目标依赖的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索自动研究能否在合作型多智能体系统中超越手工设计，并揭示不同福利目标下流水线设计的差异。

Method: 使用外层研究者智能体（编码智能体）自动修改内层LLM策略合成系统的组件（提示、反馈函数、库、迭代逻辑），并通过评估决定保留，应用于清洁和采集游戏，测试不同LLM和福利目标。

Result: 研究者智能体在功利效率和罗尔斯最大化最小两种目标下均优于手工基线，方差更小，且仅在最大化最小目标下引入显式公平机制。

Conclusion: 自动研究能根据福利目标自动发现针对性机制，支持信息设计视角，即研究者根据目标选择向合成器揭示的信息。

中文摘要：我们研究用于合作的两级自动研究：外层循环的AI智能体自主重新设计多智能体序贯社会困境（SSD）的LLM策略合成系统的内层循环流水线。一个研究者智能体（作为编码智能体运行）读取内层循环源代码，编辑系统提示、反馈函数、辅助库和迭代逻辑，运行评估，并决定保留什么，遵循自动研究范式。在两个游戏（Cleanup和Gathering）、两个策略合成器LLM以及两个福利目标（功利效率和罗尔斯最大化最小原则）上，研究者可靠地超越了手工设计的基线，显著缩小了运行间方差，并优于仅优化提示的方法。发现的流水线依赖于目标：仅在最大化最小原则下，研究者才会向合成器流水线注入显式的公平机制，而这种机制在其自身目标无关的系统提示和所有效率优化的流水线中都不存在。这支持了一种信息设计解读，即研究者根据福利目标选择向有限理性的合成器揭示什么。代码见 https://github.com/vicgalle/autoresearch-social-dilemmas。

Original abstract: We study two-level autoresearch for cooperation: an outer-loop AI agent autonomously redesigns the inner-loop pipeline of an LLM policy-synthesis system for multi-agent Sequential Social Dilemmas (SSDs). A researcher agent $\mathcal{R}$ (run as a coding agent) reads the inner-loop source code, edits system prompts, feedback functions, helper libraries, and iteration logic, runs evaluations, and decides what to keep, following the autoresearch paradigm. Across two games (Cleanup and Gathering), two policy-synthesizer LLMs, and two welfare objectives (utilitarian efficiency and Rawlsian maximin), the researcher reliably exceeds hand-designed baselines, sharply tightens run-to-run variance, and outperforms prompt-only optimization. The discovered pipelines are objective-dependent: only under maximin does the researcher inject an explicit fairness mechanism into synthesizer pipelines, a class of mechanism that is absent from its own objective-agnostic system prompt and from every efficiency-optimized pipeline. This supports an information-design reading in which the researcher chooses what to reveal to the boundedly rational synthesizer as a function of the welfare objective. Code at https://github.com/vicgalle/autoresearch-social-dilemmas.

</details>


### [112] [When Cloud Agents Meet Device Agents: Lessons from Hybrid Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30102v1)
*Corrado Rainone,Davide Belli,Bence Major,Arash Behboodi*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 混合多agent系统设计，直接关于agent架构权衡，对agent系统设计有重要可迁移价值

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了混合多智能体系统的设计空间，发现最优架构高度任务依赖，且更大计算量不一定带来更好性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合多智能体系统在任务准确性、成本和能耗之间紧密耦合，缺乏通用设计原则，需要系统性的研究。

Method: 改造两种代表性MAS架构以支持混合推理，并通过实验研究设计选择对帕累托前沿的影响。

Result: SLM可受益于LLM辅助，但最优架构高度任务依赖，且更大计算量并不一致提升性能。

Conclusion: 混合MAS设计需权衡任务依赖性，前沿计算量并非性能保证。

中文摘要：智能体AI推理的设计空间包含两个极端：通常部署在云端、在广泛任务上提供强大性能但成本高昂的前沿大型语言模型（LLM），以及成本效益更高、适合设备端推理的小型语言模型（SLM）。结合设备端和云端模型的混合多智能体系统（MAS）提供了一个有前景的中间地带，但同时也引入了一个复杂且理解不足的设计空间，其中任务准确性、货币成本和边缘能耗紧密耦合；在缺乏通用设计原则的情况下，混合组件尽管不是最常见的选择，通常是通过针对特定领域的临时决策引入的。在这项工作中，我们更系统地审视了这一设计空间。我们改造了两种代表性的MAS架构以支持混合推理，并研究了单个设计选择如何沿功耗、成本和性能的帕累托前沿移动操作点。我们的研究结果描绘了混合MAS设计的细致图景：虽然SLM可以有效受益于LLM的辅助，但最优架构高度依赖于任务，且更大的前沿计算量并不一致地转化为更好的性能。

Original abstract: The design space of agentic AI inference spans two extremes: frontier large language models (LLMs), typically hosted in the cloud and offering strong performance across a wide range of tasks at substantially high cost, and more cost-efficient small language models (SLMs), which are amenable to on-device inference. Hybrid multi-agent systems (MASs) combining on-device and cloud models offer a promising middle ground, but they also introduce a complex and poorly understood design space in which task accuracy, monetary cost, and edge energy consumption are tightly coupled; in the absence of general design principles, hybrid components, although not the most prevalent choice, are typically introduced through ad hoc decisions tailored to specific domains. In this work, we examine this design space more systematically. We adapt two representative MAS architectures to support hybrid inference and study how individual design choices shift the operating point along the Pareto frontier of power, cost, and performance. Our findings paint a nuanced picture of hybrid MAS design: while SLMs can effectively benefit from LLM assistance, the optimal architecture is highly task-dependent, and greater frontier-level compute does not consistently translate to better performance.

### [113] [Unifying Temporal and Structural Credit Assignment in LLM-Based Multi-Agent Prompt Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30227v1)
*Wenwu Li,Yuran Song,Mingze Zhao,Bo Jin,Wenhao Li*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 提出多agent系统的时域和结构信用分配方法，用于prompt优化，直接相关agent协作与规划。

TL;DR: 提出时间与结构信用分配方法，结合离散语言化块坐标下降算法，通过分解误差信号并交替优化角色提示和聚合协议，显著降低了多智能体系统的查询复杂度并提升了推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统优化面临计算图离散非可微和全局监督信号稀疏的挑战，现有黑盒优化器无法有效归因轨迹级错误，导致低效高方差探索，需要结构性的归纳偏差来分离误差信号。

Method: 通过时间信用（状态空间瓶颈识别关键轮次）和结构信用（固定角色策略隔离智能体贡献）分解目标，并引入离散语言化块坐标下降算法，利用LLM生成的代理梯度交替优化角色提示和聚合协议。

Result: 在多个推理基准测试中，该方法在提高性能的同时大幅降低了查询复杂度。

Conclusion: 提供了一种有原则且可解释的自我改进多智能体系统路径，有效解决了归因和优化效率问题。

中文摘要：尽管多智能体系统（MAS）通过协作交互赋予了大型语言模型处理复杂推理任务的能力，但由于计算图的离散、非可微性质以及全局监督信号的稀疏性，优化其动态过程仍然是一个艰巨的挑战。现有的黑盒优化器难以将轨迹级别的失败归因于特定的局部组件，导致低效的高方差探索。我们认为，可处理的MAS优化需要结构性的归纳偏差来分离误差信号。我们提出了时间与结构信用分配，该方法沿两个轴分解目标：（i）时间信用，使用状态空间瓶颈来识别关键轮次；（ii）结构信用，使用固定角色策略来隔离智能体贡献。利用这些分解后的信号，我们引入了一种离散的、语言化的块坐标下降算法用于迭代优化。它不是进行无差别的全局更新，而是交替优化角色提示和聚合协议，使用LLM生成的“代理梯度”仅针对识别出的薄弱环节。在不同的推理基准测试中，我们的方法在提高性能的同时大幅降低了查询复杂度，为自我改进的MAS提供了一条有原则且可解释的路径。

Original abstract: While Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) empower Large Language Models to tackle complex reasoning tasks through collaborative interaction, optimizing their dynamics remains a formidable challenge due to the discrete, non-differentiable nature of the computation graph and the sparsity of global supervisory signals. Existing black-box optimizers struggle to attribute trajectory-level failure to specific local components, resulting in inefficient, high-variance exploration. We argue that tractable MAS optimization needs structural inductive biases to disentangle error signals. We propose temporal and structural credit assignment, which decomposes the objective along two axes: (i) temporal credit, using state-space bottlenecks to identify critical rounds, and (ii) structural credit, using stationary role policies to isolate agent contributions. Leveraging these decomposed signals, we introduce a discrete, verbalized block coordinate descent algorithm for iterative refinement. Rather than indiscriminate global updates, it alternates between optimizing role prompts and aggregation protocols, using LLM-generated "proxy gradients" to target only the identified weak links. Across diverse reasoning benchmarks, our approach substantially reduces query complexity while improving performance, providing a principled and interpretable path toward self-improving MAS.

</details>


### [114] [Specialize Roles, Mix Deployments: Pushing the Cost-Accuracy Frontier of LLM Agent Teams](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20629v1)
*Yinsicheng Jiang,Liang Cheng,Yeqi Huang,Yufan Zhao,Zhan Lu,Li Dong,Wenda Li,Edoardo Ponti,Luo Mai*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 提出agent团队角色分配和部署的benchmark，直接研究多agent系统成本与准确性。

TL;DR: 提出AgentCARD，一个用于评估多角色LLM团队在角色分配和部署模式下成本-准确性权衡的基准测试套件，发现异构团队和混合部署能显著提升效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试仅评估固定模型或固定智能体配置，无法为多角色团队的成本-准确性最优部署提供有效指导。

Method: AgentCARD包含角色分解的评估框架、统一的API/自托管成本模型、帕累托前沿分析以及基于Shapley值的角色瓶颈诊断工具。

Result: 异构团队在成本-准确性前沿上始终优于同构团队，最高提升44%的准确性或降低12倍成本；最佳角色分配具有领域依赖性，部分领域为规划者瓶颈，部分为执行者瓶颈。

Conclusion: AgentCARD可扩展至包含验证等额外角色的工作流，并支持持续评估，为多角色LLM团队的优化部署提供了有效工具。

中文摘要：LLM智能体越来越多地被部署为多角色团队，其中任务被划分到诸如规划者、执行者和验证者等专门角色中。在这些系统中，成本和准确性不再是单个模型的属性：它们取决于每个角色由哪个模型担任以及模型的托管位置，包括API、自托管和混合部署。现有的智能体基准测试通常评估固定模型或固定智能体配置，因此对于成本-准确性最优部署提供的指导有限。我们提出AgentCARD，这是一个角色感知的基准测试套件，用于评估LLM智能体团队在角色分配和部署模式方面的表现。AgentCARD结合了角色分解的评估框架、统一的API/自托管成本模型、帕累托前沿分析以及基于Shapley值的诊断工具，用于识别角色瓶颈。我们的评估表明，异构团队始终占据成本-准确性前沿。与成本等效的同构团队相比，它们将准确性提高了高达44%，或者通过混合部署，以每任务成本低至12倍的方式匹配最强的同构团队。我们进一步发现，最佳角色分配是领域相关的：一些领域是规划者瓶颈，而其他领域是执行者瓶颈。最后，AgentCARD超越了规划者-执行者团队，扩展到具有验证等额外角色的工作流，并支持随着新领域和团队结构的出现而进行持续评估。我们的代码已在 https://github.com/Auto-CAP/AgentCAP 发布。

Original abstract: LLM agents are increasingly deployed as multi-role teams, where tasks are divided across specialized roles such as planner, executor, and verifier. In these systems, cost and accuracy are no longer properties of a single model: they depend on which model fills each role and where it is hosted, including API, self-hosted, and hybrid deployment. Existing agentic benchmarks typically evaluate fixed models or fixed agent configurations, and therefore offer limited guidance for cost-accuracy-optimal deployment. We introduce AgentCARD, a role-aware benchmark suite for evaluating LLM agent teams across role assignment and deployment mode. AgentCARD combines a role-decomposed evaluation harness, a unified API/self-hosted cost model, Pareto-frontier analysis, and a Shapley-based diagnostic for identifying role bottlenecks. Our evaluation shows that heterogeneous teams consistently occupy the cost-accuracy frontier. They improve accuracy by up to $44\%$ over cost-equivalent homogeneous teams, or match the strongest homogeneous team at up to $12\times$ lower per-task cost through hybrid deployment. We further find that the best role assignment is domain-dependent: some domains are planner-bottlenecked, while others are executor-bottlenecked. Finally, AgentCARD extends beyond planner--executor teams to workflows with additional roles such as verification, and supports continual evaluation as new domains and team structures emerge. Our code is released at: https://github.com/Auto-CAP/AgentCAP

</details>

# cs.RO [[Back]](#toc)

### [115] [Structured interactions improve distributed coordination beyond model scaling in a real-world multi-robot system](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30383v1)
*Junping Wang,Zhizhong Zhang,Yongqiang Tang,Geng Zheng,Jiaming Zhang,Shiji Song,Yanmei Li,Yushan Ma*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 多机器人协调中交互结构优于模型规模，发现可迁移到多agent协作设计

TL;DR: 在多机器人运输与映射任务中，将通信拓扑从全连接改为模块化层次结构带来了47个百分点的性能提升，而将神经网络隐藏层大小翻倍最多只提升9个百分点，表明交互结构比模型规模更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在固定硬件预算下，调整多机器人间的通信拓扑结构（系统级设计）与增加单个机器人机载模型规模（扩展个体能力）相比，哪种方式能带来更大的性能提升。

Method: 在10个物理机器人上执行运输与映射任务，比较全连接与模块化层次两种通信拓扑，以及不同神经网络隐藏层大小（2倍变化）的性能，共60次运行（每种条件5次），并使用嵌套混合效应模型和独立SMAC复制进行验证。

Result: 切换拓扑结构带来47个百分点的标准化性能提升（满分100），而增加隐藏层大小最多只提升9个百分点；嵌套混合效应模型显示拓扑的模型拟合改进远超规模效应，且在SMAC复制中一致，模拟外推显示超过1024隐藏单元后性能饱和。

Conclusion: 在测试的系统与任务中，交互结构对性能的主导作用远大于模型规模，但该结论的量化泛化性仍需进一步研究。

中文摘要：扩展单个机器人能力是常见但昂贵的。这里我们在现实世界的多机器人协调中研究了一个系统级设计问题：在给定的硬件预算下，改变机器人之间的通信结构是否比增加机载模型大小带来更大的收益？我们使用一个具有10个物理机器人的代表性运输与映射任务（每个条件5次运行，总共60次运行），发现从全连接切换到模块化层次交互将标准化性能提高了47个百分点（0-100），而将神经网络隐藏层大小加倍最多只能提高9个百分点。嵌套混合效应模型比较显示，拓扑结构的模型拟合改进远大于规模。该模式在独立的SMAC复制中得到确认；异构基准重新分析提供了次要支持性一致性检查，而非主要证据。在模拟校准的外推中观察到超过1024个隐藏单元的性能饱和，而非直接在硬件上。这些结果表明，在测试的系统和任务设置中，交互结构可以发挥主导作用，而更广泛的量化泛化仍有待建立。

Original abstract: Scaling individual robot capabilities is common but costly. Here we investigate a system-level design question in real-world multi-robot coordination: given matched hardware budgets, does restructuring communication among robots yield larger gains than increasing onboard model size? Using a representative transport-and-mapping task with 10 physical robots (5 runs per condition, 60 runs total), we find that switching from fully connected to modular hierarchical interactions improves normalised performance by 47 points (0--100), whereas doubling neural network hidden size yields at most 9 points. Nested mixed-effects model comparisons show a substantially larger improvement in model fit for topology than for scale. The pattern is confirmed in independent SMAC replications; heterogeneous benchmark reanalyses provide secondary supporting consistency checks rather than primary evidence. Performance saturation beyond 1024 hidden units is observed in simulation-calibrated extrapolation, not directly on hardware. These results indicate that interaction structure can play a dominant role within the tested system and task setting, while broader quantitative generalisation remains to be established.

</details>


### [116] [VLA-Pro: Cross-Task Procedural Memory Transfer for Vision-Language-Action Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29562v1)
*Shengyu Si,Yuanzhuo Lu,Ruimeng Yang,Ziyi Ye,Zuxuan Wu,Yu-Gang Jiang*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 提出过程记忆存储与检索用于跨任务迁移，通用agent记忆机制，可应用于coding agent。

TL;DR: VLA-Pro通过存储和检索任务特定的程序性记忆（LoRA适配器）来增强VLA模型的跨任务泛化，在仿真和真实世界任务中取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型在需要跨对象、场景和动作模式迁移经验的新任务上泛化能力不足。

Method: 提出VLA-Pro框架，训练时存储任务特定的LoRA适配器作为程序性记忆，推理时基于多模态上下文检索并动态融合这些记忆来生成动作。

Result: 在RoboTwin、RLBench和真实世界任务上，VLA-Pro一致提升跨任务泛化，仿真中相对改进高达207%，真实世界成功率从5.8%升至65.0%。

Conclusion: 程序性记忆检索与适应为迁移操作经验到新任务提供了有效机制，同时保持模块化和执行稳定性。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在通用机器人操作方面显示出强大潜力，但它们仍然难以泛化到需要跨对象、场景和动作模式迁移相关经验的新任务。本文提出VLA-Pro，一个即插即用的框架，旨在通过在训练时存储与任务相关的程序性记忆并在推理时迁移这些记忆来增强跨任务泛化。具体来说，VLA-Pro在训练期间将任务特定的LoRA适配器存储为参数化的程序性记忆。在推理时，VLA-Pro基于当前多模态上下文检索相关的程序性记忆，并动态融合这些记忆以生成当前的动作块。在RoboTwin、RLBench和真实世界操作任务上的实验表明，VLA-Pro在多个骨干网络上一致地提升了跨任务泛化能力，在仿真中实现了高达207%的相对改进，并将真实世界成功率从5.8%提高到65.0%。这些结果表明，程序性记忆检索和适应为将操作经验迁移到新任务提供了一种有效的机制，同时保持了模块化和执行稳定性。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action~(VLA) models have shown strong potential for general-purpose robotic manipulation, yet they still struggle to generalize to unseen tasks that necessitate transferring relevant experience across objects, scenes, and action patterns. This paper proposes VLA-Pro, a plug-and-play framework designed to enhance cross-task generalization by storing task-relevant procedural memories at training time and transferring these memories during inference. Specifically, VLA-Pro stores task-specific LoRA adapters as parameterized procedural memories during training. At inference time, VLA-Pro retrieves relevant procedural memories based on the current multi-modal context and dynamically fuses these memories for generating the current action chunk. Experiments on RoboTwin, RLBench, and real-world manipulation tasks show that VLA-Pro consistently improves cross-task generalization across multiple backbones, achieving up to a 207% relative improvement in simulation and increasing real-world success rate from 5.8% to 65.0%. These results suggest that procedural memory retrieval and adaptation provide an effective mechanism for transferring manipulation experience to novel tasks while preserving modularity and execution stability.

</details>


### [117] [RoboWits: Unexpected Challenges for Robotic Creative Problem Solving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30326v1)
*Chunru Lin,Hongxin Zhang,Fenghao Yu,Zhehuan Chen,Thomas L. Griffiths,Yejin Choi,David Held,Chuang Gan*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 多agent协作自动生成推理任务，可迁移至agent评估设计

TL;DR: RoboWits是一个双臂机器人基准测试，通过自动化任务生成流水线创建推理中心化意外场景，评估机器人认知推理、创造性工具使用和鲁棒性，发现预训练VLA在变异任务上表现脆弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人基准测试侧重于技能执行，缺乏对认知推理能力的评估，因此需要专门测试机器人推理、适应和创造力的基准。

Method: 提出一个多智能体协作框架的自动化任务生成流水线，包括种子任务生成与验证、度量生成、场景生成和任务变异，构建了30个种子任务和208个变异任务，覆盖几何、材料和装配推理。

Result: 预训练VLA在种子任务上单任务微调后有初步成功，但在变异任务上表现困难，显示出对推理、策略适应和鲁棒性要求的脆弱性。

Conclusion: RoboWits揭示了当前机器人策略在认知推理和适应意外条件方面的显著不足，为未来研究提供了方向。

中文摘要：在现实环境运行的机器人必须具备在意外挑战下推理、适应和创造性解决问题的能力。然而，当前的机器人基准测试主要强调技能级执行，对此类认知推理能力的洞察有限。我们提出了RoboWits，一个双臂机器人基准测试，旨在系统评估认知推理、创造性工具使用以及对意外条件的鲁棒性。为了实现高质量推理中心化意外场景的可扩展构建，我们提出了一个自动化任务生成流水线，该流水线被构建为多智能体协作框架，包括种子任务生成与验证智能体、度量生成智能体、场景生成智能体和任务变异智能体。利用该流水线，我们整理了30个不同的种子任务和208个带变异及分级难度的任务，涵盖几何、材料和装配推理。我们对流行的机器人策略、预训练VLA和oracle状态规划器进行了基准测试。结果显示显著的性能差距：预训练VLA在单任务微调后在种子任务上表现出初步成功，但在变异任务上表现不佳，这暗示了它们在需要推理、策略适应以及对欺骗或受限环境鲁棒性的操作任务中的脆弱性。项目页面可见于https://umass-embodied-agi.github.io/RoboWits。

Original abstract: The ability to reason, adapt, and creatively solve problems under unexpected challenges is essential for robots operating in real-world environments. However, current robotic benchmarks primarily emphasize skill-level execution and provide limited insight into such cognitive reasoning capabilities. We introduce RoboWits, a bi-manual robotic benchmark designed to systematically evaluate cognitive reasoning, creative tool use, and robustness to unexpected conditions. To enable scalable construction of high-quality reasoning-centric unexpected scenarios, we propose an automated task generation pipeline formulated as a multi-agent cooperative framework, comprising agents for seed task generation and verification, metric generation, scene generation, and task mutation. Using the pipeline, we curated 30 diverse seed tasks and 208 tasks with mutations and graded difficulty across geometry, material, and assembly-based reasoning. We benchmark popular robot policies, pre-trained VLAs, and oracle-state planners. Our results reveal a significant performance gap: while pre-trained VLAs exhibit preliminary success on seed tasks after single-task fine-tuning, they struggle to perform on mutated tasks, implying their brittleness in manipulation tasks requiring reasoning, strategy adaptation, and robustness to deceptive or constrained environments. Project page is available at https://umass-embodied-agi.github.io/RoboWits.

### [118] [Learning User-Aware Recall: Personalized Retrieval in Long-Term Conversational Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00017v2)
*ZhiShu Jiang,Haibo Liu,Xin Shen,Guanqiang QI,Chenxi Miao,Weikang Li,Liwei Qian,Xin Pei,Jizhou Huang*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 个性化记忆检索优化，直接相关agent长期记忆与检索增强

TL;DR: 提出PPRO框架，通过用户画像引导的排名和查询重写优化，提升长期对话代理的记忆检索个性化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆增强LLM代理的检索多依赖查询中心相似性或固定排名，忽略用户条件相关性。

Method: 构建情景和语义记忆库，推导用户画像作为显式先验用于排名；使用Group Relative Policy Optimization训练查询重写器，以检索和答案质量反馈优化检索。

Result: 在LoCoMo和LongMemEval-S数据集上，PPRO一致优于免训练和基于训练的基线。

Conclusion: 检索优化是个性化长期记忆的关键，用户画像和检索导向重写均对性能有显著贡献。

中文摘要：长期对话代理期望能记住过去的交互，但只有在正确的证据被召回给正确的用户时，记忆才是有用的。现有的记忆增强型LLM代理在构建紧凑的记忆库方面取得了进展，但检索仍然通常由以查询为中心的相似性或固定排名规则驱动，用户条件相关性未被充分探索。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了Profile-guided Personalized Retrieval Optimization (PPRO)，一个以检索为中心的框架，使记忆检索既用户感知又可优化。PPRO从对话历史中构建情景和语义记忆库，并从累积的记忆中推导出用户画像。该画像作为显式的个性化先验在记忆排名中使用，允许检索考虑稳定的用户属性、偏好和关系。PPRO进一步使用Group Relative Policy Optimization训练查询重写器，使用证据检索质量和下游答案质量作为反馈，同时保持记忆库和答案模型固定。在LoCoMo和LongMemEval-S上的实验显示，与免训练记忆系统和基于训练的基线相比，持续改进。消融研究进一步表明，画像引导的排名和检索导向的重写都对性能有显著贡献，突出了检索优化作为个性化长期记忆使用的关键因素。

Original abstract: Long-term conversational agents are expected to remember past interactions, but memory is useful only when the right evidence is recalled for the right user. Existing memory-augmented LLM agents have made progress in building compact memory banks, yet retrieval is still often driven by query-centered similarity or fixed ranking rules, leaving user-conditioned relevance underexplored. To address this gap, we propose Profile-guided Personalized Retrieval Optimization (PPRO), a retrieval-centric framework that makes memory retrieval both user-aware and optimizable. PPRO builds episodic and semantic memory banks from dialogue histories and derives a user profile from accumulated memories. The profile serves as an explicit personalized prior in memory ranking, allowing retrieval to account for stable user attributes, preferences, and relationships. PPRO further trains a query rewriter with Group Relative Policy Optimization, using both evidence retrieval quality and downstream answer quality as feedback while keeping the memory banks and answer model fixed. Experiments on LoCoMo and LongMemEval-S show consistent gains over training-free memory systems and training-based baselines. Ablation studies further show that both profile-guided ranking and retrieval-oriented rewriting contribute substantially to performance, highlighting retrieval optimization as a key factor in personalized long-term memory use.

</details>

### [119] [Relevance as a Vulnerability: How Web Retrieval Degrades Safety Alignment in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29224v1)
*Aditya Nawal,Manit Baser,Mohan Gurusamy*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 诊断检索增强agent的安全退化，对agent安全设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出AgentREVEAL框架分析检索导致LLM智能体安全性退化，发现单步绑定集成和安全来源均会增加有害顺从性，揭示安全-效用权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作表明检索增强智能体会增加对有害请求的顺从性，但缺乏系统性诊断框架来分析其成因，因此需要研究检索集成方式和内容属性如何影响安全性。

Method: 设计AgentREVEAL诊断框架，从检索集成方式（单步/多步）和检索内容属性（来源立场、相关性等）两个维度分析安全性退化，并构建HarmURLBench基准（含1405个URL和320个有害行为）支持评估。

Result: 单步绑定工具调用与响应生成放大有害输出；安全来源（如警告页面）使有害顺从性平均增加25%；相关性是两种漏洞的共同激活条件；前沿闭源模型也呈现类似模式。

Conclusion: 检索在提升智能体能力的同时削弱了安全性，存在固有的安全-效用权衡，HarmURLBench为后续研究提供评估工具。

中文摘要：AI智能体通过外部工具（如网络检索）增强大型语言模型，使其能够提供基于事实且最新的响应。然而，将外部内容引入生成流程可能会削弱控制模型输出的安全对齐机制。先前研究表明，在智能体中启用检索会增加对有害请求的顺从性。我们引入了AgentREVEAL，一个用于分析LLM智能体中检索诱导的安全性退化的诊断框架。该框架考察两个轴：检索如何集成到智能体流程中，以及检索内容的属性。在集成轴上，我们发现将工具调用和响应生成绑定在单个步骤中会放大有害输出。在内容轴上，我们揭示了安全来源悖论：即使是反对性或面向安全的来源，例如包含警告或风险免责声明的页面，与无检索基线相比，也会使有害顺从性平均增加25%。最后，我们表明相关性是这两种漏洞的共同激活条件。类似模式出现在前沿闭源模型中，并且在几种代表性流程干预下，有害顺从性仍然较高，一些智能体在自主检索下也会进入这种状态。由于相关性也是检索有用性的原因，这些结果揭示了检索启用型智能体的安全-效用权衡。我们引入了HarmURLBench，一个包含1,405个真实世界URL和320个有害行为的基准，以支持未来评估。

Original abstract: AI agents augment large language models with external tools such as web retrieval, enabling grounded and up-to-date responses. However, incorporating external content into the generation pipeline can weaken the safety alignment mechanisms that govern model outputs. Prior work shows that enabling retrieval in agents increases compliance with harmful requests. We introduce AgentREVEAL, a diagnostic framework for analyzing retrieval-induced safety degradation in LLM agents. The framework examines two axes: how retrieval is integrated into the agent pipeline and the properties of the retrieved content. Along the integration axis, we find that binding tool invocation and response generation in a single step amplifies harmful outputs. Along the content axis, we uncover the Safe Source Paradox: even oppositional or safety-oriented sources, such as pages containing warnings or risk disclaimers, can increase harmful compliance by an average of 25% compared to the no-retrieval baseline. Finally, we show that relevance acts as a shared activation condition for both vulnerabilities. Similar patterns appear on frontier closed models, and harmful compliance remains elevated under several representative pipeline interventions, with some agents also entering this regime under autonomous retrieval. Because relevance is also what makes retrieval useful, these results expose a safety-utility trade-off for retrieval-enabled agents. We introduce HarmURLBench, a benchmark containing 1,405 real-world URLs paired with 320 harmful behaviors to support future evaluations.

</details>


### [120] [OmniRetrieval: Unified Retrieval across Heterogeneous Knowledge Sources](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29250v1)
*Jinheon Baek,Soyeong Jeong,Sangwoo Park,Woongyeong Yeo,Minki Kang,Patara Trirat,Heejun Lee,Sung Ju Hwang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 统一检索框架处理异构源，作为agent检索组件方法，可迁移。

TL;DR: OmniRetrieval是一个通用检索框架，能处理自然语言查询并分发到各知识源的原生引擎，在多种结构的知识源上超越单源模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检索器只能处理单一知识源且接口不兼容，导致知识碎片化；简单统一会丢失各源独有的结构特性，因此需要一种保留结构多样性的统一接口。

Method: 提出OmniRetrieval框架，输入自然语言查询，自动识别合适知识源，然后生成源原生查询并分派到对应的原生执行引擎处理。

Result: 在13个数据集、309个知识库（含文本、关系、图结构）的基准测试中，OmniRetrieval的性能超过了所有单源基线方法。

Conclusion: OmniRetrieval能作为异构知识源的通用接口，在保持各源结构价值的同时实现高效跨源检索。

中文摘要：真实世界的信息需求需要访问结构多样的知识源，从非结构化文本和关系表到知识图谱和属性图。然而，现有的检索器一次只能在一个固定的查询语言下操作一个源，使得更广泛的知识景观因不兼容的接口而碎片化。一个自然的统一尝试是将这些源合并到一个共享空间，但这会抹去每个源赋予其表达能力的结构特性（如模式、本体、组合操作符）。因此，多样化知识的有效检索不需要同质化，而需要一个能够以每个源自身方式与之交互的覆盖层。为了实现这一目标，我们提出了OmniRetrieval，一个框架，它接受任何自然语言查询，识别合适的知识源，并将源原生查询分派到其原生执行引擎。在一个跨越13个数据集和309个不同知识库（涵盖文本、关系和图形结构源）的广泛基准测试中，OmniRetrieval超越了单源基线，证明了它可以作为异构源的通用接口，同时保留每个源的结构差异，使其有价值。

Original abstract: Real-world information needs require access to structurally diverse knowledge sources, from unstructured text and relational tables to knowledge graphs and property graphs. Existing retrievers, however, operate over one source at a time under a fixed query language, leaving the broader landscape of available knowledge fragmented behind incompatible interfaces. A natural attempt at unification would collapse these sources into a shared space, but this erases the structural affordances (such as schemas, ontologies, compositional operators) that give each source its expressive power. Effective retrieval over diverse knowledge, therefore, requires not homogenization but an overarching layer that meets each source on its own terms. To achieve this, we present OmniRetrieval, a framework that takes any natural-language query, identifies appropriate knowledge sources, and dispatches source-native queries to their native execution engines. Across an extensive benchmark spanning 13 datasets and 309 distinct knowledge bases over text, relational, and graph-structured sources, OmniRetrieval exceeds single-source baselines, demonstrating that it can serve as a general-purpose interface to the heterogeneous sources while preserving the structural distinctions that make each source valuable.

</details>


### [121] [DynSess: Dynamic Session-Level Evaluation and Optimization Framework for Role-Playing Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29256v1)
*Rongsheng Zhang,Jiji Tang,Junnan Ren,Zuyi Bao,Weijie Chen,Ruofan Hu,Zhou Zhao,Tangjie Lv,Yan Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 角色扮演agent会话级评估优化框架，agent评测方法可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出会话级框架DynSess用于角色扮演代理，通过会话级评估和训练方法显著提升长期角色一致性和交互质量，且参数效率高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有角色扮演评估和优化方法主要基于逐轮级别，无法有效捕捉长期会话质量，导致代理在多轮对话中难以维持角色身份和交互一致性。

Method: 提出DynSess框架，包含DynSess-Eval（基于评分标准评估完整会话）和DynSess-Character（利用会话级奖励通过多轮前瞻搜索构建训练轨迹，并采用DSPO和GSRPO两种策略变体进行训练）。

Result: DynSess-Eval与人类判断对齐显著优于先前评估器；DynSess-Character在参数更少的情况下匹配最强角色模型，且保持强角色一致性和交互能力。

Conclusion: 会话级框架能有效提升角色扮演代理的长期性能，且参数效率高；数据集和代码将开源以推动研究。

中文摘要：与大型语言模型的角色扮演本质上是一个会话级任务，要求代理在扩展的多轮对话中维持角色身份和交互质量。然而，现有的评估和优化方法大多停留在逐轮级别，无法捕捉长期质量。我们提出了DynSess，一个统一的会话级角色扮演代理框架。DynSess-Eval通过针对长期行为的评分标准对完整对话会话进行评分。利用其会话级奖励，我们通过多轮前瞻搜索构建高质量训练轨迹，并训练DynSess-Character，包含两个互补变体：DSPO（离策略）和GSRPO（在策略）。实验表明，DynSess-Eval与人类判断的对齐程度显著优于先前的评估器，并且盲人评估进一步显示，尽管使用更少的参数，DynSess-Character仍能匹配最强的角色模型，同时保持强大的角色一致性和交互能力。我们的数据集和代码将发布以促进未来研究。

Original abstract: Role-playing with large language models is fundamentally a session-level task, requiring agents to sustain character identity and interaction quality across extended multi-turn conversations. Yet existing evaluation and optimization methods remain largely turn-level, failing to capture long-horizon quality. We propose DynSess, a unified session-level framework for role-playing agents. DynSess-Eval scores complete dialogue sessions via rubrics targeting long-horizon behaviors. Leveraging its session-level rewards, we construct high-quality training trajectories through multi-turn lookahead search and train DynSess-Character with two complementary variants: DSPO (off-policy) and GSRPO (on-policy). Experiments show that DynSess-Eval aligns with human judgments substantially better than prior evaluators, and blind human evaluation further shows that DynSess-Character matches the strongest character model despite using substantially fewer parameters, while maintaining strong role consistency and interactive ability. Our dataset and code will be released to facilitate future research.

### [122] [Compute Allocation in Evolutionary Search: From Depth-Breadth to Multi-Armed Bandits](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29268v2)
*Sixue Xing,Haoyu He,Kerui Wu,Zhuo Yang,Haozheng Luo,Tianfan Fu,Aarthy Nagarajan*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM进化搜索中计算分配研究，多臂老虎机分配策略对agent资源分配有启发

TL;DR: BaSE是一种基于多臂老虎机的LLM调用分配策略，通过跨并行轨迹分配固定预算，在不改变模型或提示的情况下，平均适应度提高12.3%，尤其在高方差任务中提升可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Evolve系统仅报告单次最佳结果，忽略运行间分布，且缺乏对固定LLM调用预算如何分配以可靠达到报告性能的指导。

Method: 通过深度-广度网格扫描识别出适应度-计算包络线和双线性深度-广度拟合规律，据此提出BaSE：一个多臂老虎机算法，在并行进化轨迹间自适应分配LLM调用。

Result: 在8个（模型、任务）组合上，BaSE相比最强基线平均适应度提升12.3%，高方差设置下增益最大，仅通过分配策略即可提升可靠性。

Conclusion: BaSE有效利用分配规律，在不改变核心组件下提升进化搜索的均值性能和可靠性，验证了调用分配策略的重要性。

中文摘要：LLM引导的进化搜索（Evolve系统）在数学和组合任务上达到了最先进的结果，但大多数现有系统仅报告多次运行中的最佳结果，而未记录运行间的分布。我们询问如何分配固定的LLM调用预算，以及单次运行可靠地达到报告数字的可能性。通过五个模型和三个任务上的深度-广度网格扫描，我们确定了两个经验规律：一个适应度-计算包络线，其中能力排序主要根据有效FLOPs折叠；以及一个具有任务特定交互的双线性深度-广度拟合；两者都受模型-任务能力门控。受这些规律启发，我们提出了BaSE（基于Bandit的自进化），一种多臂老虎机，跨并行轨迹分配LLM调用。在不改变模型、提示或评估器的情况下，BaSE在8个（模型、任务）组合上比最强的小岛协议基线平均适应度提高了12.3%，最大的改进出现在高方差设置中：仅通过分配就获得了可靠性增益。

Original abstract: LLM-guided evolutionary search (Evolve systems) has reached state-of-the-art results on mathematical and combinatorial tasks, yet most existing systems report only the best of many runs and leave the run-to-run distribution undocumented. We ask how a fixed budget of LLM calls should be allocated, and how reliably a single run reaches the reported numbers. Sweeping the depth-breadth grid over five models and three tasks, we identify two empirical regularities: a fitness-compute envelope along which capability ordering largely collapses on effective FLOPs, and a bilinear depth-breadth fit with task-specific interaction; both are gated by model-task capability. Motivated by these regularities, we propose BaSE (Bandit-based Self-Evolving), a multi-armed bandit that allocates LLM calls across parallel trajectories. Without changing the model, prompt, or evaluator, BaSE improves mean fitness by 12.3% over the strongest island-protocol baseline across 8 (model, task) cells, with the largest gains on high-variance settings: a reliability gain from allocation alone.

### [123] [GrepSeek: Training Search Agents for Direct Corpus Interaction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29307v1)
*Alireza Salemi,Chang Zeng,Atharva Nijasure,Jui-Hui Chung,Razieh Rahimi,Fernando Diaz,Hamed Zamani*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 训练搜索agent直接与语料库交互，使用shell命令和GRPO训练，直接相关coding agent

TL;DR: GrepSeek提出一种直接通过shell命令与语料库交互的搜索代理，使用两阶段训练（冷启动+GRPO）和分片并行执行引擎，在开放域问答上取得最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM搜索代理通常依赖基于预计算索引的检索器，忽略了直接与语料库交互的可能性，而直接交互（如shell命令）可能提供更灵活和精确的证据获取方式。

Method: 提出GrepSeek，采用直接语料库交互（DCI）方法，训练紧凑搜索代理通过shell命令查找证据。两阶段训练：先由Tutor和Planner生成冷启动数据，再用GRPO优化策略。使用分片并行执行引擎加速shell命令执行。

Result: 在七个开放域问答基准上，GrepSeek在token级F1和精确匹配上达到最优，且分片并行执行加速高达7.6倍。

Conclusion: DCI是一种实用且有竞争力的方法，可补充现有检索范式，但在处理表面形式变化大的查询时存在局限性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）搜索代理通过多轮推理和信息检索，在知识密集型语言任务中展现出强大潜力。现有系统大多使用检索器，该检索器接受关键词或自然语言查询，并通过预先计算的文档表示索引返回排序后的文档列表。在这项工作中，我们探索了一种互补视角：搜索代理将语料库本身视为搜索环境，并通过执行可执行的shell命令来查找证据。我们引入了GrepSeek，一种优化的直接语料库交互（DCI）搜索代理，它训练一个紧凑的搜索代理从大型文本语料库中查找、过滤和组合证据。为了解决在大语料库上直接使用强化学习训练行为的不稳定性，我们提出了一个两阶段训练流程。首先，我们使用一个感知答案的导师和盲答案的计划器构建一个冷启动数据集，生成经过验证的、因果基础牢固的搜索轨迹。其次，我们使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）优化初始化策略，使代理能够通过与语料库的直接交互改进其任务导向的搜索行为。为了使DCI在实践中可扩展，我们进一步使用语义保持的分片并行执行引擎，将基于shell的检索加速高达7.6倍，同时保持与shell命令顺序执行的字节精确等价。在七个开放域问答基准上的实验表明，GrepSeek在整体token级别的F1和精确匹配上达到最强。我们的分析还揭示了纯词汇交互在表面形式变化较大的查询上的局限性，表明DCI作为一种实用且有竞争力的搜索代理方法，可以在现实世界中补充现有的检索范式。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) search agents have shown strong promise for knowledge-intensive language tasks through multiple rounds of reasoning and information retrieval. Most existing systems access information using a retriever that takes a keyword or natural language query and returns a ranked list of documents using an index of pre-computed document representations. In this work, we explore a complementary perspective in which the search agent treats the corpus itself as the search environment and finds evidence by issuing executable shell commands. We introduce GrepSeek, an optimized direct corpus interaction (DCI) search agent that trains a compact search agent to find, filter, and compose evidence from large text corpora. To address the instability of learning behavior directly with reinforcement learning on large corpora, we propose a two-stage training pipeline. First, we construct a cold-start dataset using an answer-aware Tutor and answer-blind Planner to generate verified, causally grounded search trajectories. Second, we refine the initialized policy with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), allowing the agent to improve its task-oriented search behavior through direct interaction with the corpus. To make DCI practical at scale, we further use a semantics-preserving sharded-parallel execution engine that accelerates shell-based retrieval by up to $7.6\times$ while preserving byte-exact equivalence with sequential execution of the shell command. Experiments across seven open-domain question answering benchmarks show that GrepSeek achieves the strongest overall token-level $F_1$ and Exact Match. Our analysis also highlights the limitations of purely lexical interaction on queries with substantial surface-form variation, suggesting DCI as a practical and competitive method for search agents that can complement existing retrieval paradigms in the real world.

</details>


### [124] [SkillBrew: Multi-Objective Curation of Skill Banks for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29440v1)
*Wentao Hu,Zhendong Chu,Yiming Zhang,Junda Wu,Ming Jin,Xiangyu Zhao,Yilei Shao,Yanfeng Wang,Qingsong Wen*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出多目标技能库策划方法，直接关系agent记忆与工具使用，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: 提出SkillBrew框架，将技能库策划分形式化为多目标优化问题，通过帕累托感知优化和双层提议-验证循环实现，实验表明优于仅追加方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能库以仅追加方式扩展，导致冗余、过时和有害技能累积，效率低且策划不良。

Method: SkillBrew框架，将技能库策划作为带约束多目标问题（有用性、多样性、覆盖度），采用帕累托感知优化和双层提议-验证循环求解。

Result: 在两个公开基准上评估，显示方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 将技能库视为有原则策划的对象是构建自我改进LLM智能体的重要一步。

中文摘要：检索增强的LLM智能体越来越依赖精心策划的技能库：可复用的文本原则集合，指导复杂任务决策。现有方法通常以仅追加方式扩展这些库，不断添加新技能而不移除冗余、过时或有害的技能，导致低效和策划不良的仓库。本文中，我们将技能库策划形式化为一个带约束的多目标问题：一个理想的库必须对智能体有用、内容多样、并且对查询分布有良好覆盖。为此，我们引入SkillBrew，一个多目标策划框架，将技能库策划形式化为在效用约束下的帕累托感知优化，并通过双层提议-验证循环求解。我们在两个公开基准上评估。我们的发现表明，将技能库视为有原则策划的对象，而不是不断增长的仅追加日志，是构建自我改进LLM智能体的重要一步。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented LLM agents increasingly rely on curated skill banks: collections of reusable textual principles that guide decision making on complex tasks. Existing approaches typically expand these banks in an append-only fashion, continuously adding new skills without removing redundant, outdated, or harmful ones, resulting in inefficient and poorly curated repositories. In this paper, we formulate the skill bank curation as a constrained multi-objective problem: a desirable bank must be useful for the agent, diverse in its content, and provide good coverage of the query distribution. To this end, we introduce SkillBrew, a multi-objective curation framework that formalizes skill bank curation as Pareto-aware optimization under a utility constraint, and solves it via a bi-level propose-then-verify loop. We evaluate our approach on two public benchmarks. Our findings suggest that treating skill banks as objects of principled curation, rather than ever-growing append-only logs, is an important step toward building self-improving LLM agents.

*Hongran An,Zonglin Yang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) show remarkable potential in scientific hypothesis discovery. However, existing approaches face two critical limitations: they treat divergent exploratory search and convergent fine-grained refinement as isolated tasks, and they operate autonomously with little to no human guidance. We present MOOSE-Copilot, the first unified framework to bridge this abstraction gap through a formalized human-AI interaction (HAII) protocol. Our system empowers scientists to steer the generative process via three explicit signals: initial blueprints, inter-stage routing, and intra-stage feedback. Using an oracle-simulated evaluation in which an LLM provides idealized expert signals, we show that injecting these structured signals significantly outperforms purely autonomous baselines, characterizing the gains achievable under high-quality guidance. Furthermore, we build a web-based interface that turns the framework into a no-code workflow: researchers pose a question, watch the hypothesis search unfold as an interactive tree, and steer it by selecting hypotheses, routing between stages, and injecting feedback-no command-line agents required. ### [126] [PhoneWorld: Scaling Phone-Use Agent Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29486v1)
*Zhengyang Tang,Yuxuan Liu,Xin Lai,Junyi Li,Pengyuan Lyu,Jason,Yiduo Guo,Zhengyao Fang,Yang Ding,Yi Zhang,Weinong Wang,Huawen Shen,Xingran Zhou,Liang Wu,Fei Tang,Sunqi Fan,Shangpin Peng,Zheng Ruan,Anran Zhang,Benyou Wang,Rui Yan,Ji-Rong Wen,Chengquan Zhang,Han Hu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 手机使用agent环境缩放方法，对agent环境构建与迁移训练有直接价值

TL;DR: PhoneWorld是一个可复用的流水线，能将真实GUI轨迹转化为可控手机使用环境、任务、验证器和训练数据。在固定预算下，用PhoneWorld监督替换部分AndroidWorld语料，同时提升四个基准，最高提升52.5点。扩展监督量和应用覆盖范围均能进一步改善性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有手机使用智能体基准无法大规模构建可控、可复现环境，阻碍了智能体研究。PhoneWorld旨在提供可扩展的解决方案。

Method: 利用真实轨迹恢复屏幕关系、交互和环境状态变化，构建模拟Android应用及衍生任务、验证器和训练数据。

Result: 替换10K步辅助语料后，四个基准分别提升17.7、6.0、14.7、52.5点。增加监督量或扩大应用覆盖均能提升性能。

Conclusion: PhoneWorld实现了从手工构建单个基准到规模化供应手机使用环境的转变，可扩展性强。

中文摘要：手机使用智能体的一个核心瓶颈是，能够覆盖真实移动行为的可控、可复现环境难以大规模构建。现有的移动智能体基准在评估方面取得了重要进展，但它们本身并不能提供一种可扩展的方式来构建大量新的手机使用环境。我们提出PhoneWorld，这是一个可复用的流水线，能够将真实的GUI轨迹和截图转化为可控的手机使用环境、可执行任务、自动验证器以及训练回滚。PhoneWorld不是一次手工构建一个移动基准，而是利用真实轨迹来恢复哪些屏幕是重要的、屏幕之间如何连接、哪些交互必须改变环境状态，以及哪些用户目标可以进行自动验证。从这些信号中，它构建了由只读应用内容和可变状态支持的可运行的模拟Android应用，然后从相同的环境中衍生出可执行任务、基于规则的验证器以及训练回滚。在当前实例中，PhoneWorld涵盖了16个领域的34个应用，涉及搜索、浏览、购物、预订、媒体和社交互动等常见消费者移动行为。在固定训练预算下，将基于AndroidWorld的基线中的10K步辅助AndroidWorld语料替换为广泛的PhoneWorld监督，可以同时提升所有四个评估基准：HYMobileBench提升17.7点，AndroidControl提升6.0点，AndroidWorld提升14.7点，PhoneWorld提升52.5点。然后我们研究了另外两个扩展问题：增加PhoneWorld监督量会大幅提升PhoneWorld性能；在固定PhoneWorld预算下，扩大应用覆盖范围会带来更大的收益。总体而言，PhoneWorld将焦点从一次构建一个移动基准转向了扩展手机使用环境本身的供应。

Original abstract: A central bottleneck for phone-use agents is that controllable, reproducible environments covering real mobile behavior are hard to build at scale. Existing mobile-agent benchmarks have made important progress on evaluation, but they do not by themselves provide a scalable way to construct many new phone-use environments. We present PhoneWorld, a reusable pipeline that converts real GUI trajectories and screenshots into controllable phone-use environments, executable tasks, automatic verifiers, and training rollouts. Rather than hand-building one mobile benchmark at a time, PhoneWorld uses real trajectories to recover which screens matter, how screens connect, which interactions must change environment state, and which user goals admit automatic verification. From these signals, it builds runnable mock Android apps backed by read-only app content and mutable state, then derives executable tasks, rule-based verifiers, and training rollouts from the same environments. In its current instantiation, PhoneWorld covers 34 apps across 16 domains, spanning common consumer mobile behaviors such as search, browsing, shopping, booking, media, and social interaction. Under a fixed training budget, replacing 10K steps from an auxiliary AndroidWorld corpus in an AndroidWorld-based baseline with broad PhoneWorld supervision improves all four evaluation benchmarks at once, raising HYMobileBench by 17.7 points, AndroidControl by 6.0 points, AndroidWorld by 14.7 points, and PhoneWorld by 52.5 points. We then study two additional scaling questions: increasing the amount of PhoneWorld supervision strongly improves PhoneWorld performance, and under a fixed PhoneWorld budget, expanding app coverage yields even larger gains. Overall, PhoneWorld shifts the focus from building one mobile benchmark at a time to scaling the supply of phone-use environments themselves.
